## Psalms 1:1 (id: 1019001001)

1A joyful person is someone who does not do what evil people tell him to do, who does not imitate sinful people’s behavior, and who does not become like people who enjoy mocking.


## Psalms 1:2 (id: 1019001002)

2Instead, he delights in what Yahweh teaches, he thoughtfully reads it aloud every day and every night.


## Psalms 1:3 (id: 1019001003)

3Like having plenty of water causes a well\-cultivated tree to produce fruit at the right time, and keeps it from dying, so {his faithfulness to Yahweh} causes everything this person does to prosper.


## Psalms 1:4 (id: 1019001004)

4That is not what wicked people are like! Instead, like chaff that the wind blows away,


## Psalms 1:5 (id: 1019001005)

5just so, wicked people will not be able to endure {when Yahweh} judges {the world}. Neither will sinful people {be present when Yahweh} gathers all the righteous people together.


## Psalms 1:6 (id: 1019001006)

6{All of this is} because Yahweh cares for righteous people, but wicked people keep sinning until {Yahweh} destroys them {forever}.


## Psalms 2:1 (id: 1019002001)

1Foreign kingdoms are scheming, and people groups are planning, but it is useless.


## Psalms 2:2 (id: 1019002002)

2Earthly kings prepare to revolt, the rulers plot together to fight against Yahweh and against his chosen king.


## Psalms 2:3 (id: 1019002003)

3{They shout,} “We should break free from the shackles {that they control us with}. We should throw aside the ropes {that they rule over us with}!”


## Psalms 2:4 (id: 1019002004)

4But the heavenly ruler sneers at them; the Lord ridicules those rulers.


## Psalms 2:5 (id: 1019002005)

5Then he speaks to them angrily. He terrifies them by {showing them how} furious he is.


## Psalms 2:6 (id: 1019002006)

6{Yahweh says,} “It is I who has made my king rule in Zion, {which is} my sacred hill.”


## Psalms 2:7 (id: 1019002007)

7{Yahweh’s king says,} “I will proclaim what Yahweh has decreed. Yahweh said to me, ‘You are my son; today I have become your father.


## Psalms 2:8 (id: 1019002008)

8Request {this from} me: {ask to} inherit the nations, {ask to} own the {whole} earth {even the} farthest parts. I will give them to you.


## Psalms 2:9 (id: 1019002009)

9You will strike them with an iron rod and they will shatter into small pieces as if they were a clay pot.”


## Psalms 2:10 (id: 1019002010)

10So then, you kings should act wisely! All rulers on the earth should allow Yahweh and his king to correct them!


## Psalms 2:11 (id: 1019002011)

11Worship Yahweh respectfully. Be joyful and afraid {while you are worshipping him}!


## Psalms 2:12 (id: 1019002012)

12Swear to be truly loyal to his son otherwise, he may become angry and suddenly kill you because he can become angry quickly. But all those who ask him to protect them are fortunate.


## Psalms 3:1 (id: 1019003001)

1A psalm written by David when he was fleeing from his son Absalom. Yahweh, I have so many enemies! Many people are deciding to oppose me.


## Psalms 3:2 (id: 1019003002)

2Many people are saying about me, “God will not rescue him.” Selah


## Psalms 3:3 (id: 1019003003)

3But Yahweh, you are like a shield that protects me. You greatly honor me, and you encourage me.


## Psalms 3:4 (id: 1019003004)

4Whenever I cry loudly to Yahweh {for help}, he {comes} from {Zion,} his sacred hill to help me. Selah


## Psalms 3:5 (id: 1019003005)

5I {can} lie down and sleep, {knowing that} I {will} wake up because Yahweh guards me {all night}.


## Psalms 3:6 (id: 1019003006)

6There may be thousands {of enemy soldiers} who surround me, but I am not afraid.


## Psalms 3:7 (id: 1019003007)

7Yahweh, get up! My God, rescue me! You can {insultingly} slap my enemies on their cheeks, and destroy those wicked people’s {power like breaking animals’} teeth,


## Psalms 3:8 (id: 1019003008)

8Yahweh rescues! Bless your people! Selah


## Psalms 4:1 (id: 1019004001)

1Righteous God, respond to me when I pray to you. You who have {always} rescued me when I was distressed, act mercifully toward me and pay attention to what I pray.


## Psalms 4:2 (id: 1019004002)

2How long will you mortal people dishonor me instead of honoring me? How long will you love what is useless, and chase lies? Selah


## Psalms 4:3 (id: 1019004003)

3You all should know that Yahweh treats people who are faithful to him as special to him. Yahweh will pay attention when I pray to him.


## Psalms 4:4 (id: 1019004004)

4You should be afraid of Yahweh, and {because of that} stop sinning! While you lie on your bed, examine what you are thinking and stop accusing {me}. Selah


## Psalms 4:5 (id: 1019004005)

5Instead, offer to Yahweh the proper sacrifices and continually trust him.


## Psalms 4:6 (id: 1019004006)

6Many people are wishing for something good to happen. Yahweh, please do good things for us!


## Psalms 4:7 (id: 1019004007)

7You have made me very joyful, even more than {these complainers are} when they have plenty of food and drink.


## Psalms 4:8 (id: 1019004008)

8I can lie down at night and sleep without worrying because {I know that} it is only you, Yahweh, who keeps me safe.


## Psalms 5:1 (id: 1019005001)

1Yahweh, listen to what I say! Comprehend my distressed sigh.


## Psalms 5:2 (id: 1019005002)

2{Since} you are my king and my God, hear and respond when I plead aloud for rescuing, because I am praying to you {only}.


## Psalms 5:3 (id: 1019005003)

3Yahweh, you will hear me pleading each morning. Every morning I will request that you save me, and I will wait for you to do it.


## Psalms 5:4 (id: 1019005004)

4You are a God who certainly does not approve of wicked people; evil\-doers never stay as your guests.


## Psalms 5:5 (id: 1019005005)

5Boasters are not allowed to come worship you. You hate everyone who does evil things.


## Psalms 5:6 (id: 1019005006)

6You kill liars. Yahweh despises murderers and people who deceive others.


## Psalms 5:7 (id: 1019005007)

7As for me, I will come {worship you} where you live, because you are extremely faithful. I will reverently kneel to worship you at your sacred temple.


## Psalms 5:8 (id: 1019005008)

8Yahweh, my enemies are watching me {to try to catch me doing something wrong}. Please show me how to do what is right, just as you always do what is right. Make it easy for me to live obediently to you.


## Psalms 5:9 (id: 1019005009)

9Please do this because my enemies are untrustworthy; one of their strongest desires is to destroy people. They speak things that are vile like the smell of an open grave. They flatter people {to trap and destroy them}.


## Psalms 5:10 (id: 1019005010)

10O God, declare that they are guilty and punish them. Cause to happen to them the harmful events that they plan to cause to happen to others. Get rid of them because they have sinned often, and rebelled against you.


## Psalms 5:11 (id: 1019005011)

11But enable all the people who ask you to protect them to be glad; enable them to sing gladly always. Please protect them. Enable everyone who loves it when you are famous to praise you.


## Psalms 5:12 (id: 1019005012)

12{I ask this} because Yahweh, you always bless those who act righteously; you protect them as if your good acts are like a shield around them.


## Psalms 6:1 (id: 1019006001)

1Yahweh, do not correct me angrily, do not punish me wrathfully.


## Psalms 6:2 (id: 1019006002)

2Yahweh, act kindly toward me because I have become weak. Yahweh, heal me because my body shakes fearfully.


## Psalms 6:3 (id: 1019006003)

3Yahweh, I am greatly troubled in my inner being. How long must I endure this?


## Psalms 6:4 (id: 1019006004)

4Yahweh, relent from your anger and deliver me! Help me because you always do what you promise!


## Psalms 6:5 (id: 1019006005)

5{Do this} because {I and} no one {else} who is dead can honor you, {I and} no one {else} can praise you {if we are} in the place where the dead are.


## Psalms 6:6 (id: 1019006006)

6I am exhausted because of my pain. I cry all night long, so that my tears soak and seem as if they will wash away my bed and my cushions.


## Psalms 6:7 (id: 1019006007)

7I am very sad and {I cry so much that} I cannot see well. My vision has become weak from {crying because of} all my enemies.


## Psalms 6:8 (id: 1019006008)

8{I advise} all you people who do evil things to get away from me because Yahweh heard me when I was crying,


## Psalms 6:9 (id: 1019006009)

9he heard me when I called out for him to help me, and he will answer my prayer.


## Psalms 6:10 (id: 1019006010)

10{When that happens,} all my enemies will be ashamed and very troubled. They will relent {from attacking me because they will} suddenly {be} ashamed.


## Psalms 7:1 (id: 1019007001)

1A psalm that David sang to Yahweh because of a Benjamite named Cush. Yahweh my God, I have come to you so that you can protect me. Save me from everyone who is chasing me {in order to harm me}. Rescue me!


## Psalms 7:2 (id: 1019007002)

2If you do not do that, they will maul me like a lion {does when it attacks the animals it wants to kill}; they shred me and there is not a rescuer.


## Psalms 7:3 (id: 1019007003)

3My God Yahweh, suppose that I have done these things, that I am really guilty.


## Psalms 7:4 (id: 1019007004)

4Suppose that I have harmed my ally, {maybe} I {was unfaithful to my ally and instead} rescued an enemy for no reason.


## Psalms 7:5 (id: 1019007005)

5Then allow my enemies to chase and capture me. Allow them to stomp me into the ground and leave me lying {dead} in the dirt.


## Psalms 7:6 (id: 1019007006)

6Get up Yahweh! Because you are angry, show that you are greater than what my furious enemies can do! Be alert so you can rescue me by doing what you have said is just!


## Psalms 7:7 (id: 1019007007)

7The people of all nations gather around you, return to ruling over them all!


## Psalms 7:8 (id: 1019007008)

8Yahweh, judge the people of all nations! Decide favorably for me, Yahweh, because I am righteous and honorable {before you the} highest judge.


## Psalms 7:9 (id: 1019007009)

9God, you are righteous and look closely at what people think and want. Please stop evil people from doing wicked things, and make {all of us} who are righteous secure!


## Psalms 7:10 (id: 1019007010)

10God, you protect me as a shield protects soldiers; you rescue all those who are righteous in their inner being.


## Psalms 7:11 (id: 1019007011)

11God judges everyone correctly. God condemns {the wicked} constantly.


## Psalms 7:12 (id: 1019007012)

12Whenever the wicked do not repent, it is as though God sharpens his sword and puts a string on his bow {to get ready to kill them}.


## Psalms 7:13 (id: 1019007013)

13He prepares his deadly weapons to kill {the wicked}, he makes his arrows have flaming tips.


## Psalms 7:14 (id: 1019007014)

14Look at the wicked person who is filled with evil intentions, as though pregnant with them, who plans to trouble people like conceiving a child, and who lies as naturally as giving birth.


## Psalms 7:15 (id: 1019007015)

15If he digs a deep pit to trap others, he will fall into his own trap.


## Psalms 7:16 (id: 1019007016)

16He experiences the bad things that he wants to cause to others, he hurts himself by the violent things that he wants to do to others.


## Psalms 7:17 (id: 1019007017)

17I thank Yahweh because he always acts justly, I sing to praise Yahweh, who is the highest judge, and to make him famous.


## Psalms 8:1 (id: 1019008001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be accompanied by a stringed instrument; Our Lord Yahweh, people all over the world know how impressive you are! You have made the sky show {everyone} how grand you are {every time anyone looks at it}!


## Psalms 8:2 (id: 1019008002)

2When {anyone who is weak cries for help like} nursing little children cry {for help} you {listen and} protect them from your enemies, {the ones that want to hurt your people}. In order to protect them, you destroy enemies who want to harm them in return {for what you have justly done to them}.


## Psalms 8:3 (id: 1019008003)

3I look up at the sky {at night} and see the things that you have made— the moon and the stars that you have set in place.


## Psalms 8:4 (id: 1019008004)

4It is amazing to me that you think about people, that you are concerned about humans!


## Psalms 8:5 (id: 1019008005)

5In fact though, you made humans to be just slightly lower than heavenly beings. You made humans to be glorious and majestic {like you}.


## Psalms 8:6 (id: 1019008006)

6You put humans in charge of everything that you made, you made them rule over all things—


## Psalms 8:7 (id: 1019008007)

7{over} all {the domestic animals like} sheep, goats, and cattle, the wild animals too,


## Psalms 8:8 (id: 1019008008)

8the birds in the sky, the fish in the sea, and everything else that swims in the ocean.


## Psalms 8:9 (id: 1019008009)

9Our Lord Yahweh, people all over the world know how impressive you are!


## Psalms 9:1 (id: 1019009001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, in the ‘Muth Labben’ style; Yahweh, I will praise you with all of my inner being. I will tell others about all the wonderful things that you have done.


## Psalms 9:2 (id: 1019009002)

2You make me extremely happy, so I will sing to celebrate what you, who are much greater than all other gods, have done.


## Psalms 9:3 (id: 1019009003)

3When my foes flee {from your righteous anger}, they trip and fall. You kill them just by being near them.


## Psalms 9:4 (id: 1019009004)

4{You are angry because} you have found my legal case to be righteous {and my enemies’ to be wicked}. You sit on a throne {like a king} judging {everything} rightly.


## Psalms 9:5 (id: 1019009005)

5You reprimanded the people from other nations, and killed the wicked people; you eradicate them so thoroughly no one will ever remember their names.


## Psalms 9:6 (id: 1019009006)

6Nothing remains of our enemies except the ruins of their cities which you permanently destroyed. No one even remembers those enemies anymore.


## Psalms 9:7 (id: 1019009007)

7But Yahweh rules forever. He is prepared to judge from his throne.


## Psalms 9:8 (id: 1019009008)

8He will judge all the people in the world justly; he will be fair when he judges the people of every nation.


## Psalms 9:9 (id: 1019009009)

9Let Yahweh be like a fortress for those whom oppressors oppress; like a strong fort for them when they have trouble.


## Psalms 9:10 (id: 1019009010)

10Those who know your reputation should trust you; because you, Yahweh, never abandon those who come to you {for help}.


## Psalms 9:11 (id: 1019009011)

11Yahweh rules on Mount Zion; praise him by singing to him! Tell people from every nation the marvelous things that he has done.


## Psalms 9:12 (id: 1019009012)

12Do this because Yahweh always remembers to repay any person who murders another person. When someone's enemy has oppressed him, and when that person calls to Yahweh to help him, Yahweh does not forget to avenge him.


## Psalms 9:13 (id: 1019009013)

13Yahweh, act mercifully toward me! You who rescue me when I am almost dead, look at the ways that my enemies have oppressed me.


## Psalms 9:14 (id: 1019009014)

14{I want to live} in order to tell all your people at the entrance to Jerusalem all the reasons to praise you and to rejoice because you rescued me.


## Psalms 9:15 (id: 1019009015)

15{When you rescue me} it is like wicked people of many nations had dug a pit for me to fall into, but have fallen into that same pit, or like they hid a net to catch me, but their feet have been caught in that same net.


## Psalms 9:16 (id: 1019009016)

16So you allow the traps that wicked people make to trap them. Because of that, people can discover that you, Yahweh, are just. 


## Psalms 9:17 (id: 1019009017)

17Wicked people will flee {from you} back to the place where dead people stay. {There are people there} from every nation, people who have forgotten {to worship the true} God.


## Psalms 9:18 (id: 1019009018)

18This all happens because there is a certainly time when God will remember {to take care of} poor people. It is good for oppressed people to expect him to rescue them because he will do it one day.


## Psalms 9:19 (id: 1019009019)

19Yahweh, do something! Do not let {evil} people win! {Bring them} to your court and judge them!


## Psalms 9:20 (id: 1019009020)

20Yahweh, teach them that they must be afraid of you and honor you. Cause {the rulers of} nations to know that they are mortal. 


## Psalms 10:1 (id: 1019010001)

1Yahweh, please do not stay far away from us. Please let us find you when enemies threaten us.


## Psalms 10:2 (id: 1019010002)

2Wicked people proudly chase people until they can oppress them. Yahweh, please make the bad things they plan to do others to happen to them instead.


## Psalms 10:3 (id: 1019010003)

3A wicked person even brags about what he strongly wants to do. He praises people who unjustly take things from other people. He curses Yahweh.


## Psalms 10:4 (id: 1019010004)

4The wicked person is so proud that he does not care {about God}. He plans {to do evil things} as if there was no God.


## Psalms 10:5 (id: 1019010005)

5What he does always prospers. He ignores doing what you say is right. He makes a mocking noise at all his enemies.


## Psalms 10:6 (id: 1019010006)

6He thinks, “Nothing bad can happen to me! As long as I live, nothing will trouble me.”


## Psalms 10:7 (id: 1019010007)

7He constantly curses, lies, and threatens others. He is always talking about harming others and doing wrong.


## Psalms 10:8 (id: 1019010008)

8He hides outside villages to surprise attack people. From his secret spot he kills people who have done nothing wrong. From there he sneakily watches for some unlucky person.


## Psalms 10:9 (id: 1019010009)

9He hides in a secret spot like a lion, {crouching} in the bushes, waiting for people to catch and oppress. He catches people and drags them away in a net to oppress them.


## Psalms 10:10 (id: 1019010010)

10The wicked person makes sure everything is properly prepared so he can oppress his unlucky victim.


## Psalms 10:11 (id: 1019010011)

11He convinces himself, “God is not recording what I do. He is not paying attention; he will never notice.”


## Psalms 10:12 (id: 1019010012)

12Do something Yahweh! Prove that you are powerful God! Pay attention to oppressed people!


## Psalms 10:13 (id: 1019010013)

13Do not let wicked people curse you, God! Do not let him believe that you do not care about his evil deeds!


## Psalms 10:14 (id: 1019010014)

14Surely you see everything! You pay attention to how wicked people hurt and frustrate other people so that you can punish those wicked people. Unlucky people trust that you will protect them. You help orphans.


## Psalms 10:15 (id: 1019010015)

15Cause people who are always doing very evil things to become powerless! When someone tries to oppress other people may he discover he cannot do it.


## Psalms 10:16 (id: 1019010016)

16Yahweh reigns eternally! Foreign people no longer occupy his land.


## Psalms 10:17 (id: 1019010017)

17Yahweh, when oppressed people ask you to help, you listen and encourage them. You pay close attention,


## Psalms 10:18 (id: 1019010018)

18so you can act justly for the orphans and oppressed people. You will stop any mere human from ever terrifying them again.


## Psalms 11:1 (id: 1019011001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; I trust that Yahweh will protect me. So I do not fly off to the mountains like birds do.


## Psalms 11:2 (id: 1019011002)

2It is true that wicked people have hidden in the darkness, that they have pulled back their bowstrings and aimed their arrows to shoot them at people who honor Yahweh.


## Psalms 11:3 (id: 1019011003)

3When wicked people do not suffer for disobeying the laws, what can righteous people do?


## Psalms 11:4 (id: 1019011004)

4But Yahweh is sitting on his throne in his sacred temple in heaven, and he sees everything that people do.


## Psalms 11:5 (id: 1019011005)

5Yahweh examines what righteous people do and what wicked people do, and he hates those who love to injure others.


## Psalms 11:6 (id: 1019011006)

6He will send down from the sky flaming coals and burning sulfur on the wicked; he will send scorching hot winds to punish them.


## Psalms 11:7 (id: 1019011007)

7Yahweh does everything that is right, and he loves those who do what is right; such people will come into his presence.


## Psalms 12:1 (id: 1019012001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; Yahweh, help us! It seems like people who honor you are no more, that those who are loyal to you have all vanished.


## Psalms 12:2 (id: 1019012002)

2Everyone tells lies to other people; they deceive others by flattering them, but they tell lies.


## Psalms 12:3 (id: 1019012003)

3Yahweh, we wish that you would cut off their tongues so that they cannot continue to boast.


## Psalms 12:4 (id: 1019012004)

4They say, “By telling lies we will get what we want; we control what we say, so no one can tell us what we should do!”


## Psalms 12:5 (id: 1019012005)

5But Yahweh replies, “I have seen the violent things that they have done to helpless people; I have heard those people groaning, so I will arise and rescue the people who are wanting me to help them.”


## Psalms 12:6 (id: 1019012006)

6Yahweh, you always do what you have promised to do; what you have promised is as precious and pure as silver that has been heated seven times in a furnace to get rid of all the impure material.


## Psalms 12:7 (id: 1019012007)

7Yahweh, we know that you will protect us who honor you from those wicked people,


## Psalms 12:8 (id: 1019012008)

8those who strut around proudly, while people praise them for doing evil deeds.


## Psalms 13:1 (id: 1019013001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; Yahweh, how long will you continue to forget about me? Will you hide yourself from me forever?


## Psalms 13:2 (id: 1019013002)

2How long must I endure anguish within myself? Must I be miserable every day? How long will my enemies continue to defeat me?


## Psalms 13:3 (id: 1019013003)

3Yahweh my God, look at me and answer me. Restore my strength, or I will die.


## Psalms 13:4 (id: 1019013004)

4Do not allow my enemies to boast and to say, “We have defeated him!” Do not allow them to defeat me, with the result that they will rejoice about it!


## Psalms 13:5 (id: 1019013005)

5But I trust that you will faithfully love me; I will rejoice when you rescue me.


## Psalms 13:6 (id: 1019013006)

6Yahweh, you have done many good things for me, so I will sing to you.


## Psalms 14:1 (id: 1019014001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; Only foolish people say to themselves, “There is no God!” People who say those things only do corrupt deeds; there is not one of them who does what is good.


## Psalms 14:2 (id: 1019014002)

2From heaven Yahweh looks down at everyone; he looks to see if anyone is very wise, wise enough to desire to know him.


## Psalms 14:3 (id: 1019014003)

3Everyone turns away from Yahweh. They are depraved and do disgusting, filthy things. No one does what is good.


## Psalms 14:4 (id: 1019014004)

4Will those evil people never learn what God will do to punish them? They act violently toward Yahweh’s people and want to consume them like one who eats food consumes it, and they never pray to Yahweh.


## Psalms 14:5 (id: 1019014005)

5But some day they will become very terrified because God helps those who act righteously and will punish those who reject him.


## Psalms 14:6 (id: 1019014006)

6Those who do evil may prevent helpless people from doing what they plan to do, but Yahweh protects them.


## Psalms 14:7 (id: 1019014007)

7Out of Zion Yahweh will come and rescue the Israelite people! He will make his people free again and will bring them back to their home. On that day all of us Israelite people will rejoice, and we, who are also called the descendants of Jacob, will be happy.


## Psalms 15:1 (id: 1019015001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, who are allowed to enter your sacred tent? Who are allowed to live on your sacred mountain?


## Psalms 15:2 (id: 1019015002)

2Only those who always do what is right and do not sin may do that, those who always speak the truth.


## Psalms 15:3 (id: 1019015003)

3They do not slander others. They do not do to others things that are wrong, and they do not say bad things about anyone.


## Psalms 15:4 (id: 1019015004)

4People who honor God hate those whom he has rejected, but they respect those who have a fearful respect for Yahweh. They do what they have promised to do even if it causes them trouble to do that.


## Psalms 15:5 (id: 1019015005)

5They lend money to others without charging interest, and they never accept bribes in order to lie about people who have not done anything wrong. Those who do those things will always live in safety.


## Psalms 16:1 (id: 1019016001)

1A psalm written by David; God, protect me because I go to you to keep me safe!


## Psalms 16:2 (id: 1019016002)

2I said to Yahweh, “You are my Lord; all the good things that I have come from you.”


## Psalms 16:3 (id: 1019016003)

3People who try to be holy who live in this land are wonderful; I delight to be with them.


## Psalms 16:4 (id: 1019016004)

4Those who choose to worship other gods will have many things that cause them to be sad. I will not join them when they make sacrifices to their gods; I will not even join them in speaking the names of their gods.


## Psalms 16:5 (id: 1019016005)

5Yahweh, you are the one whom I have chosen, and you give me great blessings. You protect me and control what happens to me.


## Psalms 16:6 (id: 1019016006)

6Yahweh has given me a wonderful place in which to live; I am delighted with all the things that he has given me.


## Psalms 16:7 (id: 1019016007)

7I will praise Yahweh, the one who teaches me; even at night he tells my heart what is right for me to do.


## Psalms 16:8 (id: 1019016008)

8I know that Yahweh is always with me. Nothing will take me from his side.


## Psalms 16:9 (id: 1019016009)

9Therefore I am glad; I am honored to praise him, and I can rest securely


## Psalms 16:10 (id: 1019016010)

10because you, Yahweh, will not allow me to remain in the place where the dead people are, and you will not allow me, someone who has been faithful to the covenant, to stay there.


## Psalms 16:11 (id: 1019016011)

11You will show me the road that leads to where I receive eternal life, and you will make me joyful when I am with you. I will have pleasure forever when I am at your right hand.


## Psalms 17:1 (id: 1019017001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, listen to me while I plead with you to act justly toward me. Hear me while I call out to you to help me. Pay attention to what I say while I pray because I am speaking honestly.


## Psalms 17:2 (id: 1019017002)

2You are the one who is able to declare that I am innocent; please agree to do what is right for me.


## Psalms 17:3 (id: 1019017003)

3If you come to me at night to learn what I think, if you see what I think in my heart, you will know that I have determined to never tell any lies; you will find that I do not think evil things.


## Psalms 17:4 (id: 1019017004)

4I have not acted like those who do not honor you; I have always acted in the power of what you have instructed me; I have not acted like those who do not know your law.


## Psalms 17:5 (id: 1019017005)

5I have always done what you told me to do; I have never failed to do those things.


## Psalms 17:6 (id: 1019017006)

6O God, I am praying to you because you answer me; please listen to what I am saying.


## Psalms 17:7 (id: 1019017007)

7Continue to show me your love as you promised you would do. By your great power you protect all who trust in you; you keep them safe from their enemies.


## Psalms 17:8 (id: 1019017008)

8Protect me as carefully as people protect their own eyes; protect me like birds protect their babies under their wings.


## Psalms 17:9 (id: 1019017009)

9Do not allow wicked people to attack me, those enemies of mine who surround, wanting to kill me.


## Psalms 17:10 (id: 1019017010)

10They are proud of their riches and success, but they have no mercy on anyone.


## Psalms 17:11 (id: 1019017011)

11They have hunted for me and found me. They surround me, watching for an opportunity to throw me to the ground and kill me.


## Psalms 17:12 (id: 1019017012)

12They are like lions that are ready to tear apart the animals that they capture; They are like young lions that are hiding, waiting to jump on their prey.


## Psalms 17:13 (id: 1019017013)

13Yahweh, arise, attack my enemies, and defeat them! With your sword save me from those wicked people!


## Psalms 17:14 (id: 1019017014)

14Yahweh, by your power rescue me from those people who are interested only in things here in this world. But you provide plenty of food for those whom you love dearly; their children also have many things that their grandchildren will inherit.


## Psalms 17:15 (id: 1019017015)

15Yahweh, because I act in the right way, I will be with you one day. When I awake after I die, I will see you face to face, and then I will be happy.


## Psalms 18:1 (id: 1019018001)

1A psalm written by God’s servant David. He sang it after Yahweh had rescued him from Saul and his other enemies. Yahweh, I love you, the one who enables me to be strong.


## Psalms 18:2 (id: 1019018002)

2Yahweh is like a huge rock; when I am on top of it, my enemies cannot reach me. He is like a strong fortress; I run into it to be safe. He protects me like a shield protects a soldier; he is the one whom I trust to keep me safe; he defends me by his great power!


## Psalms 18:3 (id: 1019018003)

3I called out to Yahweh, who deserves for me to praise him, and he rescued me from my enemies.


## Psalms 18:4 (id: 1019018004)

4All around me were dangerous situations in which I might die; it was as though there were huge waves that almost crashed on me and killed me.


## Psalms 18:5 (id: 1019018005)

5It was as though the place where dead people are had ropes that were wrapped around me, or it was as though there was a trap that would seize and kill me.


## Psalms 18:6 (id: 1019018006)

6But when I was very distressed, I called out to Yahweh, and far off in his temple he heard me. He listened to me when I cried out for help.


## Psalms 18:7 (id: 1019018007)

7Then Yahweh became angry, and the earth quaked, and the mountains shook to their very foundations!


## Psalms 18:8 (id: 1019018008)

8He was so angry that it was as though smoke poured out from his nostrils, as though burning coals came out of his mouth!


## Psalms 18:9 (id: 1019018009)

9He opened the sky and came down with a black cloud under his feet.


## Psalms 18:10 (id: 1019018010)

10He flew, riding on the back of an angel traveling fast, which the wind was blowing along.


## Psalms 18:11 (id: 1019018011)

11Darkness was all around him like a blanket; dark clouds, full of water moisture, covered him.


## Psalms 18:12 (id: 1019018012)

12Hailstones and flashes of lightning were around him; hail and burning coals fell down from the sky.


## Psalms 18:13 (id: 1019018013)

13Then Yahweh shouted loudly from the sky, and to his enemies, it sounded like thunder. Yahweh, the Supreme God, rained hailstones on them and caused lightning to flash against them.


## Psalms 18:14 (id: 1019018014)

14He shot his arrows at them and caused them to scatter; his flashes of lightning caused them to become very confused.


## Psalms 18:15 (id: 1019018015)

15The bottom of the ocean became visible, and the water uncovered the foundations of the earth when Yahweh rebuked his enemies with the breath that came in his anger!


## Psalms 18:16 (id: 1019018016)

16It was as though he reached down from heaven and grabbed me and pulled me up out of the deep ocean.


## Psalms 18:17 (id: 1019018017)

17He rescued me from my strong enemies who hated me; they were very strong, and I could not defeat them by myself.


## Psalms 18:18 (id: 1019018018)

18When I was distressed, they attacked me, but Yahweh defended me.


## Psalms 18:19 (id: 1019018019)

19He made me completely safe; he rescued me because he was pleased with me.


## Psalms 18:20 (id: 1019018020)

20Yahweh has rewarded me because I do what is right; he has blessed me because I am innocent.


## Psalms 18:21 (id: 1019018021)

21I have obeyed Yahweh’s laws; I have not abandoned him.


## Psalms 18:22 (id: 1019018022)

22I have followed his decrees; I have not stopped obeying them.


## Psalms 18:23 (id: 1019018023)

23He knows that I have not done what is wrong and that I have kept myself from sinning.


## Psalms 18:24 (id: 1019018024)

24So he rewards me because I do what is right; he knows that I have not committed sins.


## Psalms 18:25 (id: 1019018025)

25Yahweh, you are faithful to those who faithfully do your covenant; you always do what is good to those who do not do evil.


## Psalms 18:26 (id: 1019018026)

26You are kind to those who are honest toward others, but you act wisely toward those who act dishonestly.


## Psalms 18:27 (id: 1019018027)

27You save those who are humble, but you humiliate those who are proud.


## Psalms 18:28 (id: 1019018028)

28You keep me alive, and you will continue to do so.


## Psalms 18:29 (id: 1019018029)

29You enable me to be strong, so that I can attack and defeat a line of enemy soldiers; with your help I can scale the walls that surround my enemies’ cities.


## Psalms 18:30 (id: 1019018030)

30Everything that Yahweh my God does is perfect. We can depend on him to do what he promises. He is like a shield to protect all those who go to him to be safe.


## Psalms 18:31 (id: 1019018031)

31Yahweh is the only one who is God; only he is like a huge rock on top of which we can be safe.


## Psalms 18:32 (id: 1019018032)

32God is the one who enables me to be strong and who keeps me safe on the roads that I walk on.


## Psalms 18:33 (id: 1019018033)

33He enables me to walk swiftly without stumbling as a deer walks in the mountains.


## Psalms 18:34 (id: 1019018034)

34He teaches me how to use a strong bow in order that I can use it to fight in battles.


## Psalms 18:35 (id: 1019018035)

35Yahweh, you protect and save me with your shield; you are strong and have therefore kept me safe. I have become strong because you have helped me.


## Psalms 18:36 (id: 1019018036)

36You have made a safe path for me, with the result that now I do not slip.


## Psalms 18:37 (id: 1019018037)

37I pursued my enemies and caught them; I did not stop until I had defeated them all.


## Psalms 18:38 (id: 1019018038)

38When I strike them, they are not able to get up again; they lie on the ground, defeated.


## Psalms 18:39 (id: 1019018039)

39You have enabled me to be strong in order that I can fight battles and defeat my enemies.


## Psalms 18:40 (id: 1019018040)

40You delivered my enemies to me, for me to strike them on their necks. I have gotten rid of all those who hated me.


## Psalms 18:41 (id: 1019018041)

41They shouted for someone to help them, but no one saved them. They shouted out to Yahweh, but he did not help them.


## Psalms 18:42 (id: 1019018042)

42I crushed them to powder, and they became like the dust that the wind blows away; I threw them out like people throw dirt out into the streets.


## Psalms 18:43 (id: 1019018043)

43You enabled me to defeat those who fought against me and appointed me to be the ruler of many nations; people whom I did not know about previously are now slaves in my kingdom.


## Psalms 18:44 (id: 1019018044)

44When foreigners hear about me, they cringe and they obey me.


## Psalms 18:45 (id: 1019018045)

45They are no longer courageous, and from their holes where they were hiding they come to me trembling.


## Psalms 18:46 (id: 1019018046)

46Yahweh is alive! Praise the one who is like a huge rock on top of which I am safe! Exalt the God who saves me!


## Psalms 18:47 (id: 1019018047)

47He enables me to get revenge on my enemies; he causes me to defeat nations and to rule over them.


## Psalms 18:48 (id: 1019018048)

48it is Yahweh who rescues me from my enemies. He has lifted me up high so that violent men could not reach me and harm me.


## Psalms 18:49 (id: 1019018049)

49So I praise him, and I tell the nations the great things that he has done.


## Psalms 18:50 (id: 1019018050)

50He has enabled me, his king, to powerfully defeat my enemies; he faithfully loves me as he promised in his covenant. He loves me, David, the one he has chosen to be king, and he will faithfully love my descendants forever.


## Psalms 19:1 (id: 1019019001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; When people look at everything that God has placed in the skies, they can see that he is very great; they can see the great things that he has created.


## Psalms 19:2 (id: 1019019002)

2Day after day it is as though the sun proclaims the glory of God, and night after night it is as though the moon and stars say that they know that God made them.


## Psalms 19:3 (id: 1019019003)

3They do not really speak; they do not say any words. There is no sound from them for anyone to hear.


## Psalms 19:4 (id: 1019019004)

4But what they declare about God goes throughout the world, and even people who live in the most distant places on earth can know it. The sun is in the skies where God placed it;


## Psalms 19:5 (id: 1019019005)

5it rises each morning like a bridegroom who is happy as he comes out of his bedroom after his wedding. It is like a strong athlete who is very eager to start running in a race.


## Psalms 19:6 (id: 1019019006)

6The sun rises at one side of the sky and goes across the sky and sets on the other side; nothing can hide from its heat.


## Psalms 19:7 (id: 1019019007)

7The instructions that Yahweh has given us are perfect; they revive us. We can be sure that the things that Yahweh has told us will never change, and by learning them people who have not been previously taught will become wise.


## Psalms 19:8 (id: 1019019008)

8Yahweh’s laws are fair; when we obey them, we become joyful. The commands of Yahweh are clear, and by reading them we start to understand how God wants us to behave.


## Psalms 19:9 (id: 1019019009)

9It is good for people to revere Yahweh; that is something that they will do forever. What Yahweh has decreed is fair, and it is always right.


## Psalms 19:10 (id: 1019019010)

10The things that God has decided are more valuable than gold, even the finest gold. They are sweeter than honey that drips from honeycombs.


## Psalms 19:11 (id: 1019019011)

11Furthermore, by reading them I learn what things are good to do and what things are evil, and they promise a great reward to us who obey them.


## Psalms 19:12 (id: 1019019012)

12But there is no one who can know all his errors; so Yahweh, forgive me for these things which I do that I do not realize are wrong.


## Psalms 19:13 (id: 1019019013)

13Keep me from doing things that I know are wrong; do not let me keep doing the evil things I want to do. If you do that, I will no longer be guilty for committing such sins, and I will not commit the great sin of rebelling terribly against you.


## Psalms 19:14 (id: 1019019014)

14O Yahweh, you are like a huge rock on top of which I can be safe; you are the one who protects me. I hope that the things that I say and what I think will always please you.


## Psalms 20:1 (id: 1019020001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; We desire that Yahweh may help you when you call out to him when you have troubles! We desire that God, whom our ancestor Jacob honored, may keep you safe from your enemies.


## Psalms 20:2 (id: 1019020002)

2We desire that he may reach out from his sacred temple and help you and aid you from where he lives on Mount Zion.


## Psalms 20:3 (id: 1019020003)

3We desire that he may accept all the offerings that you give him to be burned on the altar and all your other offerings.


## Psalms 20:4 (id: 1019020004)

4We desire that he may give to you what you desire in your heart, and that you may be able to accomplish all that you desire to do.


## Psalms 20:5 (id: 1019020005)

5When you defeat your enemies, we will shout joyfully. We will lift up a banner proclaiming that it is God who has helped you. May Yahweh do for you all that you request him to do.


## Psalms 20:6 (id: 1019020006)

6I know now that Yahweh rescues me, the one whom he has chosen to be king. From his holy place in heaven he will answer me, and he will save me by his great power.


## Psalms 20:7 (id: 1019020007)

7Some kings trust that because they have chariots they will be able to defeat their enemies, and some trust that their horses will enable them to defeat their enemies, but we will trust in the power of Yahweh our God.


## Psalms 20:8 (id: 1019020008)

8Some will stumble and fall down, but we will be strong and not be moved.


## Psalms 20:9 (id: 1019020009)

9Yahweh, help the king defeat our enemies! Answer us when we call out to you to help us!


## Psalms 21:1 (id: 1019021001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; Yahweh, the man you made king is glad because you have caused him to be strong. He rejoices because you have enabled him to defeat his enemies.


## Psalms 21:2 (id: 1019021002)

2You have given him everything he most desired, and you have not refused to do what he requested you to do.


## Psalms 21:3 (id: 1019021003)

3You have done so many wonderful things for him. You placed a gold crown on his head.


## Psalms 21:4 (id: 1019021004)

4He asked you to let him live for a long time, and you have enabled him to live for a long time.


## Psalms 21:5 (id: 1019021005)

5His power as king is very great because you have allowed him to win victories over his enemies.


## Psalms 21:6 (id: 1019021006)

6You will bless him forever, and you have caused him to be joyful in your presence.


## Psalms 21:7 (id: 1019021007)

7Yahweh, you are God Almighty, and the king trusts in you. Because you faithfully love him, disastrous things will never happen to him.


## Psalms 21:8 (id: 1019021008)

8You will enable him to kill all his enemies, all those who hate him.


## Psalms 21:9 (id: 1019021009)

9When you appear, you will throw them into a fiery furnace. Because you are angry with them, you will swallow them up; the fire will burn them up.


## Psalms 21:10 (id: 1019021010)

10You will remove their children from this earth; their descendants will all disappear.


## Psalms 21:11 (id: 1019021011)

11They wanted to harm you, but what they plan will never succeed.


## Psalms 21:12 (id: 1019021012)

12You will cause them to run away by shooting arrows at them.


## Psalms 21:13 (id: 1019021013)

13Yahweh, show us that you are very strong! When you do that, we will sing and praise you because you are very powerful.


## Psalms 22:1 (id: 1019022001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be sung to the tune ‘Doe of the Dawn’ My God, my God, why have you abandoned me? Why do you stay so far from me, and why do you not listent to me? Why do you not hear me when I am suffering and groaning?


## Psalms 22:2 (id: 1019022002)

2My God, every day I call to you during the daytime, but you do not answer me. I call to you during the night; I am not silent at all.


## Psalms 22:3 (id: 1019022003)

3But you are holy. You sit on your throne as king, and we the people of Israel praise you.


## Psalms 22:4 (id: 1019022004)

4Our ancestors trusted in you. Because they trusted in you, you rescued them.


## Psalms 22:5 (id: 1019022005)

5When they called out to you for help, you saved them. They trusted in you, and they were not disappointed.


## Psalms 22:6 (id: 1019022006)

6But you have not rescued me! People despise me and consider that I am not a man; they think that I am a worm! Everyone scorns me and despises me.


## Psalms 22:7 (id: 1019022007)

7Everyone who sees me makes fun of me. They sneer at me and insult me by shaking their heads at me as though I were an evil man. They say,


## Psalms 22:8 (id: 1019022008)

8“He trusts in Yahweh, so Yahweh should save him! He says that Yahweh is very pleased with him; if that is so, Yahweh should rescue him!”


## Psalms 22:9 (id: 1019022009)

9You, God, have been with me since I was in my mother’s womb, and you taught me to trust you when I was at my mother’s breasts.


## Psalms 22:10 (id: 1019022010)

10It was as though you had adopted me right when I was born. You have been my God ever since I was born.


## Psalms 22:11 (id: 1019022011)

11So do not stay far from me now because enemies who will cause me much trouble are near me, and there is no one else who can help me.


## Psalms 22:12 (id: 1019022012)

12My enemies surround me like a herd of wild bulls. Fierce people, like those strong bulls that graze on the hills in the region of Bashan, surround me.


## Psalms 22:13 (id: 1019022013)

13They are like roaring lions that are attacking the animals that they want to eat; they rush toward me to kill me; they are like lions that have their mouths open, ready to chew their victims to pieces.


## Psalms 22:14 (id: 1019022014)

14I am completely exhausted, and all my bones are out of their joints. I no longer expect that God will save me; I am completely discouraged.


## Psalms 22:15 (id: 1019022015)

15My strength is all dried up like a broken piece of a clay jar that has dried in the sun. I am so thirsty that my tongue sticks to the roof of my mouth. God, I think that you are about to let my body die and become dust!


## Psalms 22:16 (id: 1019022016)

16My enemies are like wild dogs that surround me. A group of evil men has encircled me, ready to attack me. They have pierced through my hands and my feet.


## Psalms 22:17 (id: 1019022017)

17I am so weak and thin that I can count all my bones. My enemies stare at me and gloat about what has happened to me.


## Psalms 22:18 (id: 1019022018)

18They looked at the clothes that I was wearing and gambled to determine which piece each of them would get.


## Psalms 22:19 (id: 1019022019)

19Yahweh, be concerned for me! You who are my source of strength, come quickly and help me!


## Psalms 22:20 (id: 1019022020)

20Rescue me from those who want to kill me with their swords. Save my life from the power of those who are like wild dogs.


## Psalms 22:21 (id: 1019022021)

21Snatch me away from my enemies who are like lions with jaws open and ready to chew me up! Grab me away from those men who are like wild oxen that attack other animals with their horns!


## Psalms 22:22 (id: 1019022022)

22If you save me from them, I will declare to my fellow Israelites how great you are. I will praise you among the group of your people gathered together to worship you.


## Psalms 22:23 (id: 1019022023)

23You people who have an awesome respect for Yahweh, praise him! All you who are descended from Jacob, honor Yahweh! All you Israelite people, revere him!


## Psalms 22:24 (id: 1019022024)

24He does not despise or ignore those who are suffering; he does not hide his face from them. He has listened to them when they cried out to him for help.


## Psalms 22:25 (id: 1019022025)

25Yahweh, in the great gathering of your people, I will praise you for what you have done. In the presence of those who have an awesome respect for you, I will offer the sacrifices that I promised.


## Psalms 22:26 (id: 1019022026)

26The poor people whom I have invited to the meal will eat as much as they want. All who come to worship Yahweh will praise him. I pray that God will enable you all to live a long and happy life!


## Psalms 22:27 (id: 1019022027)

27I pray that people in all nations, even in the remote areas, will think about Yahweh and turn to him, and that people from all the clans in the world will bow down before him.


## Psalms 22:28 (id: 1019022028)

28For Yahweh is the king! He rules all the nations.


## Psalms 22:29 (id: 1019022029)

29All the rich people on the earth will celebrate and bow before him. Some day they will die, for they cannot avoid it, but they will prostrate themselves on the ground in his presence.


## Psalms 22:30 (id: 1019022030)

30People in the future generations will also serve Yahweh. They will tell their children about what Yahweh has done.


## Psalms 22:31 (id: 1019022031)

31People who are not yet born, who will live in future years, will learn how Yahweh rescued his people. People will tell them, “Yahweh did it!”


## Psalms 23:1 (id: 1019023001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, you care for me like a shepherd cares for his sheep, so I have everything that I need.


## Psalms 23:2 (id: 1019023002)

2You enable me to rest in peace as when a shepherd leads his sheep to places where there is plenty of green grass for them to eat, as when he lets them lie down beside streams where the water is flowing slowly.


## Psalms 23:3 (id: 1019023003)

3You renew my strength. You show me how to live in the right way, in order that I can honor you.


## Psalms 23:4 (id: 1019023004)

4Even when I am walking in very dangerous places where I might die, I will not be afraid of anything because you are with me. You protect me like a shepherd protects his sheep.


## Psalms 23:5 (id: 1019023005)

5You prepare a great feast for me in a place where my enemies can see me. You welcome me as a guest whom you honor. You have given me very many blessings!


## Psalms 23:6 (id: 1019023006)

6I am certain that you will be good to me and act mercifully toward me as long as I live; then, O Yahweh, I will live in your home forever.


## Psalms 24:1 (id: 1019024001)

1A psalm written by David; The earth and everything in it belongs to Yahweh; all the people in the world belong to him, too;


## Psalms 24:2 (id: 1019024002)

2he built the land on the water, above the water that is deep below.


## Psalms 24:3 (id: 1019024003)

3Who will be allowed to go up onto Mount Zion in Jerusalem, in order to stand and worship in Yahweh’s holy temple?


## Psalms 24:4 (id: 1019024004)

4Only those whose actions and thoughts are pure, who have not worshiped idols, and who do not tell lies when they have solemnly promised to tell the truth.


## Psalms 24:5 (id: 1019024005)

5Yahweh will bless them. When God judges them, he will rescue them and say that they have done nothing wrong.


## Psalms 24:6 (id: 1019024006)

6They are the people who come to God, they are the ones who desire to worship God, and serve the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 24:7 (id: 1019024007)

7Open up the temple gates in order that our glorious king may enter!


## Psalms 24:8 (id: 1019024008)

8Do you know who the glorious king is? It is Yahweh, the one who is very strong; It is Yahweh, who conquers all his enemies in battles!


## Psalms 24:9 (id: 1019024009)

9Open up the temple gates in order that our glorious king may enter!


## Psalms 24:10 (id: 1019024010)

10Do you know who the glorious king is? It is Yahweh, commander of the angel armies; he is our glorious king!


## Psalms 25:1 (id: 1019025001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, I give myself to you.


## Psalms 25:2 (id: 1019025002)

2My God, I trust in you. Do not allow my enemies to defeat me and shame me. Do not allow my enemies to defeat me and rejoice over me.


## Psalms 25:3 (id: 1019025003)

3Do not allow any of those who trust in you to be ashamed. Cause those who act treacherously toward others to be disgraced.


## Psalms 25:4 (id: 1019025004)

4Yahweh, show me the way that I should conduct my life, teach me how to act in the manner that you want me to act.


## Psalms 25:5 (id: 1019025005)

5Teach me to conduct my life by obeying your truth because you are my God, the one who saves me. All during the day I trust in you.


## Psalms 25:6 (id: 1019025006)

6Yahweh, do not forget how you have acted mercifully to me and have faithfully loved me because of your covenant with me; that is the way that you have acted toward me from long ago.


## Psalms 25:7 (id: 1019025007)

7Forgive me for all the sinful things I did and the ways that I rebelled against you when I was young; I request this because you faithfully love your people and do good things for them, as you promised in your covenant. Yahweh, do not forget me!


## Psalms 25:8 (id: 1019025008)

8Yahweh is good and fair, so he shows sinners how they should conduct their lives.


## Psalms 25:9 (id: 1019025009)

9He shows humble people what is right for them to do and teaches them what he wants them to do.


## Psalms 25:10 (id: 1019025010)

10He always faithfully loves us and does what he has promised for those who obey his covenant and who do what he requires.


## Psalms 25:11 (id: 1019025011)

11Yahweh, forgive me for all my sins, which are many, in order that I may honor you.


## Psalms 25:12 (id: 1019025012)

12To all those who have an awesome respect for you, you show them the right way to conduct their lives.


## Psalms 25:13 (id: 1019025013)

13They will always be prosperous, and their descendants will continue to live in this land.


## Psalms 25:14 (id: 1019025014)

14Yahweh is a friend of those who have an awesome respect for him, and he teaches them the covenant that he made with them.


## Psalms 25:15 (id: 1019025015)

15I always request Yahweh to help me, and he rescues me from danger.


## Psalms 25:16 (id: 1019025016)

16Yahweh, pay attention to me and be merciful to me because I am alone, and I am greatly distressed because I am suffering.


## Psalms 25:17 (id: 1019025017)

17I have many troubles that make me afraid; rescue me from them.


## Psalms 25:18 (id: 1019025018)

18Note that I am distressed and troubled, and forgive me for all my sins.


## Psalms 25:19 (id: 1019025019)

19Note that I have many enemies; you see that they hate me very much.


## Psalms 25:20 (id: 1019025020)

20Protect me and rescue me from them; do not allow them to defeat me with the result that I would be ashamed; I have gone to you to get refuge.


## Psalms 25:21 (id: 1019025021)

21Protect me because I do what is good and honest and because I trust in you.


## Psalms 25:22 (id: 1019025022)

22God, rescue us Israelite people from all of our troubles!


## Psalms 26:1 (id: 1019026001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, show that I am innocent. I always do what is right; I have trusted in you and never doubted that you would help me.


## Psalms 26:2 (id: 1019026002)

2Yahweh, examine what I have done and test me; thoroughly evaluate what I think in my inner being.


## Psalms 26:3 (id: 1019026003)

3I never forget that you are true to your covenant and faithfully love me; I conduct my life according to your faithfulness.


## Psalms 26:4 (id: 1019026004)

4I do not spend my time with liars, and I stay away from hypocrites.


## Psalms 26:5 (id: 1019026005)

5I do not like to be with evil people, and I avoid wicked people.


## Psalms 26:6 (id: 1019026006)

6Yahweh, I wash my hands to show that I am innocent. As I join with others marching around your altar,


## Psalms 26:7 (id: 1019026007)

7we sing songs to thank you, and we tell others the wonderful things that you have done.


## Psalms 26:8 (id: 1019026008)

8Yahweh, I love to be in the house where you live, in the place where your glory appears.


## Psalms 26:9 (id: 1019026009)

9Do not get rid of me like you get rid of sinners; do not cause me to die like you cause those who murder people to die,


## Psalms 26:10 (id: 1019026010)

10people who are ready to do wicked things and those who are always taking bribes.


## Psalms 26:11 (id: 1019026011)

11But as for me, I always try to do what is right. So act kindly toward me and rescue me.


## Psalms 26:12 (id: 1019026012)

12I stand in places where I am safe, and when all your people gather together, I praise you.


## Psalms 27:1 (id: 1019027001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh is the one who gives me life and the one who saves me, so I do not need to be afraid of anyone. Yahweh is the one to whom I go for refuge, so I will never be afraid.


## Psalms 27:2 (id: 1019027002)

2When those who do evil come near me to destroy me, they stumble and fall down.


## Psalms 27:3 (id: 1019027003)

3Even if an army surrounds me, I will not be afraid. Even if they attack me, I will trust in God.


## Psalms 27:4 (id: 1019027004)

4There is one thing that I have requested from Yahweh; this is the one thing that I desire: that I may worship in Yahweh’s house every day during my life, that I may see how wonderful Yahweh is, and that I may ask him what he wants me to do.


## Psalms 27:5 (id: 1019027005)

5He will protect me when I have troubles; he will keep me safe in his sacred tent. He will set me safely on a high rock.


## Psalms 27:6 (id: 1019027006)

6Then I will triumph over my enemies. I will shout joyfully as I offer sacrifices in his sacred tent, and I will praise Yahweh as I sing.


## Psalms 27:7 (id: 1019027007)

7Yahweh, listen to me while I call to you. Act kindly toward me and answer my prayer.


## Psalms 27:8 (id: 1019027008)

8Within my inner being I desire to worship you, so, Yahweh, I will come to your temple to pray to you.


## Psalms 27:9 (id: 1019027009)

9I am your servant; do not be angry with me, or turn away from me. You have always helped me. You are the one who has saved me, so do not abandon me now.


## Psalms 27:10 (id: 1019027010)

10Even if my father and mother desert me, Yahweh always takes care of me.


## Psalms 27:11 (id: 1019027011)

11Yahweh, teach me to do what you want me to do, and lead me on a safe path because I have many enemies.


## Psalms 27:12 (id: 1019027012)

12Do not allow my enemies to do to me what they want; they say many false things about me and threaten to do violent things to me.


## Psalms 27:13 (id: 1019027013)

13I would have died if I had not trusted you to be good to me as long as I live.


## Psalms 27:14 (id: 1019027014)

14So trust in Yahweh! Be strong and courageous, and wait expectantly for him to help you!


## Psalms 28:1 (id: 1019028001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, I call out to you; You are like a huge rock on top of which I am safe. Do not refuse to answer me because if you are silent, I will soon be with those who are in their graves.


## Psalms 28:2 (id: 1019028002)

2Listen to me when I call out for you to help me, when I lift up my hands as I face your very holy place in your sacred tent.


## Psalms 28:3 (id: 1019028003)

3Do not drag me away with wicked people, with those who do wicked deeds, with those who pretend to act peacefully toward others while in their inner beings, they hate them.


## Psalms 28:4 (id: 1019028004)

4Punish those people in the way that they deserve for what they have done; punish them for their evil deeds.


## Psalms 28:5 (id: 1019028005)

5Yahweh, they do not pay attention to the wonderful things that you have done and that you have created; so get rid of them permanently and do not let them appear again!


## Psalms 28:6 (id: 1019028006)

6Praise Yahweh because he has heard me when I called out for him to help me!


## Psalms 28:7 (id: 1019028007)

7Yahweh makes me strong and protects me like a shield; I trust in him, and he helps me. So I was glad in my inner being, and from my inner being I praise him as I sing to him.


## Psalms 28:8 (id: 1019028008)

8Yahweh causes us to be strong and protects us; he saves me, the one he appointed to be king.


## Psalms 28:9 (id: 1019028009)

9Yahweh, save your people; bless those who belong to you. Take care of them like a shepherd takes care of his sheep; take care of them forever.


## Psalms 29:1 (id: 1019029001)

1A psalm written by David; Mighty people, praise Yahweh! Praise him because he is very glorious and powerful.


## Psalms 29:2 (id: 1019029002)

2Praise Yahweh with the glory his names deserves. Bow down and worship Yahweh because he is holy and his holiness shines out from him with wonderful beauty.


## Psalms 29:3 (id: 1019029003)

3Yahweh’s voice is heard above the oceans; the glorious God thunders. He appears over the huge oceans.


## Psalms 29:4 (id: 1019029004)

4His voice is powerful and majestic.


## Psalms 29:5 (id: 1019029005)

5Yahweh’s voice breaks great cedar trees, the cedars that grow in Lebanon.


## Psalms 29:6 (id: 1019029006)

6He causes earthquakes to shake the region of Lebanon as a young cow jumps; he causes Sirion (also called Mount Hermon) to shake as a young bull jumps.


## Psalms 29:7 (id: 1019029007)

7Yahweh’s voice tells the lightning to flash.


## Psalms 29:8 (id: 1019029008)

8His voice causes the desert to shake; he shakes the wilderness of Kadesh.


## Psalms 29:9 (id: 1019029009)

9Yahweh’s voice makes the large trees shake, and strips the leaves from the trees while the people in the temple shout, “Praise God!”


## Psalms 29:10 (id: 1019029010)

10Yahweh rules over the flood that covered the earth; he is our king who will rule forever.


## Psalms 29:11 (id: 1019029011)

11Yahweh enables his people to be strong, and he blesses them by causing things to go well for them.


## Psalms 30:1 (id: 1019030001)

1A psalm written by David for the dedication of the temple; Yahweh, I praise you because you rescued me. You did not allow me to die or my enemies to gloat over me.


## Psalms 30:2 (id: 1019030002)

2Yahweh, my God, I called out for you to help me when I was wounded, and you healed me.


## Psalms 30:3 (id: 1019030003)

3You saved me from death. I was nearly dead, but you caused me to become healthy again.


## Psalms 30:4 (id: 1019030004)

4All you who are faithful to the covenant with Yahweh, sing to praise him! Remember what God, the holy one, has done and thank him!


## Psalms 30:5 (id: 1019030005)

5When he becomes angry, he is angry for only a very short time, but he is good to us all of our lives. We may cry during the night, but the next morning we will be joyful.


## Psalms 30:6 (id: 1019030006)

6As for me, I was calm when I said to myself, “No one will defeat me!”


## Psalms 30:7 (id: 1019030007)

7Yahweh, because you were good to me, at first you caused me to be secure as though I were a high mountain. But then I thought that you had turned away from me, and I became afraid.


## Psalms 30:8 (id: 1019030008)

8So I called out to you, and I pleaded for you to help me.


## Psalms 30:9 (id: 1019030009)

9I said, “Yahweh, what will you gain if I die? In what way will it benefit you if I go to the place where the dead people are? When I am dead I will certainly not be able to praise you, and I will not be able to tell others that you are trustworthy!


## Psalms 30:10 (id: 1019030010)

10Yahweh, listen to me, and act mercifully to me! Yahweh, help me!”


## Psalms 30:11 (id: 1019030011)

11But now you have healed me, and you have changed me from being sad to dancing joyfully. You have taken away the clothes that showed that I was very sad and given me clothes that showed that I was very joyful.


## Psalms 30:12 (id: 1019030012)

12So I will not be silent; I will sing out and praise you. Yahweh, you are my God, and I will thank you forever.


## Psalms 31:1 (id: 1019031001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; Yahweh, I have come to you to be protected; do not allow me to be defeated and disgraced. Since you always do what is fair, rescue me!


## Psalms 31:2 (id: 1019031002)

2Listen to me, and save me right now! Be like a huge rock on which I can be safe and like a strong fort in which I will be secure.


## Psalms 31:3 (id: 1019031003)

3Yes, you are like my huge rock and my fort; guide me and lead me because I worship you.


## Psalms 31:4 (id: 1019031004)

4You are the one who protects me, so keep me from falling into the hidden traps that my enemies have set for me.


## Psalms 31:5 (id: 1019031005)

5Yahweh, you are a God whom I can trust, so I put myself into your care because you will rescue me.


## Psalms 31:6 (id: 1019031006)

6Yahweh, I hate those who worship useless idols, but I trust in you.


## Psalms 31:7 (id: 1019031007)

7I will be very glad because you faithfully love me. You see me when I have been afflicted, and you know when I have had troubles.


## Psalms 31:8 (id: 1019031008)

8You have not allowed my enemies to capture me; instead, you have rescued me from danger.


## Psalms 31:9 (id: 1019031009)

9But now, Yahweh, act kindly toward me because I am distressed. Because I cry so much, I cannot see well, and I am completely exhausted.


## Psalms 31:10 (id: 1019031010)

10I have become very weak because I am so miserable; my life is getting shorter. I have become weak because of all my troubles; even my bones are becoming weaker.


## Psalms 31:11 (id: 1019031011)

11All of my enemies make fun of me, and even my neighbors despise me. Even my friends are afraid of me because they think that you are punishing me. When they see me on the streets, they run away.


## Psalms 31:12 (id: 1019031012)

12People have forgotten me like they forget people who are dead. They think I am as useless as a broken pot.


## Psalms 31:13 (id: 1019031013)

13I have heard people slandering me, and they have terrified me. My enemies are making plans to kill me.


## Psalms 31:14 (id: 1019031014)

14But Yahweh, I trust in you. I say confidently that you are the God I worship.


## Psalms 31:15 (id: 1019031015)

15My whole life is in your hands; save me from my enemies, from those who pursue me.


## Psalms 31:16 (id: 1019031016)

16Act kindly toward me and rescue me because you always faithfully love me.


## Psalms 31:17 (id: 1019031017)

17Yahweh, I call out to you, so do not allow others to disgrace me. I wish that wicked people may be disgraced; I wish that they may go down to the place where the people are silent and dead.


## Psalms 31:18 (id: 1019031018)

18I wish that you may cause people who tell lies to be unable to speak. Do that to people who are proud and to those who arrogantly accuse others.


## Psalms 31:19 (id: 1019031019)

19You have stored up many great and good things to do for those who have great respect for you. You do good things for those who go to you to be protected; everyone sees you doing that.


## Psalms 31:20 (id: 1019031020)

20You hide people in your presence where it is safe, and you protect them from others who plot to kill them. You hide them in safe places where their enemies cannot speak evil at them.


## Psalms 31:21 (id: 1019031021)

21Praise Yahweh! When my enemies surrounded the city in which I was living, he showed me wonderfully that he faithfully loves me.


## Psalms 31:22 (id: 1019031022)

22I was afraid and cried out in a hurry, “I have been separated from Yahweh!” but you heard me and answered my cry for help.


## Psalms 31:23 (id: 1019031023)

23You people who belong to Yahweh, love him! He protects those who are loyal to him, but he punishes the proud; he punishes them severely as they deserve.


## Psalms 31:24 (id: 1019031024)

24You who confidently expect Yahweh to do great things for you, be strong and be courageous!


## Psalms 32:1 (id: 1019032001)

1A psalm written by David, which will help people to be wise; Those whom God has forgiven for rebelling against him and those whose sin God does not look at, these are the ones who are truly fortunate!


## Psalms 32:2 (id: 1019032002)

2Those whose record of sins Yahweh has erased and those who no longer do deceitful things, these are the ones who are truly fortunate!


## Psalms 32:3 (id: 1019032003)

3When I did not confess my sins, my body was very weak and sick, and I groaned all day long.


## Psalms 32:4 (id: 1019032004)

4Day and night, Yahweh, you punished me severely. My strength disappeared like water that evaporates on a hot summer day.


## Psalms 32:5 (id: 1019032005)

5Then I confessed my sins to you; I stopped trying to hide them. I said to myself, “I will tell Yahweh the wrong things that I have done.” When I confessed them, you forgave me, so now I am no longer guilty for my sins.


## Psalms 32:6 (id: 1019032006)

6Therefore the people who honor you should pray to you when they are in great trouble. If they do that, difficulties will not come on them like a great flood.


## Psalms 32:7 (id: 1019032007)

7You are like a place where I can hide from my enemies; you protect me from troubles and enable me to shout, praising you for saving me from my enemies.


## Psalms 32:8 (id: 1019032008)

8Yahweh says to me, “I will instruct you about how you should conduct your life. I will teach you and watch over you.


## Psalms 32:9 (id: 1019032009)

9Do not be stupid like horses and mules that do not understand anything; they need bits so they will go in the direction you want them to go.”


## Psalms 32:10 (id: 1019032010)

10Wicked people will have many troubles that will make them sad, but those who trust in Yahweh will experience him faithfully loving them all the time.


## Psalms 32:11 (id: 1019032011)

11So, all you righteous people, rejoice about what Yahweh has done for you; you whose heart are pure, be glad and shout joyfully!


## Psalms 33:1 (id: 1019033001)

1You righteous people should shout joyfully to Yahweh because that is what he deserves.


## Psalms 33:2 (id: 1019033002)

2Praise Yahweh as you play songs on the harp. Praise him as you play harps that have ten strings.


## Psalms 33:3 (id: 1019033003)

3Sing a new song to him; play those instruments well, and shout joyfully as you play them.


## Psalms 33:4 (id: 1019033004)

4Yahweh always does what he says that he will do; we can trust that everything that he does is right.


## Psalms 33:5 (id: 1019033005)

5He loves everything that we do that is just and right. Yahweh helps people all over the earth because he always loves them.


## Psalms 33:6 (id: 1019033006)

6Yahweh created everything in the sky by commanding it. By what he commanded, he created all the stars.


## Psalms 33:7 (id: 1019033007)

7He gathered all the water into one huge mass like someone scoops liquid into a container.


## Psalms 33:8 (id: 1019033008)

8Everyone on the earth should honor Yahweh; everyone on the earth should honor him.


## Psalms 33:9 (id: 1019033009)

9When he spoke, he created the world. Everything started to exist when he commanded it to be.


## Psalms 33:10 (id: 1019033010)

10Yahweh stops the other nations from doing the things they want to do. He prevents them from doing the evil things that they plan to do.


## Psalms 33:11 (id: 1019033011)

11But what Yahweh decides to do will last forever. What he plans to do will never change.


## Psalms 33:12 (id: 1019033012)

12Yahweh blesses our nation, we who worship him; How fortunate are we, the nation that belongs to him forever!


## Psalms 33:13 (id: 1019033013)

13Yahweh looks down from heaven and sees all people.


## Psalms 33:14 (id: 1019033014)

14From where he rules, he looks down on all the people who live on the earth.


## Psalms 33:15 (id: 1019033015)

15He forms our inner beings, and he sees everything that we do.


## Psalms 33:16 (id: 1019033016)

16It is not because a king has a great army that he is able to win battles, and it is not because a soldier is very strong that he is able to defeat his enemy.


## Psalms 33:17 (id: 1019033017)

17It is foolish to think that because horses are very strong, they will be able to win a battle and save their riders.


## Psalms 33:18 (id: 1019033018)

18Do not forget that Yahweh watches over those who honor him, those who confidently expect him to faithfully love them.


## Psalms 33:19 (id: 1019033019)

19He saves them from dying before they should die; he preserves them when there is a famine.


## Psalms 33:20 (id: 1019033020)

20We trust Yahweh to help us; he protects us as a shield protects a soldier.


## Psalms 33:21 (id: 1019033021)

21We rejoice because of what he has done for us; we trust in him because he is holy.


## Psalms 33:22 (id: 1019033022)

22Yahweh, we pray that you will always faithfully love us while we confidently expect you to do great things for us.


## Psalms 34:1 (id: 1019034001)

1A psalm written by David when he pretended to be insane in front of King Abimelech so that the king would send him away; I will always thank Yahweh; I will constantly praise him.


## Psalms 34:2 (id: 1019034002)

2I will praise Yahweh for what he has done. All those who are oppressed should listen to me and rejoice.


## Psalms 34:3 (id: 1019034003)

3Join with me in telling others that Yahweh is great! You and I should together proclaim how glorious he is!


## Psalms 34:4 (id: 1019034004)

4I prayed to Yahweh, and he answered my prayer; he rescued me from all those who caused me to be afraid.


## Psalms 34:5 (id: 1019034005)

5Those who trust that he will help them will be joyful; they will never have to look down in disgrace.


## Psalms 34:6 (id: 1019034006)

6I was miserable, but I called out to Yahweh, and he heard me. He rescued me from all my troubles.


## Psalms 34:7 (id: 1019034007)

7An angel from Yahweh guards those who have an awesome respect for him, and the angel rescues them.


## Psalms 34:8 (id: 1019034008)

8Try for yourself, and you will experience that Yahweh is good to you! How fortunate are those who trust him to protect them.


## Psalms 34:9 (id: 1019034009)

9All you who belong to him, have an awesome respect for him! Those who do that will always have the things that they need.


## Psalms 34:10 (id: 1019034010)

10Lions are usually very strong, but sometimes even young lions are hungry and become weak. However, those who trust in Yahweh will have everything that they need.


## Psalms 34:11 (id: 1019034011)

11You who are my students, come and listen to me, and I will teach you how to have an awesome respect for Yahweh.


## Psalms 34:12 (id: 1019034012)

12If any of you wants to enjoy life and have a good long life,


## Psalms 34:13 (id: 1019034013)

13do not speak what is evil! Do not tell lies!


## Psalms 34:14 (id: 1019034014)

14Refuse to do evil; instead, do what is good! Always try hard to enable people to live peacefully with each other!


## Psalms 34:15 (id: 1019034015)

15Yahweh carefully watches over those who act righteously; he always responds to them when they call to him for help.


## Psalms 34:16 (id: 1019034016)

16But Yahweh works against those who do what is evil. After they die, people here on earth will forget them completely.


## Psalms 34:17 (id: 1019034017)

17Yahweh hears righteous people when they call out to him; he rescues them from all their troubles.


## Psalms 34:18 (id: 1019034018)

18Yahweh is always ready to help those who are discouraged; he rescues those who have no hope for anything good.


## Psalms 34:19 (id: 1019034019)

19Righteous people may have many troubles, but Yahweh rescues them from all those troubles.


## Psalms 34:20 (id: 1019034020)

20Yahweh protects them from being harmed; when their enemies attack them, they will not break any bones of those righteous people.


## Psalms 34:21 (id: 1019034021)

21Disasters will kill the wicked people, and Yahweh will punish those who oppose righteous people.


## Psalms 34:22 (id: 1019034022)

22Yahweh will save those who serve him. He will not condemn those who trust in him.


## Psalms 35:1 (id: 1019035001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, fight against those who fight against me! Fight with my enemies when they fight me!


## Psalms 35:2 (id: 1019035002)

2Be like a shield to protect me and come to help me!


## Psalms 35:3 (id: 1019035003)

3Lift up your spear and throw it at those who pursue me! Promise me that you will enable me to defeat my enemies.


## Psalms 35:4 (id: 1019035004)

4Those who are trying to kill me—make others disgrace and dishonor them. Push back and confuse those who are planning to do evil things to me.


## Psalms 35:5 (id: 1019035005)

5Send your angel to pursue them and to make them disappear like chaff that the wind blows away.


## Psalms 35:6 (id: 1019035006)

6Cause the path on which they run to be dark and slippery as your angel pursues them!


## Psalms 35:7 (id: 1019035007)

7Although I did not do anything wrong to them, they dug a deep pit for me to fall into; they hid a net in which they would catch me.


## Psalms 35:8 (id: 1019035008)

8Cause them to suddenly experience disaster! Cause their own nets to trap them. Cause them to fall into the pits that they have dug for me, and make them die in them!


## Psalms 35:9 (id: 1019035009)

9Then I will rejoice in what you, Yahweh, have done for me; I will be glad that you have rescued me.


## Psalms 35:10 (id: 1019035010)

10With my whole inner being I will say, “There is no one like Yahweh! No one else can rescue helpless people from powerful people. No one else can rescue weak and needy people from those who want to rob them.”


## Psalms 35:11 (id: 1019035011)

11People who tell lies stand in court and accuse me of doing things that I do not know anything about.


## Psalms 35:12 (id: 1019035012)

12In return for my doing good things for them, they do evil things to me, with the result that I feel that I am alone.


## Psalms 35:13 (id: 1019035013)

13When they were ill, I showed that I was sad. I did not eat any food, and I bowed my head as I prayed for them.


## Psalms 35:14 (id: 1019035014)

14I mourned and bowed my head as I prayed as though it were a friend or my mother for whom I was grieving.


## Psalms 35:15 (id: 1019035015)

15But when I had troubles, they were all happy about it. They unexpectedly gathered around to make fun of me. Strangers kept striking me; they would not stop.


## Psalms 35:16 (id: 1019035016)

16People who respect no one ridiculed me and snarled at me.


## Psalms 35:17 (id: 1019035017)

17Lord, how long will you only watch them doing this? Rescue me from their attacks; Save me from being killed by these men who are attacking me as lions attack other animals!


## Psalms 35:18 (id: 1019035018)

18Then, when many of your people gather, I will praise you, and I will thank you in front of all of them.


## Psalms 35:19 (id: 1019035019)

19Do not allow my enemies, who tell lies about me, defeat me and then rejoice about it! Do not allow those who hate me when there is no reason to hate me to laugh about how I suffer!


## Psalms 35:20 (id: 1019035020)

20They do not speak peacefully to people; instead, they look for ways to tell lies about people in our land who do no harm to anyone.


## Psalms 35:21 (id: 1019035021)

21They shout at me in order to accuse me; they say, “We saw the wrong things that you did!”


## Psalms 35:22 (id: 1019035022)

22Yahweh, you have seen these things, so do not be silent! Do not stay far from me!


## Psalms 35:23 (id: 1019035023)

23Arise, my God, plead my case in court, and successfully defend me!


## Psalms 35:24 (id: 1019035024)

24Yahweh, my God, because you are righteous, prove that I am innocent so that my enemies will not be able to gloat that I was judged to be guilty.


## Psalms 35:25 (id: 1019035025)

25Do not allow them to be able to say to themselves, “Yes, we have gotten rid of him just like we desired!”


## Psalms 35:26 (id: 1019035026)

26Cause those who rejoice about my misfortunes to be completely confused and disgraced; cause those who boast that they are much greater than I am to be disgraced and dishonored!


## Psalms 35:27 (id: 1019035027)

27But cause those who desire that you declare me innocent to be happy and shout joyfully; cause them to always say, “Yahweh is great! He is delighted to cause things to go well for those who serve him.”


## Psalms 35:28 (id: 1019035028)

28Then I will proclaim that you act in the right way, and I will praise you all the time.


## Psalms 36:1 (id: 1019036001)
