1A psalm written for the choir director by David, a man who served God faithfully; A continual desire to sin is in the inner beings of wicked people. They consider that they do not need to have an awesome respect for God.


## Psalms 36:2 (id: 1019036002)

2Because they want to believe good things about themselves, they do not think that God knows and hates their sins.


## Psalms 36:3 (id: 1019036003)

3Everything that they say is deceitful and full of lies; they no longer do what is good and are no longer wise.


## Psalms 36:4 (id: 1019036004)

4While they are lying on their beds, they plan to do things to harm others; they are determined to do things that are not good, and they never refuse to do what is evil.


## Psalms 36:5 (id: 1019036005)

5Yahweh, your faithful love for us reaches as high as the heavens; your faithfulness in doing what you have promised extends up to the clouds.


## Psalms 36:6 (id: 1019036006)

6Your righteous behavior is as permanent as the highest mountains; your acting justly will continue as long as the deepest oceans will continue. You take care of people and you take care of animals.


## Psalms 36:7 (id: 1019036007)

7God, your faithful love for us is very precious. You protect us like birds protect their baby birds under their wings .


## Psalms 36:8 (id: 1019036008)

8You provide for us plenty of food from the abundant supply that you have; your great gifts flow to us like a river.


## Psalms 36:9 (id: 1019036009)

9You are the one who causes everything to live; your light is what enables us to know the truth about you.


## Psalms 36:10 (id: 1019036010)

10Continue to faithfully love those who are faithful to you, and protect those who act righteously.


## Psalms 36:11 (id: 1019036011)

11Do not allow proud people to attack me, or allow wicked people to chase me away.


## Psalms 36:12 (id: 1019036012)

12Look where evil people have fallen on the ground, defeated; they were thrown down, and they will never rise again.


## Psalms 37:1 (id: 1019037001)

1A psalm written by David; Do not be bothered by what wicked people do. Do not desire to have the things that people who do wrong have


## Psalms 37:2 (id: 1019037002)

2because they will soon disappear like grass withers in the hot sun and dries up. Just like some green plants come up but die during the hot summer, evil people will soon die also.


## Psalms 37:3 (id: 1019037003)

3Trust in Yahweh and do what is good. If you do that, then you will live safely in the land he has given you, and that land will be a place where you can be faithful to God as you live your lives.


## Psalms 37:4 (id: 1019037004)

4Be delighted with all that Yahweh does for you; if you do that, he will give you the things that you desire most.


## Psalms 37:5 (id: 1019037005)

5Commit to Yahweh all the things that you plan to do; trust in him, and he will do whatever is needed to help you.


## Psalms 37:6 (id: 1019037006)

6He will show as clearly as the sunlight that you are innocent; he will show as clearly as the sun at noontime that all the things that you have decided are just.


## Psalms 37:7 (id: 1019037007)

7Be quiet in Yahweh’s presence and wait patiently for him to do what you want him to do. Do not be bothered when what evil men do is successful, when they are able to do the wicked things that they plan.


## Psalms 37:8 (id: 1019037008)

8Do not be angry about what wicked people do. Do not want to punish them yourself. Do not be envious of such people because you will only harm yourself if you try to do that.


## Psalms 37:9 (id: 1019037009)

9Someday Yahweh will get rid of wicked people, but those who trust in him will live safely in the land that he has given to them.


## Psalms 37:10 (id: 1019037010)

10Soon the wicked will disappear. You will look for them, but they will be gone.


## Psalms 37:11 (id: 1019037011)

11But those who are humble will live safely in their land. They will happily enjoy living peacefully and having the other good things that Yahweh gives them.


## Psalms 37:12 (id: 1019037012)

12Wicked people plan to harm righteous people; they snarl at them like wild animals.


## Psalms 37:13 (id: 1019037013)

13But Yahweh laughs at them because he knows that someday he will judge and punish the wicked people.


## Psalms 37:14 (id: 1019037014)

14Wicked people pull out their swords and they put strings on their bows, ready to kill people who are poor and to slaughter those who live righteously.


## Psalms 37:15 (id: 1019037015)

15But they will be killed by their own swords, and their bows will be broken.


## Psalms 37:16 (id: 1019037016)

16It is good to be righteous even if you do not have many possessions, but it is bad to be wicked even if you are very wealthy


## Psalms 37:17 (id: 1019037017)

17because Yahweh will completely remove the strength of wicked people, but he will sustain people who live righteously.


## Psalms 37:18 (id: 1019037018)

18Day by day Yahweh protects those who have not done any evil things; the things that Yahweh gives them will last forever.


## Psalms 37:19 (id: 1019037019)

19They will survive when calamities occur; when there are famines, they will still have plenty to eat.


## Psalms 37:20 (id: 1019037020)

20But wicked people will die; just as the beautiful wild flowers in the fields die under the hot sun and disappear like smoke, Yahweh will cause his enemies to suddenly disappear.


## Psalms 37:21 (id: 1019037021)

21The wicked people borrow money, but they are not able to repay it; righteous people, in contrast, have enough money to give generously to others.


## Psalms 37:22 (id: 1019037022)

22Those whom Yahweh has blessed will live safely in the land that he has given to them, but he will get rid of those people whom he has cursed.


## Psalms 37:23 (id: 1019037023)

23Yahweh protects those who do what is pleasing to him, and he will enable them to walk confidently wherever they go;


## Psalms 37:24 (id: 1019037024)

24even if they stumble, they will not fall down because Yahweh holds them by his hand.


## Psalms 37:25 (id: 1019037025)

25I was young previously, and now I am an old man, but in all those years, I have never seen that righteous people have been abandoned by Yahweh, nor have I seen that their children needed to beg for food.


## Psalms 37:26 (id: 1019037026)

26Righteous people are generous and happily lend money to others, and their children are a blessing to them.


## Psalms 37:27 (id: 1019037027)

27Turn away from doing evil, and do what is good. If you do that, you and your descendants will live in your land forever.


## Psalms 37:28 (id: 1019037028)

28This will happen because Yahweh likes to see people doing what is just, and he will never forsake righteous people. He will protect them forever; but he will get rid of the children of wicked people.


## Psalms 37:29 (id: 1019037029)

29Righteous people will own the land that Yahweh promised to give to them, and they will live there forever.


## Psalms 37:30 (id: 1019037030)

30Righteous people give wise advice to others, and they encourage other people to live rightly.


## Psalms 37:31 (id: 1019037031)

31They fill their minds with God’s laws; they do not stray from walking on God’s path.


## Psalms 37:32 (id: 1019037032)

32Those who are evil wait in ambush for righteous people in order to kill them as they walk by.


## Psalms 37:33 (id: 1019037033)

33But Yahweh will not abandon righteous people and let them fall into their enemies’ hands. He will not allow righteous people to be condemned when someone takes them to a judge to be put on trial.


## Psalms 37:34 (id: 1019037034)

34Be patient and trust that Yahweh will help you, and walk on his paths. If you do that, he will honor you by giving you the land that he promised, and when he gets rid of the wicked, you will see it happen.


## Psalms 37:35 (id: 1019037035)

35I have seen that wicked people who act like tyrants sometimes prosper like trees that grow well in fertile soil,


## Psalms 37:36 (id: 1019037036)

36but when I looked later, they were gone! I searched for them, but Yahweh had caused them to disappear.


## Psalms 37:37 (id: 1019037037)

37Notice the people who have not done evil things, those who act righteously; their descendants will have peace in their inner beings.


## Psalms 37:38 (id: 1019037038)

38But Yahweh will get rid of the wicked; he will also get rid of their descendants.


## Psalms 37:39 (id: 1019037039)

39Yahweh rescues righteous people; in times of trouble he protects them.


## Psalms 37:40 (id: 1019037040)

40Yahweh helps them and saves them; he rescues them from being attacked by wicked people because they go to him to be protected.


## Psalms 38:1 (id: 1019038001)

1A psalm written by David, asking God not to forget him; Yahweh, when you are angry with me, do not rebuke me and punish me!


## Psalms 38:2 (id: 1019038002)

2Now it is as though you have shot your arrows at me and wounded me; it is as though you have struck me and knocked me down.


## Psalms 38:3 (id: 1019038003)

3Because you have been angry with me, I am suffering great pain. Because of my sin, my whole body is diseased.


## Psalms 38:4 (id: 1019038004)

4All my sins are like a flood that covers my head; they are like a load that is very heavy; I cannot carry them.


## Psalms 38:5 (id: 1019038005)

5Because I have done foolish things, I have sores that have become worse, and they stink.


## Psalms 38:6 (id: 1019038006)

6Sometimes I am bent over, and sometimes I lie prostrate; I mourn all day.


## Psalms 38:7 (id: 1019038007)

7My body is burning with fever, and I am very ill.


## Psalms 38:8 (id: 1019038008)

8I am completely exhausted, and I have no strength. I am very distressed in my inner being, and I groan with pain.


## Psalms 38:9 (id: 1019038009)

9Yahweh, you know that I desire you to heal me; you hear me while I am groaning.


## Psalms 38:10 (id: 1019038010)

10My heart pounds heavily, and all my strength is gone. I am no longer able to see well.


## Psalms 38:11 (id: 1019038011)

11My friends and neighbors stay away from me because of my sores; even my own family stays far from me.


## Psalms 38:12 (id: 1019038012)

12Those who want to kill me set traps to catch me; those who want to harm me discuss the ways that they can get rid of me; they plot against me all day.


## Psalms 38:13 (id: 1019038013)

13Now I act like a deaf man and do not listen to what they say. I act like a man who cannot talk, and I say nothing to reply to them.


## Psalms 38:14 (id: 1019038014)

14I act like a man who does not answer when people talk to him because he cannot hear anything.


## Psalms 38:15 (id: 1019038015)

15But Yahweh, I trust in you. My Lord God, you will answer me.


## Psalms 38:16 (id: 1019038016)

16I said to you, “Do not cause me to die so that my enemies will rejoice! If troubles overwhelm me, my enemies will do very bad things to me!”


## Psalms 38:17 (id: 1019038017)

17I say that because I am about to fall down, and I constantly have pain.


## Psalms 38:18 (id: 1019038018)

18I confess the wrong things that I have done; I am very sorry for the sins that I have committed.


## Psalms 38:19 (id: 1019038019)

19My enemies are healthy and strong; there are many people who hate me for no reason.


## Psalms 38:20 (id: 1019038020)

20Those who do evil things to me in return for my doing good things to them oppose me because I try to do what is right.


## Psalms 38:21 (id: 1019038021)

21Yahweh, do not abandon me! My God, do not stay far from me!


## Psalms 38:22 (id: 1019038022)

22Lord, you are the one who saves me; Quickly come and help me!


## Psalms 39:1 (id: 1019039001)

1A psalm written by David for Jeduthun, the choir director; I said to myself, “I will be careful not to sin by the things that I say. I will not say anything to complain to you while wicked people are near to me and can hear me.”


## Psalms 39:2 (id: 1019039002)

2So I was completely silent, and I did not even talk about things that were good; but it was useless because I began to suffer even more.


## Psalms 39:3 (id: 1019039003)

3I became very anxious in my inner being. As I thought about my troubles, I became more worried. Then finally I said this:


## Psalms 39:4 (id: 1019039004)

4“Yahweh, show me how long I will live. Tell me when I will die. Tell me how many years I will live!


## Psalms 39:5 (id: 1019039005)

5It seems that you have caused me to live only a short time; my lifetime seems nothing to you. The time that all we humans live is as short as a puff of air.


## Psalms 39:6 (id: 1019039006)

6Then we disappear like a shadow does. It seems that all that we do is for nothing. We sometimes get a lot of money, but we do not even know who will get it after we die.


## Psalms 39:7 (id: 1019039007)

7So now, Yahweh, I can expect to receive nothing from anyone else. You are the only one from whom I confidently expect to receive blessings.


## Psalms 39:8 (id: 1019039008)

8Deliver me from the sins that I have committed. Do not allow foolish people to make fun of me.


## Psalms 39:9 (id: 1019039009)

9I did not say anything when you punished me because I knew that you were the one who caused me to suffer.


## Psalms 39:10 (id: 1019039010)

10But now, please stop punishing me! If you do not do that, I am about to die because of how you make me suffer.


## Psalms 39:11 (id: 1019039011)

11When you rebuke someone and punish him for the sin that he has committed, you destroy the things he loves like moths eat away at clothing. Our lives disappear like a puff of air.


## Psalms 39:12 (id: 1019039012)

12Yahweh, listen to me while I pray; pay attention to me while I cry out to you. Help me while I am crying. I am here on the earth for only a short time, like all my ancestors.


## Psalms 39:13 (id: 1019039013)

13Now please allow me to be alone and do not punish me anymore so that I may smile and be happy for a while before I die.”


## Psalms 40:1 (id: 1019040001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; I waited patiently for Yahweh to help me, and he listened to me when I called out to him.


## Psalms 40:2 (id: 1019040002)

2When I had many troubles, it was as though I was in a deep pit. But he lifted me up out of the mud and slime of that pit; he set my feet on a solid rock and enabled me to walk safely.


## Psalms 40:3 (id: 1019040003)

3He has given me a new song to sing, a song to praise him who is our God. Many people will find out what he has done for me, and they will revere and trust him.


## Psalms 40:4 (id: 1019040004)

4How fortunate are those who trust Yahweh to protect them, those who do not trust in idols or join with those who worship those false gods.


## Psalms 40:5 (id: 1019040005)

5O Yahweh, my God, you have done many wonderful things! No one can list all the wonderful things that you have planned for us. If I tried to tell others about all those wonderful things, I would not be able to because there would be too many for me to mention.


## Psalms 40:6 (id: 1019040006)

6Sacrifices and other offerings are not the things that delight you most. But you have enabled me to hear your commands. Animals burned on the altar and other offerings for our sins are not what you require most.


## Psalms 40:7 (id: 1019040007)

7So I said to you, “Yahweh, here I am, to obey the laws that have been written in the scroll, things that you want me to do.”


## Psalms 40:8 (id: 1019040008)

8O my God, I enjoy doing what you desire; I am always thinking about your laws within my inner being.


## Psalms 40:9 (id: 1019040009)

9When all your people were gathered together, I told them about how you do what is right and how you rescue us. Yahweh, you know that I have not refused to tell that to them.


## Psalms 40:10 (id: 1019040010)

10I have not kept within me the news that you always act justly; when many of your people have gathered together to worship you, I have told them that you are faithful to us and save us. I have not concealed that you faithfully love us and act loyally toward us.


## Psalms 40:11 (id: 1019040011)

11Yahweh, do not stop acting mercifully toward me. Because you faithfully love me and are loyal to me, protect me always.


## Psalms 40:12 (id: 1019040012)

12I have many troubles; I cannot count them. I am now suffering the things that happened because I sinned. I can no longer see because of my tears. The sins that I have committed are more than the hairs on my head. I am very discouraged.


## Psalms 40:13 (id: 1019040013)

13O Yahweh, please save me! Come quickly to help me!


## Psalms 40:14 (id: 1019040014)

14Humble those who are happy about my troubles, and cause them to be disgraced. Chase away those who are trying to get rid of me.


## Psalms 40:15 (id: 1019040015)

15I hope that those who make fun of me will be dismayed when you defeat them.


## Psalms 40:16 (id: 1019040016)

16But I hope that all those who go to worship you will be very joyful. I hope that those who love you because you saved them will shout repeatedly, “Yahweh is great!”


## Psalms 40:17 (id: 1019040017)

17As for me, I am poor and needy, but I know that the Lord has not forgotten me. O my God, you are the one who saves and helps me, so please come quickly and help me!


## Psalms 41:1 (id: 1019041001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director; How fortunate are those who provide for the poor; Yahweh will rescue those people when they have troubles.


## Psalms 41:2 (id: 1019041002)

2Yahweh will protect them and allow them to live for a long time. He will enable them to be happy in the land of Israel and will rescue them from their enemies.


## Psalms 41:3 (id: 1019041003)

3When they are sick, Yahweh will strengthen them and will heal them.


## Psalms 41:4 (id: 1019041004)

4When I was sick, I said, “Yahweh, act mercifully toward me and heal me; I know that I am sick because I have sinned against you.”


## Psalms 41:5 (id: 1019041005)

5My enemies say cruel things about me; they say, “How soon will he die, and then everyone will forget about him?”


## Psalms 41:6 (id: 1019041006)

6When my enemies come to me, they pretend to be concerned about me. They eagerly listen to all the bad news about me. Then they go away and tell everyone what is happening to me.


## Psalms 41:7 (id: 1019041007)

7All those who hate me whisper to others about me, and they hope that very bad things will happen to me.


## Psalms 41:8 (id: 1019041008)

8They say, “He will soon die because of his being sick; he will never get up from his bed before he dies.”


## Psalms 41:9 (id: 1019041009)

9Even a very close friend, whom I trusted very much, who often ate with me, has betrayed me.


## Psalms 41:10 (id: 1019041010)

10But Yahweh, act mercifully to me, and enable me to become healthy again. When you do that, I will be able to pay back my enemies.


## Psalms 41:11 (id: 1019041011)

11If you enable me to do that, with the result that my enemies do not defeat me, I will know that you are pleased with me.


## Psalms 41:12 (id: 1019041012)

12I will know that it is because I have done what is right that you have helped me, and I will know that you will enable me to be with you forever.


## Psalms 41:13 (id: 1019041013)

13Praise Yahweh, the God whom we Israelites worship; Praise him forever! Amen! I desire that it will be so!


## Psalms 42:1 (id: 1019042001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director; In the same way that a deer desires to drink water in a dry place, so I desire you, O God.


## Psalms 42:2 (id: 1019042002)

2I desire to be with you so desperately, O you, the real God. It is as though I am thirsting for water. I say to myself, “I shall certainly return to the temple in Israel and worship in your presence again, O God!”


## Psalms 42:3 (id: 1019042003)

3Every day and every night I weep, and the only thing I have to drink is my tears. This is because my enemies are always asking me, “Your God will certainly not help you!”


## Psalms 42:4 (id: 1019042004)

4I am sorrowful, as I remember when I used to go with the large groups of people to the temple where God dwelt in Jerusalem. On our way to the festival, we would all shout joyfully and sing to thank God for what he had done.


## Psalms 42:5 (id: 1019042005)

5So now I say to myself, “You certainly should not be sad and troubled! Confidently expect for God to rescue you! Then you will once again praise him, because of how he has saved you”


## Psalms 42:6 (id: 1019042006)

6O my God, I am discouraged, so I think about you. Your presence is refreshing, like the abundant waters of Jordan River that rush down from the peaks of Mount Hermon and from Mount Mizar.


## Psalms 42:7 (id: 1019042007)

7I am in turmoil like the rush of loud waterfalls. I am troubled as if many waves were crashing over me.


## Psalms 42:8 (id: 1019042008)

8Yahweh faithfully loves me every day, and so he causes me to sing to him every night a prayer to God, who keeps me alive.


## Psalms 42:9 (id: 1019042009)

9I say to God, who is like a huge rock on top of which I am safe {from attackers}, “Surely you have forgotten me! I am living sorrowfully because my enemies are afflicting me”


## Psalms 42:10 (id: 1019042010)

10My foes are always insulting me. They keep saying to me, “Your God will not help you!” When they insult me like that, it is like wounds that break my bones.


## Psalms 42:11 (id: 1019042011)

11But now I say to myself, “You certainly should not be sad and troubled! Confidently expect for God to rescue you! Then you will once again praise him, because of how he has saved you.”


## Psalms 43:1 (id: 1019043001)

1O God, announce that I am innocent. Defend me when people try to accuse me of doing evil, people who are unfaithful to you! Rescue me from people who deceive me and lie about me.


## Psalms 43:2 (id: 1019043002)

2{I expect you to do this} since you are the God who protects me, and yet you have abandoned me! I am living sorrowfully because my enemies are afflicting me.


## Psalms 43:3 (id: 1019043003)

3Speak words that drive away my oppressors, as light causes darkness to cease. Say truthful words to me! This will allow me to return to your temple on Mount Zion, where you dwell.


## Psalms 43:4 (id: 1019043004)

4After I come to Zion, I will go to your altar to worship you, O God, who causes me to be very joyful. There I will praise you, the God whom I worship, by playing the harp.


## Psalms 43:5 (id: 1019043005)

5But now I say to myself, “You certainly should not be sad and troubled! Confidently expect for God to rescue you! Then you will once again praise him, because of how he has saved you.”


## Psalms 44:1 (id: 1019044001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director. God, we ourselves have heard what our ancestors told us. They told us about the amazing wonders that you performed long ago.


## Psalms 44:2 (id: 1019044002)

2They told us about how you powerfully expelled the ungodly people and settled our ancestors in their land, as one plants a plant. They also told us that you punished those ungodly people and brought our ancestors into the land.


## Psalms 44:3 (id: 1019044003)

3It was not because our ancestors had a strong military that they conquered the people that lived in that land. Similarly, it was not because they were powerful that they were victorious. Rather, it was because you are powerful and desired to favor them that they did those things, for you delighted in them.


## Psalms 44:4 (id: 1019044004)

4You rule over me like a king, God. Empower your people to defeat our enemies.


## Psalms 44:5 (id: 1019044005)

5You empower us to defeat our enemies, and because of you we completely overwhelm those who fight against us.


## Psalms 44:6 (id: 1019044006)

6I do not trust that I can save myself by using my bow and arrows and my sword.


## Psalms 44:7 (id: 1019044007)

7This is because you have rescued us from our enemies. This is because you have disgraced our adversaries by defeating them.


## Psalms 44:8 (id: 1019044008)

8We have always been proud about what God has done for us, and we will thank him forever.


## Psalms 44:9 (id: 1019044009)

9But now you have rejected us and embarrassed us. When our armies march out to fight a battle, you no longer go with them to empower them to be victorious.


## Psalms 44:10 (id: 1019044010)

10You have caused us to retreat from our enemies, and they robbed anything they wanted from us.


## Psalms 44:11 (id: 1019044011)

11You have made us helpless victims to our enemies, like sheep that people are about to kill in order to eat. You have spread us out among many foreign peoples.


## Psalms 44:12 (id: 1019044012)

12You allowed our enemies to take us captive. It is as though you sold us to them for a very small price. You did not gain any profit from selling us!


## Psalms 44:13 (id: 1019044013)

13You have caused our neighbors to reproach us. They laugh at us and deride us.


## Psalms 44:14 (id: 1019044014)

14You caused them to make jokes about our country, and to shake their heads to indicate that they despise us.


## Psalms 44:15 (id: 1019044015)

15People constantly make me think about how I am disgraceful, and I am completely shameful.


## Psalms 44:16 (id: 1019044016)

16This happens because people speak harshly to me, My enemies and those who want to harm me shame me.


## Psalms 44:17 (id: 1019044017)

17All of these things have happened to us, even though we have not ceased from worshipping you, and we have not disobeyed the agreement that you made with our ancestors.


## Psalms 44:18 (id: 1019044018)

18We have continued to be loyal to you, and we have continued doing what you have commanded us to do.


## Psalms 44:19 (id: 1019044019)

19But it is as though you have destroyed us in battle, so that our bodies are laying in a place where wild animals could eat them. It is also as though you have thrown us into a very dark place.


## Psalms 44:20 (id: 1019044020)

20If we had stopped worshipping you, our God, and began worshipping a foreign god,


## Psalms 44:21 (id: 1019044021)

21you surely would have known that. This is because you know even what we secretly think.


## Psalms 44:22 (id: 1019044022)

22It is surely because you allow our enemies to attack us that they are constantly killing us. They kill us easily, for we are as defenseless as sheep that people kill in order to eat them.


## Psalms 44:23 (id: 1019044023)

23Defend us, Yahweh! It certainly seems as though you are asleep! Help us! Do not treat us as though we are not your people forever!


## Psalms 44:24 (id: 1019044024)

24You certainly are not favoring us! You surely are not saving us from our afflicters and oppressors.


## Psalms 44:25 (id: 1019044025)

25We have fallen down hopelessly, with our bellies on the ground.


## Psalms 44:26 (id: 1019044026)

26Rescue us! Come and help us! Save us from our enemies, for you promised to love us faithfully.


## Psalms 45:1 (id: 1019045001)

1A love song written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director, to be sung to the tune “Lilies.” In my inner being I am aroused by something beautiful to write about, a song that I will sing to the king. The words of this song will be written by me, a skilled writer.


## Psalms 45:2 (id: 1019045002)

2O King, you are the most handsome man in the world, and you always speak eloquently! So we know that God has always blessed you.


## Psalms 45:3 (id: 1019045003)

3You who are a mighty warrior, put on your sword! You are glorious and majestic.


## Psalms 45:4 (id: 1019045004)

4Ride on like a great king to defend the truth that you speak and the fair decisions that you make! Because you fight in many battles, you will learn to do deeds that your enemies will fear.


## Psalms 45:5 (id: 1019045005)

5Your arrows are sharp, and they pierce the hearts of your enemies. Soldiers of many nations will fall at your feet.


## Psalms 45:6 (id: 1019045006)

6The kingdom that God will give to you will remain forever. You rule over people justly.


## Psalms 45:7 (id: 1019045007)

7You love right actions, and you hate evil actions. Therefore God, your God, has chosen you to be king and has caused you to be happier than any other king.


## Psalms 45:8 (id: 1019045008)

8The perfume of various spices is on your robes. Musicians entertain you in ivory palaces by playing stringed instruments.


## Psalms 45:9 (id: 1019045009)

9Among your wives are daughters of other kings. At your right hand stands your bride, the queen, wearing beautiful ornaments of gold that comes from Ophir.


## Psalms 45:10 (id: 1019045010)

10Now I will say something to your bride: “Listen to me carefully! Forget the people who live in your home country, forget your relatives!


## Psalms 45:11 (id: 1019045011)

11Because you are very beautiful, the king will desire to be with you. He is your master, so you must obey him.


## Psalms 45:12 (id: 1019045012)

12The people from the city of Tyre will bring gifts to you; their rich people will try to persuade you to do favors for them.


## Psalms 45:13 (id: 1019045013)

13You, the king’s bride, enter the palace wearing beautiful robes made from gold thread.”


## Psalms 45:14 (id: 1019045014)

14O king, while she is wearing a gown that has many colors, her woman servants will lead her to you. She will have many other young women who accompany her.


## Psalms 45:15 (id: 1019045015)

15They will be very joyful as they are led along to enter your palace.


## Psalms 45:16 (id: 1019045016)

16Someday, your sons and your grandsons will become kings, just as your ancestors were. You will enable them to become rulers in many countries.


## Psalms 45:17 (id: 1019045017)

17As for me, I will enable people in every generation to remember the great things that you have done, and people will praise you forever.


## Psalms 46:1 (id: 1019046001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director. God is the one who protects us and causes us to be strong; he is always ready to help us when we have troubles.


## Psalms 46:2 (id: 1019046002)

2So, even if the earth shakes, we will not be afraid. Even if the mountains fall into the middle of the sea,


## Psalms 46:3 (id: 1019046003)

3and if the water in the sea roars and foams, and if the hills shake violently, we will not be afraid!


## Psalms 46:4 (id: 1019046004)

4Blessings that come from God are like a river that makes everyone in the city joyful, there where we worship him. It is the city where the temple of God, who is greater than any other god, exists.


## Psalms 46:5 (id: 1019046005)

5God is in this city, and it will never be destroyed; he will come to help the people in that city at dawn every day.


## Psalms 46:6 (id: 1019046006)

6Sometimes the people of many nations are terrified; kingdoms are overthrown; God speaks loudly like thunder, and the earth melts.


## Psalms 46:7 (id: 1019046007)

7But Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, is with us; the God whom Jacob worshiped is our refuge.


## Psalms 46:8 (id: 1019046008)

8Come and see the things that Yahweh does! Come and see the things he has destroyed all over the earth.


## Psalms 46:9 (id: 1019046009)

9He stops wars all over the world; he breaks bows and arrows; he destroys spears; he burns up shields.


## Psalms 46:10 (id: 1019046010)

10God says, “Be quiet and remember that I am God! People of all nations will honor me. People all over the earth will honor me.”


## Psalms 46:11 (id: 1019046011)

11So never forget that Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, is with us; the God whom Jacob worshiped is our refuge.


## Psalms 47:1 (id: 1019047001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director; You people all over the world, clap your hands! Shout joyfully to praise God!


## Psalms 47:2 (id: 1019047002)

2Yahweh, who is much greater than any other god, is awesome; he is a king who rules over all the world!


## Psalms 47:3 (id: 1019047003)

3He enabled us to defeat the armies of the people groups that lived in Canaan.


## Psalms 47:4 (id: 1019047004)

4He chose for us this land where we now live; we Israelite people, whom he loves, are proud that we own this land.


## Psalms 47:5 (id: 1019047005)

5God has gone up into his temple. The people shouted joyfully and blew trumpets as he went up.


## Psalms 47:6 (id: 1019047006)

6Sing songs to praise our God! Sing to praise him ! Sing to God, our king!


## Psalms 47:7 (id: 1019047007)

7God is the one who rules over everything in the world; sing a psalm to him!


## Psalms 47:8 (id: 1019047008)

8God sits on his sacred throne as he rules over the people of all ethnic groups.


## Psalms 47:9 (id: 1019047009)

9The rulers of those people groups gather in front of God’s people, the people descended from Abraham. God has more power than the weapons of all the kings on the earth; he is great, and all people everywhere will honor him.


## Psalms 48:1 (id: 1019048001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah; Yahweh is great, and he deserves to be greatly praised in the city where he lives, which is built on Zion, his sacred hill.


## Psalms 48:2 (id: 1019048002)

2That city on a high hill is beautiful; it is the city where the true God, the great king, lives, and it causes people all over the world to rejoice when they see it.


## Psalms 48:3 (id: 1019048003)

3God is in the strong towers there, and he shows that he protects the people in that city.


## Psalms 48:4 (id: 1019048004)

4Many kings gathered with their armies to attack our city,


## Psalms 48:5 (id: 1019048005)

5but when they saw it, they were amazed; they became terrified, and ran away.


## Psalms 48:6 (id: 1019048006)

6Because they were very afraid, they trembled like a woman who is about to give birth to a child.


## Psalms 48:7 (id: 1019048007)

7They shook as ships sailing from Tarshish shake in a strong wind.


## Psalms 48:8 (id: 1019048008)

8We had heard that this city was glorious, and now we have seen that it is. It is the city in which Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, lives. It is the city that God will preserve forever.


## Psalms 48:9 (id: 1019048009)

9God, here in your temple we think about how you love us as you promised to do.


## Psalms 48:10 (id: 1019048010)

10People all over the earth will praise you because you rule powerfully and justly.


## Psalms 48:11 (id: 1019048011)

11The people who live at Mount Zion should be happy! The people in all the cities of Judah should rejoice because you judge people fairly.


## Psalms 48:12 (id: 1019048012)

12You Israelite people should walk around Mount Zion and count the towers there;


## Psalms 48:13 (id: 1019048013)

13notice the walls there and examine their strongest parts so that you can tell your children about them.


## Psalms 48:14 (id: 1019048014)

14Say to your children, “This is the city of our God, the one who lives forever; he will guide us during all of our lives.”


## Psalms 49:1 (id: 1019049001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director. You people of all people groups, listen! You people all over the world,


## Psalms 49:2 (id: 1019049002)

2important people and unimportant people, rich people and poor people, everyone, listen to what I am saying.


## Psalms 49:3 (id: 1019049003)

3For what I am thinking is very sensible, and what I say will enable you to become wise.


## Psalms 49:4 (id: 1019049004)

4I think about wise words to tell you, and while I play my harp, I explain what they mean.


## Psalms 49:5 (id: 1019049005)

5I do not worry when I am in trouble, when I am surrounded by my enemies.


## Psalms 49:6 (id: 1019049006)

6These are evil men who trust that things will always go well for them because they are wealthy and who boast about being very rich.


## Psalms 49:7 (id: 1019049007)

7They may be rich, but no one can pay God money so that he can live forever! No one can pay God enough so that God will allow him to continue to live


## Psalms 49:8 (id: 1019049008)

8because that cost is too much, and he will never be able to pay enough.


## Psalms 49:9 (id: 1019049009)

9No one can pay God enough money so that he will live forever and never die and be buried!


## Psalms 49:10 (id: 1019049010)

10We see that foolish and stupid people die, but we see that wise people also die; they all leave their wealth, and others inherit it.


## Psalms 49:11 (id: 1019049011)

11They once had houses on land that they owned, but now their graves are their homes forever, the place where they will stay for all time!


## Psalms 49:12 (id: 1019049012)

12Even if people are great, that cannot prevent them from dying; people all die, the same as the animals do.


## Psalms 49:13 (id: 1019049013)

13That is what happens to those who foolishly trust in what they have accomplished, to those who are delighted in all that they possess.


## Psalms 49:14 (id: 1019049014)

14They are certain to die just like sheep when a shepherd leads them away to be slaughtered. In the morning the righteous people will rule over them, and then those wealthy people will die and their bodies will quickly decay in their graves; they will be where dead people are, far from their homes.


## Psalms 49:15 (id: 1019049015)

15But it is certain that God will rescue me so that I am not held fast in the place of the dead; he will take me to himself.


## Psalms 49:16 (id: 1019049016)

16So do not be dismayed when someone becomes rich and the houses where they live become more and more luxurious;


## Psalms 49:17 (id: 1019049017)

17for when he dies, he will take nothing with him; his wealth will not go with him.


## Psalms 49:18 (id: 1019049018)

18While a rich person is alive, he congratulates himself, and people praise him for being successful,


## Psalms 49:19 (id: 1019049019)

19but he will die and join his ancestors, who will never see daylight again.


## Psalms 49:20 (id: 1019049020)

20Even if someone is great, that cannot prevent him from dying; he will die, the same as the animals do.


## Psalms 50:1 (id: 1019050001)

1A psalm written by Asaph; God, the all\-powerful one, speaks; he summons all people, from the east to the west.


## Psalms 50:2 (id: 1019050002)

2His glory shines from Mount Zion in Jerusalem, an extremely beautiful city.


## Psalms 50:3 (id: 1019050003)

3Our God comes to us, and he is not silent. A great fire is in front of him, and a storm is around him.


## Psalms 50:4 (id: 1019050004)

4He comes to judge his people. He shouts to the angels in heaven and to the people on the earth.


## Psalms 50:5 (id: 1019050005)

5He says, “Summon those who faithfully worship me, those who made a covenant with me by offering sacrifices to me.”


## Psalms 50:6 (id: 1019050006)

6The angels in heaven declare, “God is righteous, and he is the supreme judge.”


## Psalms 50:7 (id: 1019050007)

7God says, “My people, listen! You Israelite people, listen, as I, your God, say what you have done that is wrong.


## Psalms 50:8 (id: 1019050008)

8I am not rebuking you for making sacrifices to me, for the offerings that you always burn on the altar for me.


## Psalms 50:9 (id: 1019050009)

9But I do not really need the bulls from your barns and the goats from your pens that you sacrifice,


## Psalms 50:10 (id: 1019050010)

10because all the animals in the forest belong to me, and all the cattle on a thousand hills also belong to me.


## Psalms 50:11 (id: 1019050011)

11I know and own all the birds in the mountains, and all the creatures that move around in the fields.


## Psalms 50:12 (id: 1019050012)

12So if I were hungry, I would not tell you to bring me some food because everything in the world belongs to me!


## Psalms 50:13 (id: 1019050013)

13I do not eat the flesh of the bulls that you sacrifice, and I do not drink the blood of the goats that you offer to me.


## Psalms 50:14 (id: 1019050014)

14The sacrifice that I really want is that you thank me and do all that you have promised to do.


## Psalms 50:15 (id: 1019050015)

15Pray to me when you have troubles. If you do that, I will rescue you, and then you will praise me.


## Psalms 50:16 (id: 1019050016)

16But I say this to the wicked people: Why do you recite my commandments or talk about the covenant that I made with you?


## Psalms 50:17 (id: 1019050017)

17For you have refused to allow me to discipline you, and you have rejected what I told you to do.


## Psalms 50:18 (id: 1019050018)

18Every time that you see a thief, you become his friend, and you spend much time with those who commit adultery.


## Psalms 50:19 (id: 1019050019)

19You are always talking about doing wicked things, and you are always trying to deceive people.


## Psalms 50:20 (id: 1019050020)

20You are always accusing members of your own family and slandering them.


## Psalms 50:21 (id: 1019050021)

21You did all those things, and I did not say anything to you, so you thought that I was a sinner just like you. But now I rebuke you and accuse you, right in front of you.


## Psalms 50:22 (id: 1019050022)

22So, all you who have ignored me, pay attention to this, because if you do not, I will tear you to pieces, and there will be no one to rescue you.


## Psalms 50:23 (id: 1019050023)

23The sacrifice that truly honors me is to thank me for what I have done; and I will save those who always do the things that I want them to.”


## Psalms 51:1 (id: 1019051001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, concerning the time when the prophet Nathan rebuked David after he had committed adultery with Bathsheba. O God, act mercifully toward me because you love me faithfully; because you are very merciful, forget the ways that I disobeyed you!


## Psalms 51:2 (id: 1019051002)

2Make me acceptable to you again, even though I did wrong things; forgive the guilt of my sin and accept me.


## Psalms 51:3 (id: 1019051003)

3I say that because I know the ways that I have disobeyed you; I cannot forget them.


## Psalms 51:4 (id: 1019051004)

4You, you only, are the one I have really sinned against, and you have seen the evil things that I have done. When you say that I am guilty, you are right, and when you judge me, you justly say that I deserve to be punished.


## Psalms 51:5 (id: 1019051005)

5I have been a sinner since the day that I was born; truly, I have been like that since my mother conceived me.


## Psalms 51:6 (id: 1019051006)

6What you desire is that in my inner being I desire what is true in order that you can teach me how to act wisely.


## Psalms 51:7 (id: 1019051007)

7Forgive the guilt of my sins, and after that happens, I will be completely acceptable to you; if you forgive me, then I will be absolutely right with you.


## Psalms 51:8 (id: 1019051008)

8Allow me to rejoice again; you have made me immeasurably sad, but now let me rejoice again.


## Psalms 51:9 (id: 1019051009)

9Do not continue to remember the sins that I have committed; forget the evil things that I have done.


## Psalms 51:10 (id: 1019051010)

10O God, make me want to do the things that you approve of. Make me want to do only what is right.


## Psalms 51:11 (id: 1019051011)

11Do not reject me as one of your people, and do not make your holy Spirit leave me.


## Psalms 51:12 (id: 1019051012)

12Make me happy again by rescuing me from my guilt, and always help me by making me sincerely want to obey you.


## Psalms 51:13 (id: 1019051013)

13If you do that, I will teach other sinners what you want them to do; they will repent and obey you.


## Psalms 51:14 (id: 1019051014)

14O God, you are the one who saves me; forgive me for being guilty of causing someone who was not my enemy to die. When you do that, I will sing joyfully about your being very good and righteous.


## Psalms 51:15 (id: 1019051015)

15O Yahweh, help me to speak in order that I may praise you.


## Psalms 51:16 (id: 1019051016)

16When people only bring sacrifices to you, that does not please you. If that were enough to please you, I would do the same. But you are not pleased with burnt offerings alone.


## Psalms 51:17 (id: 1019051017)

17The sacrifice that you really want is for people to be truly humble and sorry for having sinned. O God, you will not refuse that kind of sacrifice.


## Psalms 51:18 (id: 1019051018)

18O God, be good to the people who live in Jerusalem; make them able to rebuild the city walls.


## Psalms 51:19 (id: 1019051019)

19When that happens, they will bring you the proper sacrifices: normal animal sacrifices and sacrifices to be completely burned. They will burn young bulls on your altar, and you will be pleased.


## Psalms 52:1 (id: 1019052001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director when Doeg went to Saul and said, “David has gone to talk with Ahimelech, the high priest.” You proud man, you think that you are strong; you boast about the trouble that you make for others, but God faithfully protects people from you every day.


## Psalms 52:2 (id: 1019052002)

2All during the day you plan to get rid of others; what you say is like a sharp blade, and you are always deceiving others.


## Psalms 52:3 (id: 1019052003)

3You like doing what is evil more than you like doing what is good, and you like telling lies more than you like telling the truth.


## Psalms 52:4 (id: 1019052004)

4You, the one who says things to deceive people, you like to say things that hurt people!


## Psalms 52:5 (id: 1019052005)

5But God will get rid of you forever; he will grab you and drag you from your home and take you away from this world where people are alive.


## Psalms 52:6 (id: 1019052006)

6When righteous people see that, they will be awestruck, and they will laugh at what happened to you, and say,


## Psalms 52:7 (id: 1019052007)

7“Look what happened to the man who would not ask God to protect him; he trusted that his great wealth would save him; he grew more powerful by wickedly hurting other people.”


## Psalms 52:8 (id: 1019052008)

8But I am secure because I worship in God’s temple; I am like a strong green olive tree. I trust in God, who faithfully loves us forever.


## Psalms 52:9 (id: 1019052009)

9God, I will always thank you for everything you have done. I will wait patiently because you are so good, especially when I stand before your faithful people.


## Psalms 53:1 (id: 1019053001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be sung using a tune called “Mahalath.” Only foolish people say to themselves, “There is no God!” People who say that are corrupt; they commit terrible sins; there is not one of them who does what is good.


## Psalms 53:2 (id: 1019053002)

2God looks down from heaven and sees humans; he looks to see if any man is very wise and seeks to know God.


## Psalms 53:3 (id: 1019053003)

3But everyone has turned away from God. They are depraved and do disgusting, filthy things. No one does what is good.


## Psalms 53:4 (id: 1019053004)

4Will all these evil people never learn what God will do to them? They hurt Yahweh’s people with terrible violence. They had no guilt in what they did. They had the same expression on their faces as people eating bread at dinner. And what is worse is that they never prayed to Yahweh.


## Psalms 53:5 (id: 1019053005)

5But someday those people will become very terrified, although they have nothing to fear. For God will cause those who attack you to die, and he will scatter their bones. They have rejected God, so he will cause them to be defeated and completely disgraced.


## Psalms 53:6 (id: 1019053006)

6I wish that God would come and rescue the Israelite people! God, when you bless your people again, all the Israelite people, all the descendants of Jacob, will rejoice.


## Psalms 54:1 (id: 1019054001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be accompanied by stringed instruments; it was written when the people of Ziph went to Saul and told him that David was hiding in their area. God, by your power save me from my enemies, and show people that I have not done anything that is wrong!


## Psalms 54:2 (id: 1019054002)

2God, listen to my prayer; listen to what I say to you


## Psalms 54:3 (id: 1019054003)

3because strangers are trying to attack me; proud men are wanting to kill me, men who have no respect for you.


## Psalms 54:4 (id: 1019054004)

4But God is the one who helps me; Yahweh defends me from my enemies.


## Psalms 54:5 (id: 1019054005)

5He will cause the evil things that they want to do to me to happen to them instead; because you faithfully do what you have promised to me, destroy them.


## Psalms 54:6 (id: 1019054006)

6Yahweh, I will gladly give an offering to you because I want to, and I will thank you, for you are good to me;


## Psalms 54:7 (id: 1019054007)

7you have rescued me from all my troubles, and I have seen that you have defeated my enemies.


## Psalms 55:1 (id: 1019055001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be accompanied by stringed instruments; God, listen to my prayer, and do not turn away from me while I am pleading with you.


## Psalms 55:2 (id: 1019055002)

2Listen to me and answer me because I am overwhelmed by all my troubles.


## Psalms 55:3 (id: 1019055003)

3My enemies terrify me; wicked people oppress me. They cause me to have great troubles; they are angry with me, and they hate me.


## Psalms 55:4 (id: 1019055004)

4I am terrified, and I am very much afraid that I will die.


## Psalms 55:5 (id: 1019055005)

5I am very fearful and I tremble; I am completely terrified.


## Psalms 55:6 (id: 1019055006)

6I said, “I wish that I had wings like a dove! If I had wings, I would fly away and find a place to rest.


## Psalms 55:7 (id: 1019055007)

7I would fly far away and live in the wilderness.


## Psalms 55:8 (id: 1019055008)

8I would quickly find a safe place where my enemies could not strike me like a strong wind and rainstorm.”


## Psalms 55:9 (id: 1019055009)

9Lord, confuse my enemies and cause their plans to fail. I saw them hurting others by their violence and causing riots throughout the city.


## Psalms 55:10 (id: 1019055010)

10During each day and night they march around on top of its walls, committing crimes and causing trouble.


## Psalms 55:11 (id: 1019055011)

11They destroy things everywhere. They oppress people and defraud people in the marketplaces.


## Psalms 55:12 (id: 1019055012)

12If it were an enemy who was making fun of me, I could endure it. If it were someone who hates me, who despises me, I could hide from him.


## Psalms 55:13 (id: 1019055013)

13But it is someone who is just like me, my companion, someone who was my friend who is doing this to me.


## Psalms 55:14 (id: 1019055014)

14We previously had many good talks together; we walked around together in God’s temple.


## Psalms 55:15 (id: 1019055015)

15I desire that my enemies will go down alive to the place where the dead people are. I want this because they do evil things in their homes.


## Psalms 55:16 (id: 1019055016)

16But I will ask Yahweh, my God, to help me, and he will save me.


## Psalms 55:17 (id: 1019055017)

17Each morning, noontime, and evening I tell him what I am concerned about, and I moan, and he hears my voice.


## Psalms 55:18 (id: 1019055018)

18He saves my life and makes me safe when I am fighting a terrible battle against my enemies. There are many enemies coming to fight against me!


## Psalms 55:19 (id: 1019055019)

19God is the one who has ruled everything forever, and he will put those who fought against me in their place. He will cause my enemies to be defeated and disgraced because they do not change their evil behavior and because they do not have any respect for God.


## Psalms 55:20 (id: 1019055020)

20My companion, whom I mentioned previously, betrayed his friends and broke the agreement that he made with them.


## Psalms 55:21 (id: 1019055021)

21What he said was as easy to listen to as butter is easy to swallow, but in his inner being he hated people; his words were as soothing as olive oil, but they hurt people as sharp swords do.


## Psalms 55:22 (id: 1019055022)

22Put your troubles in Yahweh’s hands, and he will take care of you; he will never allow disaster to destroy righteous people.


## Psalms 55:23 (id: 1019055023)

23God, you will cause murderers and liars to die before they have lived half as long as they expect to live; but as for me, I will trust in you.


## Psalms 56:1 (id: 1019056001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, concerning the time the Philistines seized David in Gath; to be sung using the tune “Dove on distant oaks.” God, act mercifully toward me because men are attacking me! All day long an enemy presses closer and closer to me because they want to take my life.


## Psalms 56:2 (id: 1019056002)

2All day long my enemies seek to crush the life from me, there are many enemies attacking me!


## Psalms 56:3 (id: 1019056003)

3But whenever I am afraid, I trust in you.


## Psalms 56:4 (id: 1019056004)

4God, I praise you because you do what you have promised; I trust in you, and then I am not afraid. Ordinary humans certainly cannot harm me!


## Psalms 56:5 (id: 1019056005)

5All day long my enemies claim that I said things that I did not say; they are always thinking of ways to harm me.


## Psalms 56:6 (id: 1019056006)

6In order to cause trouble for me, they hide and watch everything that I do, waiting for an opportunity to kill me.


## Psalms 56:7 (id: 1019056007)

7So, God, punish them for the wicked things that they are doing; show that you are angry by defeating those people!


## Psalms 56:8 (id: 1019056008)

8You have counted all the times that I have been wandering alone; it is as though you have put all my tears in a bottle so that you can see how much I have cried. You have counted my tears and written the number in your book.


## Psalms 56:9 (id: 1019056009)

9When I call out to you, my God, my enemies will be defeated; I know that will happen because you are fighting for me.


## Psalms 56:10 (id: 1019056010)

10I praise you that you do what you have promised; Yahweh, I will always praise you for that.


## Psalms 56:11 (id: 1019056011)

11I trust in you, and as a result, I will not be afraid. I know that humans cannot really harm me!


## Psalms 56:12 (id: 1019056012)

12I will bring to you the offering that I promised; I will bring an offering to you to thank you


## Psalms 56:13 (id: 1019056013)

13because you have rescued me from being killed; you have kept me from stumbling. And so I will continue to live with God every day in his light that gives me life.


## Psalms 57:1 (id: 1019057001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, when David went into a cave to escape from Saul; to be sung using the tune “Do not destroy.” God, act mercifully toward me! Act mercifully toward me because I am coming to you to protect me. I request you to protect me as little birds are protected under their mother’s wings until the storm is ended.


## Psalms 57:2 (id: 1019057002)

2God, you who are greater than all other gods, I cry out to you, the one who enables me to be all that you desire.


## Psalms 57:3 (id: 1019057003)

3You will answer me from heaven and rescue me, but you will cause those who oppress me to be defeated and disgraced! God will always faithfully love me as he has promised me.


## Psalms 57:4 (id: 1019057004)

4Sometimes I am surrounded by my enemies, who are as ready to kill me as lions are to kill people; they are like lions that chew to bits the animals that they kill. But my enemies are human, and they have spears and arrows, not teeth; they say false things about me.


## Psalms 57:5 (id: 1019057005)

5God, show in the heavens that you are very great! Show your glory to people all over the earth!


## Psalms 57:6 (id: 1019057006)

6It is as if my enemies have spread a net to seize me, and I became very distressed. It is as if they have dug a deep pit along the path where I walk, but they themselves fell into it!


## Psalms 57:7 (id: 1019057007)

7God, I am very confident in you. I will sing to you, and I will praise you while I sing.


## Psalms 57:8 (id: 1019057008)

8It is an honor to wake up and praise you. I will arise before the sun rises and praise you while I play my big harp or my lyre.


## Psalms 57:9 (id: 1019057009)

9Lord, I will thank you among all the people; and I will sing songs of praise about you to many people groups.


## Psalms 57:10 (id: 1019057010)

10For your love for us is as great as the distance from the earth to the sky, and your faithfulness to us goes up to the clouds.


## Psalms 57:11 (id: 1019057011)

11God, show in the heavens that you are very great! Show your glory to people all over the earth!


## Psalms 58:1 (id: 1019058001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be sung using the tune “Do not destroy.” When you rulers speak, you never say what is right; you people never justly decide disputes.


## Psalms 58:2 (id: 1019058002)

2No, in your inner beings you think only about doing what is wrong, and you commit violent crimes everywhere in this land of Israel.


## Psalms 58:3 (id: 1019058003)

3Wicked people do wrong things and tell lies from the time that they are born.


## Psalms 58:4 (id: 1019058004)

4What wicked people say injures people like the venom of a snake. They refuse to listen to commands; it is as though they were deaf cobras.


## Psalms 58:5 (id: 1019058005)

5As a result, like a snake that does not respond when a charmer plays a flute or when someone sings magic songs, they do not pay attention when others rebuke them.


## Psalms 58:6 (id: 1019058006)

6God, as for these enemies who want to attack me like young lions, break the teeth in their mouths!


## Psalms 58:7 (id: 1019058007)

7Cause them to disappear as water disappears in dry ground! Cause the arrows that they shoot to have no heads!


## Psalms 58:8 (id: 1019058008)

8Cause them to become like snails that disappear in the slime; cause them to be like a baby that is born dead!


## Psalms 58:9 (id: 1019058009)

9I hope that you will get rid of them as fast as thornbushes are blown away after they are cut.


## Psalms 58:10 (id: 1019058010)

10People who do what is right will rejoice when they see God punish the wicked people; they will wash their feet in the blood of wicked people.


## Psalms 58:11 (id: 1019058011)

11Then people will say, “It is true that there is a reward for righteous people; and there is indeed a God who judges people justly here on the earth!”


## Psalms 59:1 (id: 1019059001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, when Saul, wanting to kill David, sent men to watch David’s house. God, save me from my enemies! Protect me from those who want to attack me!


## Psalms 59:2 (id: 1019059002)

2Keep me safe from men who want to do what is wicked, from men who are murderers!


## Psalms 59:3 (id: 1019059003)

3Look! They are waiting to kill me! Fierce men have gathered to assault me. Yahweh, they are doing that even though I have not done what is wrong!


## Psalms 59:4 (id: 1019059004)

4It is not because I have committed any sin against them that they run and get ready to attack me. Please look at my situation and help me.


## Psalms 59:5 (id: 1019059005)

5Yahweh my God, commander of the angel armies, the one we Israelites worship, arise and punish the people of all the nations who do not honor you; do not act mercifully toward those wicked people who have acted treacherously toward us.


## Psalms 59:6 (id: 1019059006)

6They return each evening, snarling like vicious dogs as they prowl around this city.


## Psalms 59:7 (id: 1019059007)

7They loudly say terrible things; they say things that destroy as much as swords do, because they are saying, “No one will hear us!”


## Psalms 59:8 (id: 1019059008)

8But Yahweh, you laugh at them. You scoff at the people of the pagan nations.


## Psalms 59:9 (id: 1019059009)

9God, I have confidence in you because you are very strong; you are my refuge.


## Psalms 59:10 (id: 1019059010)

10Because you love me, you will come to save me as you have promised; you will allow me to watch while you defeat my enemies.


## Psalms 59:11 (id: 1019059011)

11But do not kill them immediately; it is good that my people should not forget how you punished them! Instead, Lord, you who are like a shield that protects us, scatter them by your power, and then defeat them.


## Psalms 59:12 (id: 1019059012)

12Because what they say is sinful, allow them to be trapped for being proud. Because they are always cursing and telling lies,


## Psalms 59:13 (id: 1019059013)

13because you are angry, get rid of them; destroy them completely so that people will know that you rule over us, your Israelite people, and that you rule over all the earth.


## Psalms 59:14 (id: 1019059014)

14They return each evening, snarling like vicious dogs as they prowl around this city.


## Psalms 59:15 (id: 1019059015)

15They roam around, searching for food and if they do not find enough, they growl like dogs.


## Psalms 59:16 (id: 1019059016)

16But as for me, I will sing about your power; every morning I will sing joyfully about your faithfully loving us. I will sing about how you protected me when I was very distressed.


## Psalms 59:17 (id: 1019059017)

17God, you are the one who enables me to be strong; you are my refuge; you faithfully love me, just as you have promised in your covenant.


## Psalms 60:1 (id: 1019060001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, a psalm for teaching, to be sung using the tune “Lily of the promise.” David wrote it during the wars in northern Syria, and when Joab’s army, after returning from the battle, killed twelve thousand of the Edom people group in Salt Valley. I prayed, “God, you have rejected us Israelites! Because you have been angry with us, you have enabled our enemies to break through our ranks. Please enable us to be strong again!


## Psalms 60:2 (id: 1019060002)

2It was as though you made a big earthquake in which the ground split open. So now, make us strong again, because it is as though our country is falling apart.


## Psalms 60:3 (id: 1019060003)

3You have caused us, your people, to suffer very much; it is as though you had taken away our strength by making us drink strong wine.


## Psalms 60:4 (id: 1019060004)

4But you have raised a battle flag for those who honor you. They will show your banner when they face the enemies’ arrows.


## Psalms 60:5 (id: 1019060005)

5Answer our prayers and enable us by your power to defeat our enemies so that we, the people you love, will be saved.”


## Psalms 60:6 (id: 1019060006)

6Then God answered my prayer and spoke from his temple, saying, “Because I have conquered your enemies, I will divide the city of Shechem, and I will distribute among my people the land in Succoth Valley.


## Psalms 60:7 (id: 1019060007)

7The region of Gilead is mine; the people of the tribe of Manasseh are mine; the tribe of Ephraim is like my helmet; and the tribe of Judah is like the scepter with which I rule.


## Psalms 60:8 (id: 1019060008)

8The region of Moab is like my washbasin; I throw my sandal into the region of Edom to show that it belongs to me; I shout triumphantly because I have defeated the people of all the region of Philistia.


## Psalms 60:9 (id: 1019060009)

9Because I want to defeat the people of Edom, who will lead my army to their capital city that has strong walls around it?”


## Psalms 60:10 (id: 1019060010)

10So, God, it seems that you have truly abandoned us; it seems that you do not go with us when our armies march out to fight our enemies.


## Psalms 60:11 (id: 1019060011)

11We need you to help us when we fight against our enemies because the help that humans can give us is worthless.


## Psalms 60:12 (id: 1019060012)

12But with you helping us, we will win; you will enable us to defeat our enemies.


## Psalms 61:1 (id: 1019061001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, to be accompanied by musical instruments. God, listen to me and answer my prayer.


## Psalms 61:2 (id: 1019061002)

2While I am discouraged and far from my home, I am calling out to you. Lead me to a place that will be like a high rock on top of which I will be safe.


## Psalms 61:3 (id: 1019061003)

3You have been my refuge; you have been like a strong tower in which my enemies cannot attack me.


## Psalms 61:4 (id: 1019061004)

4Allow me to live close to your sacred tent all during my life! Allow me to be safe as a little bird is safe under its mother’s wings.


## Psalms 61:5 (id: 1019061005)

5God, you heard me when I solemnly promised to give offerings to you; you have given to me the blessings that belong to those who have an awesome respect for you.


## Psalms 61:6 (id: 1019061006)

6I am the king of Israel; please allow me to live and rule for many years, and allow my descendants to rule also.


## Psalms 61:7 (id: 1019061007)

7Allow us to rule forever while you observe us; watch over us while you faithfully love us and do for us what you promised.


## Psalms 61:8 (id: 1019061008)

8If you do that, I will always sing to praise you while I offer to you each day the sacrifices that I promised to give to you.


## Psalms 62:1 (id: 1019062001)

1A psalm written by David for Jeduthun, the choir leader; God is the only one who can give me peace in my inner being, and he is the one who saves me from my enemies.


## Psalms 62:2 (id: 1019062002)

2Only he is like a huge rock on which I can be safe; he is like a fortress high up that my enemies cannot climb.


## Psalms 62:3 (id: 1019062003)

3When will you, my enemies, stop attacking me? I feel that I am as weak against you as a leaning wall or a broken\-down fence.


## Psalms 62:4 (id: 1019062004)

4My enemies plan to remove me from my important position so that people no longer honor me. They delight in telling lies. They bless people by what they say, but in their inner beings they curse those people.


## Psalms 62:5 (id: 1019062005)

5God is the only one who gives me peace in my inner being; he is the one whom I confidently expect to help me.


## Psalms 62:6 (id: 1019062006)

6Only he is like a huge rock on which I can be safe; he is like a shelter; my enemies can never reach me there.


## Psalms 62:7 (id: 1019062007)

7God is the one who saves me and honors me. He is like a huge, strong rock on which I can find shelter.


## Psalms 62:8 (id: 1019062008)

8You my people, always trust in him. Tell him all your troubles because we go to him for safety.


## Psalms 62:9 (id: 1019062009)

9People who are considered to be unimportant are as unreliable as a breath of air; people who are considered to be important also really amount to nothing. If you put them all on a scale, it would be as if they weighed less than a puff of air.


## Psalms 62:10 (id: 1019062010)

10Do not trust in money gained by extorting it from others; do not try to gain anything by robbing others. If you become very wealthy, do not trust in your money.


## Psalms 62:11 (id: 1019062011)

11I have heard God say more than once that he is the one who really has power,


## Psalms 62:12 (id: 1019062012)

12and that he is the one who faithfully loves us, as he promised. He rewards every one of us according to the deeds that we do.


## Psalms 63:1 (id: 1019063001)

1A psalm written by David when he was in the wilderness in Judah. God, you are the God whom I worship. I greatly desire to be with you as a person in a dry hot wilderness greatly desires some water.


## Psalms 63:2 (id: 1019063002)

2I have been with you in your temple In order to see that you are loving and powerful.


## Psalms 63:3 (id: 1019063003)

3You always love me, as you promised in your covenant; this is worth more than my entire life, so I will always praise you.


## Psalms 63:4 (id: 1019063004)

4I will praise you all the time that I live; I will lift up my hands to you while I pray.


## Psalms 63:5 (id: 1019063005)

5You fill me up and you meet every need I have. My response to you is much like when I eat a delicious banquet of rich foods and the food fills me. I will have great happiness when I praise you with the words that I speak about you.


## Psalms 63:6 (id: 1019063006)

6While I lie on my bed, I think about you. I think about you all during the night.


## Psalms 63:7 (id: 1019063007)

7For you have always helped me, and I sing joyfully knowing that you protect me as a bird protects her young under her wings.


## Psalms 63:8 (id: 1019063008)

8I follow you closely, and your hand protects me.


## Psalms 63:9 (id: 1019063009)

9But those who are trying to kill me will die and descend into the place of the dead;


## Psalms 63:10 (id: 1019063010)

10they will be killed in battles and their corpses will be eaten by dogs.


## Psalms 63:11 (id: 1019063011)

11But I, the king of Israel, will rejoice in what God has done; and all those who ask God to confirm their word will praise him, but he will not allow liars to say anything.


## Psalms 64:1 (id: 1019064001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director. God, listen to me as I tell you the things about which I am worried. I am afraid of my enemies; please save me from them.


## Psalms 64:2 (id: 1019064002)

2Protect me from what wicked men are planning to do to me; protect me from that group of men who do what is evil.


## Psalms 64:3 (id: 1019064003)

3The hostile things they say are like sharp swords; their cruel words are like arrows.


## Psalms 64:4 (id: 1019064004)

4They are not afraid of anyone; they lie about people and slander those who have done no wrong. They are like someone who suddenly jumps up from where he is hiding and shoots arrows at his enemies.


## Psalms 64:5 (id: 1019064005)

5They encourage each other about doing the evil things that they are planning to do; they talk with each other about where they can set traps to catch people. They say, “No one will see what we are doing


## Psalms 64:6 (id: 1019064006)

6because we have planned very well the things that we are going to do.” What people can think and plan in their inner beings is truly amazing!


## Psalms 64:7 (id: 1019064007)

7But it will be as though God will shoot his arrows at them, and suddenly they will be wounded.


## Psalms 64:8 (id: 1019064008)

8Because what they say proves they are guilty, God will get rid of them. Everyone who sees what has happened to them will shake their heads to mock them.


## Psalms 64:9 (id: 1019064009)

9Then everyone will be afraid to sin because of what might happen to them also; they will tell others what God has done, and they themselves will think much about it.


## Psalms 64:10 (id: 1019064010)

10Righteous people should rejoice because of what Yahweh has done; they should go to him to find refuge; and all those who honor him will praise him.


## Psalms 65:1 (id: 1019065001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director. God, it is right for us to praise you in Jerusalem and to do what we have promised you that we would do


## Psalms 65:2 (id: 1019065002)

2because you answer our prayers. People everywhere will come to you


## Psalms 65:3 (id: 1019065003)

3Our many sins are like a very heavy burden to us, but you forgive us.


## Psalms 65:4 (id: 1019065004)

4How fortunate are those whom you have chosen to always be in your temple courtyards. We will be satisfied with all the blessings that you will give us because we worship you in your sacred temple.


## Psalms 65:5 (id: 1019065005)

5God, when we pray to you, you answer us and save us by doing awesome deeds; you are the one who rescues us; people who live in very remote places on the earth, on the other side of the oceans, trust in you.


## Psalms 65:6 (id: 1019065006)

6You are the one who put the mountains in their places, showing that you are very powerful.


## Psalms 65:7 (id: 1019065007)

7You are the one who calms the seas when they roar, and stop the waves from pounding on the shore; you also calm people when they cause a lot of trouble.


## Psalms 65:8 (id: 1019065008)

8People who live in very remote places on the earth are awed by the miracles that you perform; because of what you do, people who live far to the west and far to the east shout joyfully.


## Psalms 65:9 (id: 1019065009)

9You take care of the soil and send rain, causing many good things to grow; you fill the streams with water and cause grain to grow. This is what you have determined would happen.


## Psalms 65:10 (id: 1019065010)

10You send plenty of rain on the fields that have been plowed, and you fill the furrows with water. With showers you soften the hard clods of soil, and you bless the soil by causing young plants to grow.


## Psalms 65:11 (id: 1019065011)

11Because you bless the soil, there are very good crops at harvest season; wherever you have gone, good crops are very abundant.


## Psalms 65:12 (id: 1019065012)

12The pastures in the wilderness are wet with the morning dew, it is as though the hills are singing joyful songs.


## Psalms 65:13 (id: 1019065013)

13The meadows are covered with sheep and goats, and the valleys are full of grain; it is as though they also sing and shout joyfully.


## Psalms 66:1 (id: 1019066001)

1A psalm that is a song for the choir director. Tell everyone on the earth that they should sing joyfully to praise God!


## Psalms 66:2 (id: 1019066002)

2They should sing songs that say that God is very great, and they should tell everyone that he is very glorious!


## Psalms 66:3 (id: 1019066003)

3They should say to God, “The things that you do are awesome! Your power is very great, with the result that your enemies cringe in front of you.”


## Psalms 66:4 (id: 1019066004)

4Everyone on the earth will worship God, sing to praise him, and honor him.


## Psalms 66:5 (id: 1019066005)

5Come and think about what God has done! Think about the awesome things that he has done among people.


## Psalms 66:6 (id: 1019066006)

6He caused the sea to become dry land, with the result that our ancestors were able to walk right through it. There we rejoiced because of what he had done.


## Psalms 66:7 (id: 1019066007)

7He rules forever by his power, and he keeps watching all the nations to see what evil things they do. The nations that want to rebel against him should not be proud.


## Psalms 66:8 (id: 1019066008)

8You people of all nations, praise our God! Praise him loudly in order that people will hear you as you praise him.


## Psalms 66:9 (id: 1019066009)

9He has kept us alive, and he has not allowed us to fall into disaster.


## Psalms 66:10 (id: 1019066010)

10God, you have tested us; you have allowed us to experience great difficulties to make our lives become pure as people put precious metals in a hot fire to burn out what is impure.


## Psalms 66:11 (id: 1019066011)

11It is as if you allowed us to fall into traps, and you forced us to endure difficult things that were like heavy loads to carry on our backs.


## Psalms 66:12 (id: 1019066012)

12You allowed our enemies to trample on us; we experienced difficulties walking through fires and floods, but now you have made us safe.


## Psalms 66:13 (id: 1019066013)

13I will bring to your temple offerings that are to be completely burned on the altar; I will offer to you what I promised.


## Psalms 66:14 (id: 1019066014)

14When I was experiencing much trouble, I said that I would bring offerings to you if you rescued me; and you did rescue me, so I will bring to you what I promised.


## Psalms 66:15 (id: 1019066015)

15I will bring sheep to be burned on the altar, and I will also sacrifice bulls and goats; when they are burning, you will be pleased as the smoke rises up to you.


## Psalms 66:16 (id: 1019066016)

16All you people who have a reverential respect for God, come and listen, and I will tell you what he has done for me.


## Psalms 66:17 (id: 1019066017)

17I called out to him to help me, and I praised him while I was speaking to him.


## Psalms 66:18 (id: 1019066018)

18If I had ignored the sins that I had committed, the Lord would not have paid any attention to me.


## Psalms 66:19 (id: 1019066019)

19But because I confessed my sins, God has listened to me and has paid attention to my prayers.


## Psalms 66:20 (id: 1019066020)

20I praise God because he has not ignored my prayers; he continues to love me as he promised in his covenant to do.


## Psalms 67:1 (id: 1019067001)

1A psalm for the choir director, to be accompanied by stringed instruments. God, act mercifully toward us and bless us; act kindly toward us.


## Psalms 67:2 (id: 1019067002)

2Do this in order that everyone in the world may know what you want them to do, and the people of all nations may know that you have the power to save them.


## Psalms 67:3 (id: 1019067003)

3God, I desire that all people groups may praise you; I want them all to praise you!


## Psalms 67:4 (id: 1019067004)

4I desire that the people of all nations will be glad and sing joyfully because you judge the people groups equally, and you guide all the nations in the world.


## Psalms 67:5 (id: 1019067005)

5God, I desire that the people groups may praise you; I want them all to praise you!


## Psalms 67:6 (id: 1019067006)

6Good crops have grown on our land; God, our God, has blessed us.


## Psalms 67:7 (id: 1019067007)

7Because God has blessed us, I desire that all people everywhere on the earth may have an awesome respect for him.


## Psalms 68:1 (id: 1019068001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director. God, arise and scatter your enemies, and cause those who hate you to run away from you.


## Psalms 68:2 (id: 1019068002)

2As wind blows smoke away, you chase your enemies away. As wax melts when it is near a fire, may you cause wicked people to disappear.


## Psalms 68:3 (id: 1019068003)

3But may the righteous people be joyful; may they rejoice when they are in God’s presence; may they be happy and very joyful.


## Psalms 68:4 (id: 1019068004)

4Sing to God; sing to praise him; sing a song for him who rides in the desert plains; his name is Yahweh; be glad when you are in his presence.


## Psalms 68:5 (id: 1019068005)

5God, who lives in his sacred temple, is like a father to those who are orphans, and he is the one who protects widows.


## Psalms 68:6 (id: 1019068006)

6He provides families for those who have no one to live with. He frees prisoners and enables them to be successful, but those who rebel against him will be forced to live in a very hot and dry land.


## Psalms 68:7 (id: 1019068007)

7God, you led your people out of Egypt, and then you marched with them through the desert.


## Psalms 68:8 (id: 1019068008)

8After you did that, the earth shook at Mount Sinai when you appeared to your people, and rain poured down from the sky, and your people worshiped you.


## Psalms 68:9 (id: 1019068009)

9You caused plenty of rain to fall there in the wilderness, and so you enabled good crops to grow again on that land that you gave to us Israelites.


## Psalms 68:10 (id: 1019068010)

10Your people built homes there; because you were good to them, you provided food for those who were poor.


## Psalms 68:11 (id: 1019068011)

11The Lord spoke this message, and many people took his message to other places.


## Psalms 68:12 (id: 1019068012)

12(12\-13\) They proclaimed, “Many kings and their armies are running away from our army!” When our army brought back to their homes the things that they captured, the women who were at home divided up those things among themselves and among their families. They got statues of pigeons whose wings were covered with silver and whose feathers were covered with pure yellow gold.
