But some of the people stayed with the sheep and did not go to fight in the battle. Why did you not go?


## Psalms 68:14 (id: 1019068014)

14When Almighty God scattered the enemy kings and their armies, it reminded me of a snowstorm on Mount Zalmon!


## Psalms 68:15 (id: 1019068015)

15There is a very high mountain in the Bashan hills, a mountain that has many peaks.


## Psalms 68:16 (id: 1019068016)

16But the people who live near that mountain should not envy those who live near Mount Zion, the mountain on which God chose to live! Yahweh will live there forever!


## Psalms 68:17 (id: 1019068017)

17After we defeated all our enemies, it was as though the Lord, surrounded by many thousands of strong chariots, descended from Mount Sinai and came into the sacred temple in Jerusalem.


## Psalms 68:18 (id: 1019068018)

18He ascended the sacred mountain where his temple is and took with him many people who had been captured in battles; he received gifts from the enemies whom he had defeated. He received gifts even from those who had rebelled against him, and Yahweh, our God, will live there in his sacred temple forever.


## Psalms 68:19 (id: 1019068019)

19Praise the Lord, who helps us carry our heavy loads every day; he is the one who saves us.


## Psalms 68:20 (id: 1019068020)

20Our God is the God who saves us; He is Yahweh, our Lord, the one who allows us to escape from dying in battles.


## Psalms 68:21 (id: 1019068021)

21But God will smash the heads of his enemies, the long\-haired skulls of those who continue to behave sinfully.


## Psalms 68:22 (id: 1019068022)

22The Lord said, “I will bring back the corpses of my enemies who were killed in Bashan, and I will bring back those who sank deep in the ocean and drowned.


## Psalms 68:23 (id: 1019068023)

23I will do that so that you may wash your feet in their blood, and your dogs can also lap up some of your enemies’ blood.”


## Psalms 68:24 (id: 1019068024)

24God, many people see you march triumphantly into your sacred temple, celebrating that you have defeated your enemies. You march like a king does, and a large crowd walks with you.


## Psalms 68:25 (id: 1019068025)

25The singers are in front, and the people who play stringed instruments are at the rear, and young women who are beating their tambourines are between them.


## Psalms 68:26 (id: 1019068026)

26They are all singing, “You Israelite people, praise God when you gather together; praise Yahweh, all you who are descendants of Jacob!”


## Psalms 68:27 (id: 1019068027)

27First come the people of the tribe of Benjamin, the smallest tribe, and following them come the leaders of the tribe of Judah and their group, and following them come the leaders of the tribes of Zebulun and Naphtali.


## Psalms 68:28 (id: 1019068028)

28You people of Israel, God made our tribes very strong. God, help us with your power as you helped us in the past.


## Psalms 68:29 (id: 1019068029)

29Show us that you are strong, there where you are in your temple in Jerusalem; kings bring gifts to you there.


## Psalms 68:30 (id: 1019068030)

30Shout as you defeat your enemies, such as those in Egypt, who are like wild animals living in the reeds. Shout as you defeat the powerful nations, who are like herds of bulls. Shame them; make them bow down and give you gifts. Drive away and scatter the people groups who love to attack other nations.


## Psalms 68:31 (id: 1019068031)

31Then the leaders of Egypt will bring gifts to you. then the people in Ethiopia will rush to lift up their hands to praise you.


## Psalms 68:32 (id: 1019068032)

32You people who are citizens of kingdoms all over the world, sing to God! Sing praises to Yahweh!


## Psalms 68:33 (id: 1019068033)

33Sing to the God, the one who rides in the sky, the sky that he created long ago. Listen as he shouts with a very powerful voice.


## Psalms 68:34 (id: 1019068034)

34Proclaim that God is very powerful; he is the king that rules over Israel, and in the skies he also shows that he is powerful.


## Psalms 68:35 (id: 1019068035)

35God is awesome as he comes out of his sacred temple; he is the God whom we Israelite people worship. He gives power and strength to his people. Praise God!


## Psalms 69:1 (id: 1019069001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director. O God, save me because I am in great danger. It is as though the flood water were up to my neck, and I were about to drown.


## Psalms 69:2 (id: 1019069002)

2I continue to sink in the deep mud, and there is no solid ground for me to stand on. I am in deep water, and the flood is swirling around me.


## Psalms 69:3 (id: 1019069003)

3I am exhausted from calling out for help; my throat is very dry. Because I have cried so much as I have waited for God to help me, my eyes are swollen from tears.


## Psalms 69:4 (id: 1019069004)

4Those who hate me when there is no reason to hate me are more than the number of hairs on my head! Those who want to get rid of me are strong, and they tell lies about me. They demand that I return to them things that I did not steal!


## Psalms 69:5 (id: 1019069005)

5O God, you see the sins that I have committed. You know that I have foolishly disobeyed your laws.


## Psalms 69:6 (id: 1019069006)

6O Yahweh God, commander of the angel armies, do not allow the wrong things that I have done cause those who trust in you to be disappointed. O God, whom we Israelite people worship, do not allow me to cause them to be shamed.


## Psalms 69:7 (id: 1019069007)

7People have insulted me because I am devoted to you. They have thoroughly humiliated me.


## Psalms 69:8 (id: 1019069008)

8Even my own older brothers act as if they do not know me; they treat me like a foreigner.


## Psalms 69:9 (id: 1019069009)

9Some people have despised your temple; but because I have tried to keep your temple holy, people have caused trouble for me. So it is as though those who are insulting you are also insulting me.


## Psalms 69:10 (id: 1019069010)

10When I have humbled myself and fasted to show my sadness about the disgraceful things that they have done to your temple, they just insult me.


## Psalms 69:11 (id: 1019069011)

11When I put on rough sackcloth to show that I am sad, they laugh at me.


## Psalms 69:12 (id: 1019069012)

12Even the elders of the city say bad things about me. The drunkards of the city sing disgusting songs about me.


## Psalms 69:13 (id: 1019069013)

13But Yahweh, I will continue praying to you. At the time that you choose, answer me and rescue me because you faithfully love me, as you have promised to do.


## Psalms 69:14 (id: 1019069014)

14Do not allow me to sink anymore in the mud. Rescue me from those who hate me! Lift me up out of these deep waters!


## Psalms 69:15 (id: 1019069015)

15Do not allow the floods to swirl around me; do not allow the deep mud to swallow me; keep me from sinking into the pit of death.


## Psalms 69:16 (id: 1019069016)

16O Yahweh, answer my prayer and help me because you are good and I can depend on your love for me. You have not punished me for what I deserve. I know you will listen to me!


## Psalms 69:17 (id: 1019069017)

17Do not hide yourself from me; answer me quickly because I am in great trouble.


## Psalms 69:18 (id: 1019069018)

18Come near to me and save me; rescue me from my enemies.


## Psalms 69:19 (id: 1019069019)

19You know that I am insulted and that people shame and dishonor me; you know who all my enemies are.


## Psalms 69:20 (id: 1019069020)

20Their insults have deeply offended me, and I feel helpless. I searched for someone who would pity me, but there was no one. I wanted someone to encourage me, but there was no one.


## Psalms 69:21 (id: 1019069021)

21Instead, they gave me food that tasted like poison, and when I was thirsty, they gave me sour wine to drink.


## Psalms 69:22 (id: 1019069022)

22I hope their own food will kill them; I hope that this will happen when they think that they are completely safe.


## Psalms 69:23 (id: 1019069023)

23I hope that their eyes become dim so that they cannot see anything and that their backs will become weaker and weaker.


## Psalms 69:24 (id: 1019069024)

24Show them that you are very angry with them! Because of your great anger, chase them and catch them.


## Psalms 69:25 (id: 1019069025)

25Cause their towns to become abandoned; may there be no one to live in their tents.


## Psalms 69:26 (id: 1019069026)

26Do this because they persecute those whom you have punished, they look at how those whom you have punished suffer, and they tell others about it.


## Psalms 69:27 (id: 1019069027)

27Keep making a record of all their sins, do not fail to punish them for the evil things that they have done.


## Psalms 69:28 (id: 1019069028)

28Erase their names from the book containing the names of those who have eternal life; do not include them in the list of righteous people.


## Psalms 69:29 (id: 1019069029)

29As for me, I have pain and am suffering. O God, protect me and rescue me.


## Psalms 69:30 (id: 1019069030)

30When God does that, I will sing as I praise God, and I will honor him by thanking him.


## Psalms 69:31 (id: 1019069031)

31My doing that will please Yahweh more than sacrificing oxen, more than offering him full grown bulls.


## Psalms 69:32 (id: 1019069032)

32Oppressed people will see that God has rescued me, and they will be glad. I desire that all who request God to help them may be encouraged.


## Psalms 69:33 (id: 1019069033)

33Yahweh listens to those who are needy; he does not ignore those who have suffered for him.


## Psalms 69:34 (id: 1019069034)

34I desire that everything will praise God— everything that is in heaven and on earth and all the creatures that are in the seas.


## Psalms 69:35 (id: 1019069035)

35God will rescue the people of Jerusalem from their enemies, and he will rebuild the towns that are in Judah. His people will live there and again possess the land.


## Psalms 69:36 (id: 1019069036)

36The descendants of his people will inherit it, and those who love him will live there safely.


## Psalms 70:1 (id: 1019070001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director, asking God to help David. God, please save me! Yahweh, come quickly to help me!


## Psalms 70:2 (id: 1019070002)

2Disgrace those who are happy about my troubles, those who are trying to kill me. Chase them away; make everyone shame them, for they want to see me suffer.


## Psalms 70:3 (id: 1019070003)

3I hope that you will cause them to become dismayed and ashamed because they have been happy about my troubles.


## Psalms 70:4 (id: 1019070004)

4But I hope that everyone who prays to you will rejoice because of you. I hope that everyone who waits for you to rescue them will say, “God is great!”


## Psalms 70:5 (id: 1019070005)

5As for me, I am poor and needy; so God, come quickly to help me! Yahweh, you are the one who saves and helps me, so please come quickly!


## Psalms 71:1 (id: 1019071001)

1Yahweh, I have come to you to be safe; never allow me to become ashamed.


## Psalms 71:2 (id: 1019071002)

2Because you always do what is right, help me and rescue me; listen to me, and save me!


## Psalms 71:3 (id: 1019071003)

3Be like a huge rock on top of which I can be safe; be like a strong fortress in which I am safe. You have commanded your angels to rescue me.


## Psalms 71:4 (id: 1019071004)

4God, rescue me from wicked people, from the power of unjust and evil men.


## Psalms 71:5 (id: 1019071005)

5Yahweh, my Lord, you are the one whom I confidently expect to help me; I have trusted in you ever since I was young.


## Psalms 71:6 (id: 1019071006)

6I have depended on you all my life; you have taken care of me since the day that I was born, so I will always praise you.


## Psalms 71:7 (id: 1019071007)

7The manner in which you have rescued me has been an example to many people because they realize that you have been my strong defender.


## Psalms 71:8 (id: 1019071008)

8I praise you all during the day, and I proclaim that you are glorious.


## Psalms 71:9 (id: 1019071009)

9Now when I have become an old man, do not reject me; do not abandon me now when I am not strong anymore.


## Psalms 71:10 (id: 1019071010)

10My enemies say that they want to kill me; they talk together and plan how they can do that.


## Psalms 71:11 (id: 1019071011)

11They say, “God has abandoned him; so now we can pursue him and seize him because there is no one who will rescue him.”


## Psalms 71:12 (id: 1019071012)

12God, do not stay far away from me; hurry to help me!


## Psalms 71:13 (id: 1019071013)

13Cause those who accuse me to be defeated and destroyed; cause those who want to harm me to be shamed and disgraced.


## Psalms 71:14 (id: 1019071014)

14But as for me, I will continually and confidently expect you to do great things for me, and I will praise you more and more.


## Psalms 71:15 (id: 1019071015)

15I will tell people that you do what is right; all during the day I will tell people how you have saved me, although what you have done is more than I can fully understand.


## Psalms 71:16 (id: 1019071016)

16Yahweh, my Lord, I will praise you for your mighty deeds; I will proclaim that only you always act justly.


## Psalms 71:17 (id: 1019071017)

17God, you have taught me many things ever since I was young, and I still tell people about your wonderful deeds.


## Psalms 71:18 (id: 1019071018)

18Now, God, when I am old and my hair is gray, do not abandon me. Stay with me while I continue to proclaim to my children and grandchildren.


## Psalms 71:19 (id: 1019071019)

19God, you do many righteous deeds; it is as though they extend up to the sky. You have done great things; there is no one like you.


## Psalms 71:20 (id: 1019071020)

20You have caused us to have many troubles and to suffer much, but you will cause us to become strong again; when I am almost dead, you will keep us alive.


## Psalms 71:21 (id: 1019071021)

21You will cause me to be greatly honored, and you will encourage me again.


## Psalms 71:22 (id: 1019071022)

22I will also praise you while I play my harp; I will praise you, my God, for faithfully doing what you have promised to do. I will play hymns to praise you, the holy God whom we Israelites worship.


## Psalms 71:23 (id: 1019071023)

23I will shout joyfully while I sing; with my entire inner being I will sing because you have rescued me.


## Psalms 71:24 (id: 1019071024)

24All during the day I will tell people that you act righteously because those who wanted to harm me will have been defeated and disgraced.


## Psalms 72:1 (id: 1019072001)

1A psalm written by Solomon. O God, enable the king whom you appointed in Israel to rule justly. Show him how to judge matters fairly


## Psalms 72:2 (id: 1019072002)

2so that he may judge your people fairly and that he may govern your oppressed people justly.


## Psalms 72:3 (id: 1019072003)

3I desire that all over the country—even on the hills and mountains — people will live peacefully and righteously.


## Psalms 72:4 (id: 1019072004)

4Help your king to defend the poor people and to rescue needy people and to defeat those who oppress them.


## Psalms 72:5 (id: 1019072005)

5I desire that your king may live as long as the sun shines, as long as the moon shines, forever.


## Psalms 72:6 (id: 1019072006)

6I desire that his rule may be enjoyed by the people as they enjoy rain on the growing crops, as they enjoy the showers that fall on the land.


## Psalms 72:7 (id: 1019072007)

7I hope that people may live righteously during the years that he rules and that the people may live peacefully and prosperously as long as the moon shines.


## Psalms 72:8 (id: 1019072008)

8I hope that the king of Israel may rule the people in all the area from one sea in the east to another in the west and from the Euphrates River to the most remote places on earth.


## Psalms 72:9 (id: 1019072009)

9I hope that those who live in the wilderness may bow down before him and that his enemies may throw themselves on the ground in submission to our king.


## Psalms 72:10 (id: 1019072010)

10I hope that the king of the land of Tarshish and the kings of the islands in the sea may pay taxes to the king of Israel. I hope that the king of Sheba to the south and the king of Seba to the southwest may bring him gifts.


## Psalms 72:11 (id: 1019072011)

11I hope that all the other kings in the world may bow before the king of Israel and that people of all nations may serve our king.


## Psalms 72:12 (id: 1019072012)

12He rescues poor people when they cry out for help, and he helps those who are needy and those who have no one to help them.


## Psalms 72:13 (id: 1019072013)

13He pities those who are weak and needy; he saves the people’s lives.


## Psalms 72:14 (id: 1019072014)

14Our king rescues people from being oppressed and from being treated cruelly because their lives are precious to our king.


## Psalms 72:15 (id: 1019072015)

15I hope that our king may live a long time! I hope that he may be given gold from Sheba. I desire that people may always pray for our king and praise him all the time, every day.


## Psalms 72:16 (id: 1019072016)

16I hope that the fields may produce plenty of grain everywhere, even on the tops of the hills in the land where he rules, like the grain that grows on the hills in Lebanon. I hope that the cities in Israel will be as full of people as the fields are full of grass.


## Psalms 72:17 (id: 1019072017)

17I desire that the name of the king may never be forgotten. I hope that people may remember him as long as the sun shines. I hope that all people will praise Yahweh, the God of Israel, just as he has blessed the king of Israel.


## Psalms 72:18 (id: 1019072018)

18Praise Yahweh, the God whom we Israelites worship; he is the only one who does wonderful things.


## Psalms 72:19 (id: 1019072019)

19Praise him forever! I desire that his glory may fill the whole world! Amen! May it be so!


## Psalms 72:20 (id: 1019072020)

20This is the end of the prayers written by David, son of Jesse.


## Psalms 73:1 (id: 1019073001)

1A psalm written by Asaph; God truly is good to us Israelite people, to those who want to do what pleases God.


## Psalms 73:2 (id: 1019073002)

2As for me, I almost stopped trusting in God; I was almost guilty of committing a great sin against him,


## Psalms 73:3 (id: 1019073003)

3because I envied those who proudly acted as if they did not need God, when I realized that they prospered even though they were wicked.


## Psalms 73:4 (id: 1019073004)

4Those people do not suffer; they always have plenty of food to eat.


## Psalms 73:5 (id: 1019073005)

5They do not experience the difficult things that other people do; they do not experience catastrophes and sicknesses like other people.


## Psalms 73:6 (id: 1019073006)

6So they are proud and violent. Their being prideful is like a necklace that they show off to others, and they openly display their violent actions like people openly display the clothes they wear.


## Psalms 73:7 (id: 1019073007)

7Their eyes protrude because their faces are fat, and they are always thinking about more evil things to do.


## Psalms 73:8 (id: 1019073008)

8They scoff at other people, and wickedly talk about doing unjust things to them; they speak pridefully.


## Psalms 73:9 (id: 1019073009)

9They exalt themselves and talk as if they are God in heaven, and they go about the earth talking boastfully.


## Psalms 73:10 (id: 1019073010)

10The result is that people pay attention to them and listen to everything they say.


## Psalms 73:11 (id: 1019073011)

11Wicked people say to themselves, “God certainly does not care what we do; the Most High certainly will not judge us for what we do!”


## Psalms 73:12 (id: 1019073012)

12Look at how these wicked people live; their lives are so easy that they never have to worry about anything, and they are always becoming richer.


## Psalms 73:13 (id: 1019073013)

13{When I saw this I thought that} certainly it is useless that I have thought about things that are pleasing to you, and have not sinned.


## Psalms 73:14 (id: 1019073014)

14Every day I suffer, and every morning you punish me.


## Psalms 73:15 (id: 1019073015)

15If I had said these things out loud in front of others, Surely, I would have been sinning against your people.


## Psalms 73:16 (id: 1019073016)

16When I tried to think about all this, it was very difficult for me to understand it.


## Psalms 73:17 (id: 1019073017)

17But when I went to the temple where people worship God, then I understood what will happen to wicked people in the future.


## Psalms 73:18 (id: 1019073018)

18I know that you make their future insecure, you will cause them to be ruined.


## Psalms 73:19 (id: 1019073019)

19God will suddenly destroy these wicked people; they will die in terrible ways.


## Psalms 73:20 (id: 1019073020)

20Lord, when you act, you will cause the wicked to quickly vanish; they will vanish like a dream which disappears as soon as a person awakes from their sleep.


## Psalms 73:21 (id: 1019073021)

21When I was grieved in my inner being, and felt emotionally hurt,


## Psalms 73:22 (id: 1019073022)

22I was stupid and ignorant; I behaved like an animal toward you.


## Psalms 73:23 (id: 1019073023)

23Nevertheless I am always with you; you constantly stay close to me.


## Psalms 73:24 (id: 1019073024)

24You lead me by instructing me, and when I die, you will take me into your glorious presence.


## Psalms 73:25 (id: 1019073025)

25You are the only one I have in heaven! There is nothing on this earth that I desire more than you.


## Psalms 73:26 (id: 1019073026)

26My body and my spirit may become very weak, but God enables me to feel encouraged; He is all I need.


## Psalms 73:27 (id: 1019073027)

27People who abandon you will perish; you will ruin every person who is not loyal to you.


## Psalms 73:28 (id: 1019073028)

28But for me, the only thing I need is to be close to God. I trust in the Lord Yahweh to keep me safe, so that I may tell others everything you have done for me.


## Psalms 74:1 (id: 1019074001)

1A psalm written by Asaph; God, it feels like you have abandoned us permanently! I do not understand why you are so angry with us, since we are like sheep in your pasture {and you are like our shepherd}!


## Psalms 74:2 (id: 1019074002)

2Do not forget your people whom you chose long ago, the people whom you freed {from being slaves in Egypt} and caused to become your tribe. {Do not forget} Jerusalem, which was where you dwelt {on earth}.


## Psalms 74:3 (id: 1019074003)

3Hurry, come and see everything that has been ruined for so long; our enemies have destroyed everything in the Temple.


## Psalms 74:4 (id: 1019074004)

4Your enemies have shouted triumphantly in your sacred place; they erected their banners to show they had defeated us.


## Psalms 74:5 (id: 1019074005)

5They chopped down all the woodwork in the Temple, like woodsmen cut down trees in a forest with their axes.


## Psalms 74:6 (id: 1019074006)

6They tore down all the carved wood with their axes and hammers.


## Psalms 74:7 (id: 1019074007)

7Then they burned your temple to the ground; they defiled the place where you dwelled on earth.


## Psalms 74:8 (id: 1019074008)

8They said to themselves, “We will subdue the Israelites completely.” They have burned down all the other places throughout the land of Israel where people gathered to worship you.


## Psalms 74:9 (id: 1019074009)

9We no longer see any signs from God’s prophets; there are no prophets any more, and no one among us knows how long this situation will continue.


## Psalms 74:10 (id: 1019074010)

10God, how long will our enemies make fun of you? Will they insult you forever?


## Psalms 74:11 (id: 1019074011)

11Why, even though you are powerful, do you refuse to help us? Please stop refusing to help us and come and rescue us by destroying our enemies.


## Psalms 74:12 (id: 1019074012)

12But still God, you are our king since long ago; and you have rescued us from our enemies here on earth.


## Psalms 74:13 (id: 1019074013)

13By your power you caused the sea to divide; it was as though you had smashed the heads of the rulers of Egypt who were like huge sea dragons.


## Psalms 74:14 (id: 1019074014)

14It was as though you crushed the head of the king of Egypt and gave his body to the animals in the desert to eat.


## Psalms 74:15 (id: 1019074015)

15You caused springs and streams to flow, and you also dried up rivers that had never dried up previously.


## Psalms 74:16 (id: 1019074016)

16You created the days and the nights, and you put the sun and the moon in their places.


## Psalms 74:17 (id: 1019074017)

17You determined where the oceans end and the land begins, and you created the summer season and the winter season.


## Psalms 74:18 (id: 1019074018)

18Yahweh, do not forget that your enemies laugh at you and that it is foolish people who despise you.


## Psalms 74:19 (id: 1019074019)

19Do not abandon your helpless people into the hands of their cruel enemies; do not forget your suffering people.


## Psalms 74:20 (id: 1019074020)

20Continue thinking about the covenant that you made with us; remember that there are violent people in every dark place on the earth.


## Psalms 74:21 (id: 1019074021)

21Do not allow your oppressed people to be disgraced; help those poor and needy people in order that they will again praise you.


## Psalms 74:22 (id: 1019074022)

22God, arise and defend yourself by defending your people! Do not forget that foolish people laugh at you all during the day!


## Psalms 74:23 (id: 1019074023)

23Do not forget that your enemies shout angrily at you; the uproar that they make while they oppose you never stops.


## Psalms 75:1 (id: 1019075001)

1A psalm written by Asaph for the choir director, to be sung using the tune ‘Do not destroy’ We give thanks to you; our God, we thank you. You are close to us, and we proclaim to others the wonderful things that you have done for us.


## Psalms 75:2 (id: 1019075002)

2You have said, “I have appointed a time when I will judge people, and I will judge everyone fairly.


## Psalms 75:3 (id: 1019075003)

3When the earth shakes and all the creatures on the earth tremble, I am the one who will keep its foundations steady.


## Psalms 75:4 (id: 1019075004)

4I say to people who boast, ‘Stop bragging!’ and I say to wicked people, ‘Do not proudly do things to show how great you are!’”


## Psalms 75:5 (id: 1019075005)

5Do not be arrogant, and do not speak so boastfully!


## Psalms 75:6 (id: 1019075006)

6The one who judges people does not come from the east or from the west, and he does not come from the desert.


## Psalms 75:7 (id: 1019075007)

7God is the one who judges people; he shames and punishes some, and he honors others.


## Psalms 75:8 (id: 1019075008)

8It is as though Yahweh held a cup in his hand; it is filled with wine that has spices mixed in it to cause those who drink it to become more drunk; and when Yahweh pours it out, he will force all the wicked people to drink it; they will drink every drop of it; yes, he will punish them fully.


## Psalms 75:9 (id: 1019075009)

9But as for me, I will never stop saying what the God whom Jacob worshiped has done; I will never stop singing to praise him.


## Psalms 75:10 (id: 1019075010)

10He promises this: “I will destroy the power of wicked people, but I will increase the power of righteous people.”


## Psalms 76:1 (id: 1019076001)

1A psalm written by Asaph for the choir director, to be accompanied by stringed instruments; God has made the people in Judah to know him; the Israelite people honor him.


## Psalms 76:2 (id: 1019076002)

2In Jerusalem is where he resides; he lives on Mount Zion.


## Psalms 76:3 (id: 1019076003)

3There he broke the flaming arrows that his enemies shot, and he also broke their shields and swords and other weapons that they used in battles.


## Psalms 76:4 (id: 1019076004)

4God, you are powerful! You are like a great king as you return from the mountains where you defeated your enemies.


## Psalms 76:5 (id: 1019076005)

5Their brave soldiers were killed, and then those who killed them took away everything that those soldiers had. Those enemies died; indeed, none of them were able to fight any longer.


## Psalms 76:6 (id: 1019076006)

6When you, the God whom Jacob worshiped, rebuked your enemies, their horses and their riders fell down dead.


## Psalms 76:7 (id: 1019076007)

7Truly, you cause everyone to be afraid. When you are angry and you punish people, no one can endure it.


## Psalms 76:8 (id: 1019076008)

8From heaven you proclaimed that you would judge people, and then everyone on the earth was afraid and did not say anything more


## Psalms 76:9 (id: 1019076009)

9when you arose to declare that you would punish wicked people and rescue all those whom they had oppressed.


## Psalms 76:10 (id: 1019076010)

10When you punish those with whom you are angry, your people will praise you, and your enemies who survive will worship you on your festival days.


## Psalms 76:11 (id: 1019076011)

11So give to Yahweh the offerings that you promised to give to him; all the people of nearby people groups should also bring gifts to him, the one who is awesome.


## Psalms 76:12 (id: 1019076012)

12He humbles the leaders, and terrifies all the kings.


## Psalms 77:1 (id: 1019077001)

1A psalm written by Asaph for Jeduthun, the choir director; I will cry out to God; I will cry aloud to him, and he will listen to me.


## Psalms 77:2 (id: 1019077002)

2At the time that I had trouble, I prayed to the Lord; all during the night I lifted up my hands while I prayed, but nothing could comfort me.


## Psalms 77:3 (id: 1019077003)

3When I thought about God, I despaired; when I meditated about him, I grew discouraged.


## Psalms 77:4 (id: 1019077004)

4All during the night he prevented me from sleeping; I was so worried that I did not know what to say.


## Psalms 77:5 (id: 1019077005)

5I thought about days that had passed; I remembered what had happened in previous years.


## Psalms 77:6 (id: 1019077006)

6I spent all the night thinking about things; I meditated, and this is what I asked myself:


## Psalms 77:7 (id: 1019077007)

7“Will the Lord always reject me? Will he never again be pleased with me?


## Psalms 77:8 (id: 1019077008)

8Has he stopped faithfully loving me? Will he not do for me what he promised to do?


## Psalms 77:9 (id: 1019077009)

9God promised to act mercifully toward me; has he forgotten that? Because he is angry with me, has he decided not to be kind to me?”


## Psalms 77:10 (id: 1019077010)

10I said, “What causes me to be sad the most is that it seems that God, who is greater than any other god, is no longer using his power for us.”


## Psalms 77:11 (id: 1019077011)

11But then, Yahweh, I recall your great deeds; I remember the wonderful things that you did in the past.


## Psalms 77:12 (id: 1019077012)

12I meditate on all that you have done, and I think about your mighty acts.


## Psalms 77:13 (id: 1019077013)

13God, everything that you do is amazing; there is certainly no god who is great like you are!


## Psalms 77:14 (id: 1019077014)

14You are God, the one who performs miracles; you showed to the people of many people groups that you are powerful.


## Psalms 77:15 (id: 1019077015)

15By your power you rescued your people from Egypt; you saved those who were descendants of Jacob and his son Joseph.


## Psalms 77:16 (id: 1019077016)

16It was as though the waters saw you and became very afraid, and even the deepest part of the water shook.


## Psalms 77:17 (id: 1019077017)

17Rain poured down from the clouds; it thundered very loudly, and lightning flashed in all directions.


## Psalms 77:18 (id: 1019077018)

18Thunder crashed in the whirlwind—your voice! Lightning lit up, and the earth shook violently.


## Psalms 77:19 (id: 1019077019)

19Then you walked through the sea in a path that you made through the deep water, but your footprints could not be seen.


## Psalms 77:20 (id: 1019077020)

20You led your people as a shepherd leads his flock of sheep while Moses and Aaron were the leaders of your people.


## Psalms 78:1 (id: 1019078001)

1A psalm written by Asaph; My friends, listen to what I am going to teach you; pay careful attention to what I will say.


## Psalms 78:2 (id: 1019078002)

2I am going to give you some sayings that wise people have said. They will be sayings about things that happened long ago, things that were difficult to understand.


## Psalms 78:3 (id: 1019078003)

3These are things that we have heard and known previously, things that our parents and grandparents told us.


## Psalms 78:4 (id: 1019078004)

4We will tell these things to our children, but we will also tell our grandchildren about Yahweh’s power and the glorious things that he has done.


## Psalms 78:5 (id: 1019078005)

5He gave laws and commandments to the Israelite people, those who are the descendants of Jacob, and he told our ancestors to teach them to their children.


## Psalms 78:6 (id: 1019078006)

6He commanded this so that their children would also know them and so that they would teach them to their own children.


## Psalms 78:7 (id: 1019078007)

7In that way, they also would trust in God and would not forget the things that he has done; instead, they would obey his commandments.


## Psalms 78:8 (id: 1019078008)

8They would not be like their ancestors, who were very stubborn and kept rebelling against God; they did not continue firmly trusting in God, and they did not worship him alone.


## Psalms 78:9 (id: 1019078009)

9The soldiers of the tribe of Ephraim had bows and arrows, but they ran away from their enemies on the day that they fought with their enemies.


## Psalms 78:10 (id: 1019078010)

10They did not do what they had agreed with God that they would do; they refused to obey his laws.


## Psalms 78:11 (id: 1019078011)

11They forgot what he had done; they forgot about the miracles that they had seen him perform.


## Psalms 78:12 (id: 1019078012)

12While our ancestors were watching, God performed miracles in the area around the city of Zoan in Egypt.


## Psalms 78:13 (id: 1019078013)

13Then he caused the Sea of Reeds to divide, causing the water on each side to pile up like a wall, with the result that our ancestors walked through it on dry ground.


## Psalms 78:14 (id: 1019078014)

14He led them by a bright cloud during the day and by a fiery light during the night.


## Psalms 78:15 (id: 1019078015)

15He split rocks open in the wilderness and gave to our ancestors plenty of water from deep inside the earth.


## Psalms 78:16 (id: 1019078016)

16He caused a stream of water to flow from the rock; the water flowed like a river.


## Psalms 78:17 (id: 1019078017)

17But our ancestors continued to sin against God; in the wilderness they rebelled against the one who is greater than any other god.


## Psalms 78:18 (id: 1019078018)

18By demanding that God give them the food that they desired, they tried to find out if he would always do what they requested him to do.


## Psalms 78:19 (id: 1019078019)

19They insulted God by saying, “Can God supply food for us here in this desert?


## Psalms 78:20 (id: 1019078020)

20It is true that he struck the rock, with the result that water gushed out, but can he also provide bread and meat for us, his people?”


## Psalms 78:21 (id: 1019078021)

21So when Yahweh heard that, he became very angry, and he sent a fire to burn up some of his Israelite people.


## Psalms 78:22 (id: 1019078022)

22He did that because they did not trust in him, and they did not believe that he would rescue them.


## Psalms 78:23 (id: 1019078023)

23But God spoke to the sky above them and commanded it to open like a door,


## Psalms 78:24 (id: 1019078024)

24and then food fell down like rain, food that they named “manna.” God gave them grain from heaven.


## Psalms 78:25 (id: 1019078025)

25So the people ate the food that angels eat, and God gave to them all the manna that they wanted.


## Psalms 78:26 (id: 1019078026)

26Later, he caused the wind to blow from the east, and by his power he also sent wind from the south,


## Psalms 78:27 (id: 1019078027)

27and the wind brought birds which were as numerous as the grains of sand on the seashore.


## Psalms 78:28 (id: 1019078028)

28God caused those birds to fall in the middle of their camp. There were birds all around their tents.


## Psalms 78:29 (id: 1019078029)

29So the people cooked the birds and ate the meat; their stomachs were full because God had given them what they wanted.


## Psalms 78:30 (id: 1019078030)

30But they had not yet eaten all that they wanted.


## Psalms 78:31 (id: 1019078031)

31At that point, God was still very angry with them, and he caused their strongest men to die; he got rid of many of the finest young Israelite men.


## Psalms 78:32 (id: 1019078032)

32In spite of all this, the people continued to sin; in spite of all the miracles that God had performed, they still did not trust that he would take care of them.


## Psalms 78:33 (id: 1019078033)

33So he made them terrified all their lives; he made them die young.


## Psalms 78:34 (id: 1019078034)

34Whenever God caused some of the Israelites to die, the others would repent; they would be sorry and seriously ask God to save them.


## Psalms 78:35 (id: 1019078035)

35They would remember that God was like a huge rock on which they would be safe, and that he, who was greater than any other god, was the one who protected them.


## Psalms 78:36 (id: 1019078036)

36But they tried to deceive God by what they said; their words were all lies.


## Psalms 78:37 (id: 1019078037)

37They were not loyal to him; they ignored the covenant that he had made with them.


## Psalms 78:38 (id: 1019078038)

38But God acted mercifully toward his people. He forgave them for having sinned and did not get rid of them. Many times he refrained from becoming angry with them and restrained himself from furiously punishing them.


## Psalms 78:39 (id: 1019078039)

39He remembered that they were only humans who die, humans who disappear as quickly as a wind that blows by and then is gone.


## Psalms 78:40 (id: 1019078040)

40Many times our ancestors rebelled against God in the wilderness and made him very sad.


## Psalms 78:41 (id: 1019078041)

41Many times they did evil things to find out if they could do those things without God punishing them. They frequently caused the holy God of Israel to become angry.


## Psalms 78:42 (id: 1019078042)

42They forgot about his great power, and they forgot about the time when he rescued them from their enemies.


## Psalms 78:43 (id: 1019078043)

43They forgot about when he performed many miracles in the area near the city of Zoan in Egypt.


## Psalms 78:44 (id: 1019078044)

44He caused the Nile River to become red like blood so that the people of Egypt had no water to drink.


## Psalms 78:45 (id: 1019078045)

45He sent among the people of Egypt swarms of flies that bit them, and he sent frogs that ate up everything.


## Psalms 78:46 (id: 1019078046)

46He sent locusts to eat their crops and the other things that grew in their fields.


## Psalms 78:47 (id: 1019078047)

47He sent hail that destroyed the grapevines, and he sent more hail that ruined the figs on the sycamore trees.


## Psalms 78:48 (id: 1019078048)

48He sent hail that killed their cattle and lightning that killed their sheep and cows.


## Psalms 78:49 (id: 1019078049)

49Because God was fiercely angry with the people of Egypt, he caused them to be very distressed. The disasters that struck them were like a group of angels that destroyed everything.


## Psalms 78:50 (id: 1019078050)

50He did not lessen his anger with them, and he did not spare their lives; he sent a plague that killed many of them.


## Psalms 78:51 (id: 1019078051)

51In that plague he caused all the firstborn sons of the people of Egypt to die.


## Psalms 78:52 (id: 1019078052)

52Then he led his people out of Egypt as a shepherd leads his sheep, and he guided them while they walked through the wilderness.


## Psalms 78:53 (id: 1019078053)

53He led them safely, and they were not afraid, but their enemies were drowned in the sea.


## Psalms 78:54 (id: 1019078054)

54Later he brought them to Canaan, his sacred land, to Mount Zion, and by his power he enabled them to conquer the people who were living there.


## Psalms 78:55 (id: 1019078055)

55He expelled the people groups while his people were advancing; he assigned part of the land for each tribe to possess, and he gave the houses of those people to the Israelites.


## Psalms 78:56 (id: 1019078056)

56However, the Israelites rebelled against God, who is greater than any other God, and they did many evil things to see if they could do those things without God punishing them; they did not obey his commandments.


## Psalms 78:57 (id: 1019078057)

57Instead, as their ancestors did, they rebelled against God and were not loyal to him; they were as unreliable as a bow that breaks when you try to shoot with it.


## Psalms 78:58 (id: 1019078058)

58Because they worshiped carved images of their gods on the tops of hills, they caused God to become angry.


## Psalms 78:59 (id: 1019078059)

59He saw what they were doing and became very angry, so he rejected the Israelite people.


## Psalms 78:60 (id: 1019078060)

60He no longer appeared to them at Shiloh in the sacred tent where he had lived among them.


## Psalms 78:61 (id: 1019078061)

61He allowed their enemies to capture the sacred chest, which was the symbol of his power and his glory.


## Psalms 78:62 (id: 1019078062)

62Because he was angry with his people, he allowed their enemies to kill them.


## Psalms 78:63 (id: 1019078063)

63Young men were killed in battles, with the result that the young women had no one to marry.


## Psalms 78:64 (id: 1019078064)

64Many priests were killed by their enemies’ swords, and the people did not allow the priests’ widows to mourn.


## Psalms 78:65 (id: 1019078065)

65Later, it was as though the Lord awoke from sleeping; he was like a strong man who became angry because he drank a lot of wine.


## Psalms 78:66 (id: 1019078066)

66He pushed his enemies back and caused them to be very ashamed for a long time because they had been defeated.


## Psalms 78:67 (id: 1019078067)

67But he did not set up his tent where the people of the tribe of Ephraim lived; he did not choose their area to do that.


## Psalms 78:68 (id: 1019078068)

68Instead he chose the area where the tribe of Judah lived; he chose Mount Zion, which he loves.


## Psalms 78:69 (id: 1019078069)

69He decided to have his temple built there, high up, like his home in heaven; he caused it to be firm, like the earth, and intended that his temple would last forever.


## Psalms 78:70 (id: 1019078070)

70He chose David, who served him faithfully, and took him from the pastures


## Psalms 78:71 (id: 1019078071)

71where he was taking care of his father’s sheep, and appointed him to be the leader of the Israelites, the people who would always belong to God.


## Psalms 78:72 (id: 1019078072)

72David took care of the Israelite people sincerely and wholeheartedly, and he guided them skillfully.


## Psalms 79:1 (id: 1019079001)

1A psalm written by Asaph; God, other people groups have invaded your own land. They have desecrated your temple, and they have destroyed all the buildings in Jerusalem.


## Psalms 79:2 (id: 1019079002)

2Instead of burying the corpses of your people whom they killed, they allowed the vultures to eat the flesh of those corpses, and they also allowed wild animals to eat the corpses of your people.


## Psalms 79:3 (id: 1019079003)

3When they killed your people, your people’s blood flowed like water through the streets of Jerusalem, and there was almost no one left to bury their corpses.


## Psalms 79:4 (id: 1019079004)

4The people groups that live in countries that surround our land insult us; they laugh at us and mock us.


## Psalms 79:5 (id: 1019079005)

5Yahweh, how long will this continue? Will you be angry with us forever? Will your anger be like a fire burning within you?


## Psalms 79:6 (id: 1019079006)

6Instead of being angry with us, be angry with the people groups that do not know you! Be angry with kingdoms whose people do not pray to you


## Psalms 79:7 (id: 1019079007)

7because they have killed Israelite people and they have ruined your country.


## Psalms 79:8 (id: 1019079008)

8Do not punish us because of the sins that our ancestors committed! Act mercifully toward us now because we are very discouraged.


## Psalms 79:9 (id: 1019079009)

9God, you have saved us many times, so help us now; rescue us and forgive us for having sinned so that other people will honor you.


## Psalms 79:10 (id: 1019079010)

10It is not right that the other people groups say about us, “If their God is very powerful, why does he not help them?” Allow us to see you punishing the people of other nations in return for their shedding our blood and killing many of us, your people.


## Psalms 79:11 (id: 1019079011)

11Listen to your people groaning while they are in prison, and by your great power, free those whom our enemies say they will certainly execute.


## Psalms 79:12 (id: 1019079012)

12In return for their having often insulted you, punish them seven times as much!


## Psalms 79:13 (id: 1019079013)

13After you do that, we, whom you take care of as a shepherd takes care of his sheep, will continue praising you; we will continue to praise you from generation to generation forever.


## Psalms 80:1 (id: 1019080001)

1A psalm written by Asaph for the choir director, to be sung using the tune ‘Lilies of the covenant’ Yahweh, you who lead us as a shepherd leads his flock of sheep, you who sit on your throne in the Very Holy Place in the temple, above the figures of winged creatures, come and do powerful things for us Israelite people.


## Psalms 80:2 (id: 1019080002)

2Show yourself to the people of the tribes of Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh! Show us that you are powerful and come and rescue us!


## Psalms 80:3 (id: 1019080003)

3God, cause our nation to be strong like it was before; act kindly toward us so that we may be saved from our enemies!


## Psalms 80:4 (id: 1019080004)

4Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, how long will you be angry with us, your people, when we pray to you?


## Psalms 80:5 (id: 1019080005)

5It is as though the only food and drink that you have given us is a cup full of our tears!


## Psalms 80:6 (id: 1019080006)

6You have allowed the people groups that surround us to argue with each other to decide which part of our land each of them will take; they laugh at us.


## Psalms 80:7 (id: 1019080007)

7God, Commander of the angel armies, make our nation strong as it was before! Act kindly toward us so that we may be saved!


## Psalms 80:8 (id: 1019080008)

8Our ancestors were like a grapevine that you brought out of Egypt; you drove out the other people groups from this land, and you put your people in their land.


## Psalms 80:9 (id: 1019080009)

9As people clear ground to plant a grapevine, you cleared out the people who were living in this land for us to live in it. As the roots of a grapevine go deep down into the ground and spread, you enabled our ancestors to prosper and start living in towns all over this land.


## Psalms 80:10 (id: 1019080010)

10As huge grapevines cover the hills with their shade and as their branches are taller than big cedar trees,


## Psalms 80:11 (id: 1019080011)

11your people ruled all of Canaan, from the Mediterranean Sea in the west to the Euphrates River in the east.


## Psalms 80:12 (id: 1019080012)

12So why have you abandoned us and allowed our enemies to tear down our walls? You are like someone who tears down the fences around his vineyard, so that all the people who pass by can steal the grapes;


## Psalms 80:13 (id: 1019080013)

13wild pigs can trample the vines, and wild animals can also eat the grapes.


## Psalms 80:14 (id: 1019080014)

14You who are the commander of the angel armies, turn to us! Look down from heaven and see what is happening to us! Come and rescue us who are like your grapevine,


## Psalms 80:15 (id: 1019080015)

15who are like the young vine that you planted and caused to grow!


## Psalms 80:16 (id: 1019080016)

16Our enemies have torn down and burned everything in our land; look at them angrily and get rid of them!


## Psalms 80:17 (id: 1019080017)

17But strengthen us people whom you have chosen, us Israelite people, whom you previously caused to be very strong.


## Psalms 80:18 (id: 1019080018)

18When you do that, we will never turn away from you again; revive us, and then we will praise you.


## Psalms 80:19 (id: 1019080019)

19Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, restore us; act kindly toward us and rescue us from our enemies!


## Psalms 81:1 (id: 1019081001)

1A psalm written by Asaph for the choir director; Sing songs to praise God, who enables us to be strong when we fight our enemies; shout joyfully to God, whom we descendants of Jacob worship!


## Psalms 81:2 (id: 1019081002)

2Start playing the music, and beat the tambourines; play nice music on the harps and lyres.


## Psalms 81:3 (id: 1019081003)

3Blow the trumpets during the festival to celebrate each new moon, each time the moon is full, and during our other festivals.


## Psalms 81:4 (id: 1019081004)

4Do that because that is a decree for us Israelite people; it is a command that God made for the descendants of Jacob.


## Psalms 81:5 (id: 1019081005)

5He made it a law at the time when God led the descendants of Joseph out of the land of Egypt. I heard a voice I did not recognize, and it said:


## Psalms 81:6 (id: 1019081006)

6“After the rulers of Egypt forced you Israelites to work as slaves, I took those heavy burdens off your backs, and I enabled you to lay down those heavy baskets of bricks that you were carrying.


## Psalms 81:7 (id: 1019081007)

7When you were greatly distressed, you called out to me, and I rescued you; I answered you out of a thundercloud. Later I tested whether you would trust me to give you water when you were in the desert at Meribah.


## Psalms 81:8 (id: 1019081008)

8You who are my people, listen while I warn you! I wish that you Israelite people would pay attention to what I say to you!


## Psalms 81:9 (id: 1019081009)

9You must not have any idols of other gods among you; you must never bow to worship any of them!


## Psalms 81:10 (id: 1019081010)

10I am Yahweh, your God; It was not any of those gods who brought you out of Egypt; I am the one who did it! So request what you want me to do for you, and I will do it.


## Psalms 81:11 (id: 1019081011)

11But my people would not listen to me; they would not obey me.


## Psalms 81:12 (id: 1019081012)

12So because they were very stubborn, I allowed them to do whatever they wanted to do.


## Psalms 81:13 (id: 1019081013)

13I wish that my people would listen to me, that the Israelite people would behave as I want them to do.


## Psalms 81:14 (id: 1019081014)

14If they did that, I would quickly defeat their enemies; I would strike dead those who are oppressing them.


## Psalms 81:15 (id: 1019081015)

15Then all those who hate me would cringe before me, and then I would punish them forever.


## Psalms 81:16 (id: 1019081016)

16But I would give you Israelites very good wheat, and I would fill your stomachs with wild honey.”


## Psalms 82:1 (id: 1019082001)

1A psalm written by Asaph; God stands in heaven in a meeting of all the spirits whom he has placed in charge of what he created. He tells them that he has decided this:


## Psalms 82:2 (id: 1019082002)

2“You must stop judging people unfairly; you must no longer make decisions that favor wicked people!


## Psalms 82:3 (id: 1019082003)

3You must defend people who are poor and orphans; you must act fairly toward those who are needy and those who have no one to help them.


## Psalms 82:4 (id: 1019082004)

4Rescue them from the power of the wicked people!”


## Psalms 82:5 (id: 1019082005)

5Those rulers do not know or understand anything! They are very corrupt, and as a result of their corrupt behavior, it is as though the foundation of the world is being shaken!


## Psalms 82:6 (id: 1019082006)

6I previously said to them, “You think you are gods! It is as though you are all my sons,


## Psalms 82:7 (id: 1019082007)

7but you will die as people do; your lives will end as the lives of all rulers end.”


## Psalms 82:8 (id: 1019082008)

8God, arise and judge everyone on the earth because all the people groups belong to you!


## Psalms 83:1 (id: 1019083001)

1A psalm which is a song written by Asaph; God, do not continue to be silent! Do not be quiet and say nothing


## Psalms 83:2 (id: 1019083002)

2because your enemies are rioting against you; those who hate you are rebelling against you!


## Psalms 83:3 (id: 1019083003)

3They are secretly planning to do things to harm us, your people; they are conspiring together against the people whom you protect.


## Psalms 83:4 (id: 1019083004)

4They say, “Come, we must destroy their nation so that no one will remember that Israel ever existed!”


## Psalms 83:5 (id: 1019083005)

5They have agreed on what they want to do to destroy Israel, and they have agreed to attack you together.


## Psalms 83:6 (id: 1019083006)

6Your enemies are the people who live in the tents of Edom— the Ishmaelites, Moab and the Hagrites, they conspire together with


## Psalms 83:7 (id: 1019083007)

7the people of Gebal, and the Ammonites, and the Amalekites, and the Philistines, and the people of the city of Tyre.


## Psalms 83:8 (id: 1019083008)

8The people of Assyria have joined them; they are strong allies of the Moab and Ammon people groups, who are descendants of Abraham’s nephew Lot.


## Psalms 83:9 (id: 1019083009)

9God, do to those people things as you did to the Midian people group, as you did to Sisera and Jabin at the river Kishon.


## Psalms 83:10 (id: 1019083010)

10You destroyed them at the town of Endor, and their corpses lay on the ground and decayed.


## Psalms 83:11 (id: 1019083011)

11Do to them things like you did to kings Oreb and Zeeb; defeat their leaders like you defeated Zebah and Zalmunna,


## Psalms 83:12 (id: 1019083012)

12who said, “We will take for ourselves the land that the Israelites say belongs to God!”


## Psalms 83:13 (id: 1019083013)

13My God, cause them to disappear quickly like whirling dust, like chaff that the wind blows away!


## Psalms 83:14 (id: 1019083014)

14As a fire completely burns a forest and as flames burn in the mountains,


## Psalms 83:15 (id: 1019083015)

15expel them with your storms and cause them to be terrified by your big storms!


## Psalms 83:16 (id: 1019083016)

16Cause them to be very ashamed so that they will admit that you are very powerful.


## Psalms 83:17 (id: 1019083017)

17Cause them to be forever disgraced because of being defeated, and cause them to die while they are still disgraced.


## Psalms 83:18 (id: 1019083018)

18Cause them to know that you, whose name is Yahweh, are the supreme ruler over everything on the earth.


## Psalms 84:1 (id: 1019084001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director; Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, your temple is very beautiful!


## Psalms 84:2 (id: 1019084002)

2I would like to be there; Yahweh, I desire that very much. With all my inner being I sing joyfully to you, the all\-powerful God.


## Psalms 84:3 (id: 1019084003)

3Even sparrows and swallows have built nests near your temple; they take care of their young babies near the altars where people offer sacrifices to you, Commander of the angel armies, my king and my God.


## Psalms 84:4 (id: 1019084004)

4How fortunate are those who are always in your temple, constantly singing to praise you.


## Psalms 84:5 (id: 1019084005)

5How fortunate are those whom you make strong, those who desire very much to make the trip up to Mount Zion.


## Psalms 84:6 (id: 1019084006)

6While they travel through the dryValley of Tears, you cause it to become a place where there are springs of water, where the rains in the autumn fill the valley with water, a blessing from you.


## Psalms 84:7 (id: 1019084007)

7As a result, those who travel through there become stronger knowing that they will appear in your presence on Mount Zion.


## Psalms 84:8 (id: 1019084008)

8Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, listen to my prayer; God, whom we descendants of Jacob worship, hear what I am saying!


## Psalms 84:9 (id: 1019084009)

9God, act kindly toward our king, the one who protects us, the one whom you have chosen to rule us.


## Psalms 84:10 (id: 1019084010)

10For me, spending one day in your temple is better than spending a thousand days somewhere else; standing at the entrance to your temple, ready to go inside, is better than living in the tents where wicked people live.


## Psalms 84:11 (id: 1019084011)

11Yahweh our God is like the sun that shines on us and like a shield that protects us; he acts favorably toward us and honors us. Yahweh does not refuse to give any good thing to those who do what is right.


## Psalms 84:12 (id: 1019084012)

12Yahweh, commander of the angel armies, how fortunate are those who trust in you!


## Psalms 85:1 (id: 1019085001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah for the choir director; Yahweh, you have acted kindly toward us people who live in this land; you have enabled us Israelite people to become prosperous again.


## Psalms 85:2 (id: 1019085002)

2You forgave us, your people, for the sins that we had committed; you pardoned us for all our sins.


## Psalms 85:3 (id: 1019085003)

3You stopped being angry with us and turned away from severely punishing us.


## Psalms 85:4 (id: 1019085004)

4Now, God, the only one who can save us, stop being angry with us and help us.


## Psalms 85:5 (id: 1019085005)

5Will you continue to be angry with us forever?


## Psalms 85:6 (id: 1019085006)

6Please enable us to prosper again so that we, your people, will rejoice about what you have done for us.


## Psalms 85:7 (id: 1019085007)

7Yahweh, by rescuing us from our troubles, show us that you faithfully love us.


## Psalms 85:8 (id: 1019085008)

8I want to listen to what Yahweh our God says because he promises that he will enable us, his people, to live peacefully if we do not return to doing foolish things.


## Psalms 85:9 (id: 1019085009)

9He is surely ready to save those who have an awesome respect for him, so that his glory will remain in our land.


## Psalms 85:10 (id: 1019085010)

10When that happens, he will both faithfully love us and faithfully do for us what he promised to do; we will act righteously, and he will give us peace, which will be like a kiss that he gives us.


## Psalms 85:11 (id: 1019085011)

11Here on earth, we will be loyal to God, and from heaven, God will act justly toward us.


## Psalms 85:12 (id: 1019085012)

12Yes, Yahweh will do good things for us, and there will be great harvests in our land.


## Psalms 85:13 (id: 1019085013)

13Yahweh always acts righteously; he acts righteously wherever he goes.


## Psalms 86:1 (id: 1019086001)

1A prayer written by David; Yahweh, listen to what I say and answer me because I am weak and needy.


## Psalms 86:2 (id: 1019086002)

2Prevent me from dying now because I am loyal to you; save me because I serve you and I trust in you, my God.


## Psalms 86:3 (id: 1019086003)

3Lord, act kindly toward me because I cry out to you all during each day.


## Psalms 86:4 (id: 1019086004)

4Lord, cause me to be glad, because I pray to you.


## Psalms 86:5 (id: 1019086005)

5Lord, you are good to us, and you forgive us; you faithfully love very much all those who pray to you.


## Psalms 86:6 (id: 1019086006)

6Yahweh, listen to my prayer; hear me when I cry out to you to help me.


## Psalms 86:7 (id: 1019086007)

7When I have troubles, I call out to you because you answer me.


## Psalms 86:8 (id: 1019086008)

8Lord, among all the gods whom the heathen nations worship, there is no one like you; not one of them has done the great things that you have done.


## Psalms 86:9 (id: 1019086009)

9Lord, someday people from all the nations that you have established will come and bow down in front of you, and they will praise you.


## Psalms 86:10 (id: 1019086010)

10You are great, and you do wonderful things; only you are God.


## Psalms 86:11 (id: 1019086011)

11Yahweh, teach me what you want me to do so that I may conduct my life according to what you say, all of which is right. Cause me to have an awesome respect for you with all my inner being.


## Psalms 86:12 (id: 1019086012)

12Lord, my God, I will thank you with all my inner being, and I will praise you forever.


## Psalms 86:13 (id: 1019086013)

13You faithfully love me very much as you have promised; you have prevented me from dying and going to the place where dead people are.


## Psalms 86:14 (id: 1019086014)

14But God, proud men are trying to attack me; a gang of cruel men are wanting to kill me; they are men who do not have any respect for you.


## Psalms 86:15 (id: 1019086015)

15But Lord, you always act mercifully and kindly; you do not become angry quickly; you faithfully love us very much and always do for us what you have promised to do.


## Psalms 86:16 (id: 1019086016)

16Look down toward me and act mercifully to me; cause me to be strong and save me, the one who serves you faithfully as my mother did.


## Psalms 86:17 (id: 1019086017)

17Yahweh, do something to show me that you are being good to me so that those who hate me will see that you have encouraged me and helped me; as a result, they will be ashamed.


## Psalms 87:1 (id: 1019087001)

1A psalm written by one of the descendants of Korah; The city is established on his holy mountain.


## Psalms 87:2 (id: 1019087002)

2Yahweh loves that city, Jerusalem, more than he loves any other place in Israel.


## Psalms 87:3 (id: 1019087003)

3All you people in Jerusalem, other people say wonderful things about your city.


## Psalms 87:4 (id: 1019087004)

4And Yahweh said, “I will talk of Rahab and Babyon and the people there who know me. There are some who know me among the people of Egypt and Babylonia, and they live in the lands of Philistia and Tyre and Ethiopia, and they will say, ‘Our home is Jerusalem and our land is Zion.’”


## Psalms 87:5 (id: 1019087005)

5Concerning Zion, people will say, “All of these people who were born far away, they call Jerusalem their home, and Almighty God will cause that city to remain strong.”


## Psalms 87:6 (id: 1019087006)

6Yahweh will write a list of the names of the people of various groups who belong to him, and he will say that he considers them all to be citizens of Jerusalem.


## Psalms 87:7 (id: 1019087007)

7They will all dance and sing, saying, “Jerusalem is the source of all our blessings.”


## Psalms 88:1 (id: 1019088001)

1A psalm that expresses sadness, written for the choir director by Zerah’s son Heman, one of the descendants of Korah; Yahweh God, you who rescue me, all during each day I call out to you to help me, and I cry out to you during each night also.


## Psalms 88:2 (id: 1019088002)

2Listen to my prayer while I cry out to you for help!


## Psalms 88:3 (id: 1019088003)

3I have experienced many troubles, and I am about to die and go where dead people are.


## Psalms 88:4 (id: 1019088004)

4Because I have no more strength, other people believe that I will soon die.


## Psalms 88:5 (id: 1019088005)

5I am like a corpse that has been abandoned; I am like dead people who lie in their graves, people who have been completely forgotten because you do not take care of them anymore.


## Psalms 88:6 (id: 1019088006)

6It is as though you have thrown me into a deep, dark pit, into a place where they throw corpses.


## Psalms 88:7 (id: 1019088007)

7It seems as though you are very angry with me, and it is as though you have crushed me as ocean waves crash down on people.


## Psalms 88:8 (id: 1019088008)

8You have caused my friends to avoid me; I have become repulsive to them. It is as though I were in a prison and cannot escape.


## Psalms 88:9 (id: 1019088009)

9My eyes cannot see well because I cry very much. Yahweh, every day I call out to you to help me; I lift up my hands to you while I pray.


## Psalms 88:10 (id: 1019088010)

10You certainly do not perform miracles for dead people! Their spirits do not arise to praise you!


## Psalms 88:11 (id: 1019088011)

11Corpses in the grave certainly do not tell about your faithfully loving us, and in the place where people are finally destroyed, no one tells about what you faithfully do for us.


## Psalms 88:12 (id: 1019088012)

12No one in the deep, dark pit ever sees the miracles that you perform, and no one in the place where people have been completely forgotten tells about your being good to us.


## Psalms 88:13 (id: 1019088013)

13But as for me, Yahweh, I cry out to you to help me; each morning I pray to you.


## Psalms 88:14 (id: 1019088014)

14Yahweh, why do you reject me? Why do you turn away from me?


## Psalms 88:15 (id: 1019088015)

15All the time since I was young, I have suffered and have often almost died; I am in despair because of enduring the terrible things that you have done to me.


## Psalms 88:16 (id: 1019088016)

16I feel that you have crushed me because of your being angry with me; the terrible things that you are doing to me are almost destroying me.


## Psalms 88:17 (id: 1019088017)

17It is as though they surround me like a flood; they are closing in on me from all sides.


## Psalms 88:18 (id: 1019088018)

18You have caused even my friends and others whom I love to avoid me, and it is as though the only friend that I have is darkness.


## Psalms 89:1 (id: 1019089001)

1A song written by Ethan, from the clan of Ezra; Yahweh, I will sing forever about the ways you faithfully love me; people not yet born will hear that you faithfully do all that you have promised.


## Psalms 89:2 (id: 1019089002)

2I will tell people that you will faithfully love us forever, and that your being faithful to do what you have promised is as permanent as the sky.


## Psalms 89:3 (id: 1019089003)

3Yahweh said, “I have made an agreement with David, whom I chose to serve me. I have made this solemn agreement with him:


## Psalms 89:4 (id: 1019089004)

4‘I will enable various ones of your descendants to always be kings; the line of kings descended from you will never end.’”


## Psalms 89:5 (id: 1019089005)

5Yahweh, I desire that all those beings who are in heaven will praise you for the wonderful things that you do, and that all your holy angels will sing about how you faithfully do what you promise.


## Psalms 89:6 (id: 1019089006)

6There is no one in heaven who can be compared with you, Yahweh. There are no angels in heaven who are equal to you.


## Psalms 89:7 (id: 1019089007)

7When your holy angels gather together, they declare that you must be revered; they say that you are more awesome than all the angels that surround your throne!


## Psalms 89:8 (id: 1019089008)

8O Yahweh God, commander of the angel armies, there is no one who is as powerful as you are; your faithfully doing all that you promise is like a cloak that always surrounds you.


## Psalms 89:9 (id: 1019089009)

9You rule over the powerful seas; when their waves rise up, you calm them.


## Psalms 89:10 (id: 1019089010)

10You are the one who crushed and killed the great sea monster named Rahab. You defeated and scattered your enemies with your great power.


## Psalms 89:11 (id: 1019089011)

11The heavens are yours, and the earth is yours; everything on the earth is yours because you created it all.


## Psalms 89:12 (id: 1019089012)

12You created everything from the north to the south. Mount Tabor and Mount Hermon joyfully praise you .


## Psalms 89:13 (id: 1019089013)

13You are very powerful; you are extremely strong.


## Psalms 89:14 (id: 1019089014)

14You rule over people fairly and justly; you are always faithfully loving us and doing what you promised.


## Psalms 89:15 (id: 1019089015)

15Yahweh, how fortunate are those who worship you with joyful shouts in their festivals, who live knowing that you are always watching over them.


## Psalms 89:16 (id: 1019089016)

16Every day, throughout the day, they rejoice in what you have done, and they praise you for being very good to them.


## Psalms 89:17 (id: 1019089017)

17You give us your glorious strength; because you act in our favor, we defeat our enemies.


## Psalms 89:18 (id: 1019089018)

18Yahweh, you gave us the one who protects us; you, the holy God whom we Israelites worship, he gave us our king.


## Psalms 89:19 (id: 1019089019)

19Long ago you spoke in a vision to one of your servants, saying, “I have crowned a famous soldier; I chose him from among all the people to be a king.


## Psalms 89:20 (id: 1019089020)

20That man is David, the one who will serve me faithfully, and I anointed him with sacred olive oil to make him king.


## Psalms 89:21 (id: 1019089021)

21My strength will always be with him; with my power, I will make him strong.


## Psalms 89:22 (id: 1019089022)

22His enemies will never find ways to outwit him, and wicked people will never defeat him.


## Psalms 89:23 (id: 1019089023)

23I will crush his enemies in front of him and get rid of those who hate him.


## Psalms 89:24 (id: 1019089024)

24I will always be loyal to him and faithfully love him and enable him to defeat his enemies.


## Psalms 89:25 (id: 1019089025)

25I will cause his kingdom to include all the land from the Mediterranean Sea to the Euphrates River.


## Psalms 89:26 (id: 1019089026)

26He will say to me, ‘You are my Father, my God, the one who protects and saves me.’


## Psalms 89:27 (id: 1019089027)

27I will give him the rights as my firstborn son; he will be the greatest king on the earth.


## Psalms 89:28 (id: 1019089028)

28I will always be loyal to him, and my agreement to bless him will last forever.


## Psalms 89:29 (id: 1019089029)

29I will establish a line of his descendants that will never end, various ones of his descendants will always be kings.


## Psalms 89:30 (id: 1019089030)

30But if some of his descendants disobey my laws and do not behave as my commands say that they should,


## Psalms 89:31 (id: 1019089031)

31if they disregard my requirements and do not do the right things that I have told them to do,


## Psalms 89:32 (id: 1019089032)

32I will punish them severely and cause them to suffer for doing wrong.


## Psalms 89:33 (id: 1019089033)

33But I will not stop faithfully loving David, and I will always do what I promised him.


## Psalms 89:34 (id: 1019089034)

34I will not break the agreement that I made with him; I will not change even one word that I spoke to him.


## Psalms 89:35 (id: 1019089035)

35Once I made a solemn promise to David, and that will never change; because I am God, I will never lie to David.


## Psalms 89:36 (id: 1019089036)

36I promised that the line of kings descended from him will go on forever; it will last as long as the sun shines.


## Psalms 89:37 (id: 1019089037)

37That line will be as permanent as the moon that is always watching everything here on earth.”


## Psalms 89:38 (id: 1019089038)

38But Yahweh, now you have rejected him! You are very angry with the king whom you appointed.


## Psalms 89:39 (id: 1019089039)

39It seems that you have broken the agreement that you made with your servant, David; it seems as though you have thrown his crown into the dust.


## Psalms 89:40 (id: 1019089040)

40You have torn down the walls that protect his city and allowed all his forts to become ruins.


## Psalms 89:41 (id: 1019089041)

41All those who pass by plunder his possessions; his neighbors laugh at him.


## Psalms 89:42 (id: 1019089042)

42You have enabled his enemies to defeat him; you have made them all happy.


## Psalms 89:43 (id: 1019089043)

43You have caused his sword to become useless, and you have not helped him in his battles.


## Psalms 89:44 (id: 1019089044)

44You have caused his splendor to end and knocked his throne to the ground.


## Psalms 89:45 (id: 1019089045)

45You have caused him to become old when he is still young and caused him to be very shamed.


## Psalms 89:46 (id: 1019089046)

46O Yahweh, how long will this continue? Will you hide yourself from us forever? How long will your anger against us burn like a fire?


## Psalms 89:47 (id: 1019089047)

47Do not forget that life is very short; Do not forget that you have created all of us to die uselessly.


## Psalms 89:48 (id: 1019089048)

48No one can keep on living and never die; no one can bring himself back from the place of the dead.


## Psalms 89:49 (id: 1019089049)

49Yahweh, you promised long ago that you would faithfully love me; why are you not doing that? You solemnly promised this to David!


## Psalms 89:50 (id: 1019089050)

50Yahweh, do not forget that people insult us! Heathen people curse me!


## Psalms 89:51 (id: 1019089051)

51Yahweh, your enemies insult your chosen king! They insult him wherever he goes.


## Psalms 89:52 (id: 1019089052)

52I hope that Yahweh will be praised forever! Amen! May it be so!


## Psalms 90:1 (id: 1019090001)

1A prayer by the prophet Moses; Lord, you have always been like a home for us.


## Psalms 90:2 (id: 1019090002)

2Before you created the mountains, before you formed the earth and everything that is in it, you were eternally God, and you will be God forever.


## Psalms 90:3 (id: 1019090003)

3When people die, you cause their corpses to become soil again; you change their corpses to become dirt like that from which the first man was created.


## Psalms 90:4 (id: 1019090004)

4When you consider time, a thousand years are as short as one day that passes; you consider that they are as short as a few hours in the night.


## Psalms 90:5 (id: 1019090005)

5You cause people to die suddenly; they live only a short time as a dream lasts only a short time. They are like grass that grows up.


## Psalms 90:6 (id: 1019090006)

6In the morning the grass sprouts and grows well, but in the evening it dries up and completely withers.


## Psalms 90:7 (id: 1019090007)

7Similarly, because of the sins that we commit, you become angry with us; you terrify us and then you destroy us.


## Psalms 90:8 (id: 1019090008)

8It is as though you place our sins in front of you; you spread out even our secret sins where you can see them.


## Psalms 90:9 (id: 1019090009)

9Because you are angry with us, you cause our lives to end; the years that we live pass as quickly as a sigh does.


## Psalms 90:10 (id: 1019090010)

10People live for only seventy years; if they are strong, some of them live for eighty years. But even during good years we have much pain and troubles; our lives soon end, and we die.


## Psalms 90:11 (id: 1019090011)

11No one has really experienced the powerful things you can do to them when you are angry with them, and people are not afraid that you will punish them because of your being angry with them.


## Psalms 90:12 (id: 1019090012)

12So teach us to realize that we live for only a short time in order that we may use our time wisely.


## Psalms 90:13 (id: 1019090013)

13Yahweh, how long will you be angry with us? Pity us who serve you.


## Psalms 90:14 (id: 1019090014)

14Each morning, show us that it is enough for us if you love us faithfully as you have promised you would do. Show us this so that we may shout joyfully and be happy all during the years that we live.


## Psalms 90:15 (id: 1019090015)

15Cause us to be now as happy for as many years as you afflicted us and we experienced troubles.


## Psalms 90:16 (id: 1019090016)

16Enable us to see the great things that you do, and enable our descendants to see your glorious power also.


## Psalms 90:17 (id: 1019090017)

17Lord, our God, give us your blessings and enable us to be successful; yes, cause us to be successful in everything that we do!


## Psalms 91:1 (id: 1019091001)

1Those who live under the protection of God Almighty, will be able to rest safely under his care.


## Psalms 91:2 (id: 1019091002)

2I will declare to Yahweh, “You protect me; you are like a fort in which I am safe. You are my God, the one in whom I trust.”


## Psalms 91:3 (id: 1019091003)

3He will rescue you from all hidden traps and save you from deadly diseases.


## Psalms 91:4 (id: 1019091004)

4He will shield you as a bird protects her young under her wings. You will be safe in his care. His faithfully doing what he has promised is like a shield that will protect you.


## Psalms 91:5 (id: 1019091005)

5You will not be afraid of things that happen during the night that could terrorize you or of arrows that your enemies will shoot at you during the day.


## Psalms 91:6 (id: 1019091006)

6You will not be afraid of plagues that demons cause when they attack people at night or of other evil forces that kill people at midday.


## Psalms 91:7 (id: 1019091007)

7Even if a thousand people fall dead alongside you, even if ten thousand people are dying around you, you will not be harmed.


## Psalms 91:8 (id: 1019091008)

8Look and see that wicked people are being punished!


## Psalms 91:9 (id: 1019091009)

9Yahweh protects me; trust God Almighty to shelter you, too.


## Psalms 91:10 (id: 1019091010)

10If you do, nothing evil will happen to you; no plague will come near your house


## Psalms 91:11 (id: 1019091011)

11because Yahweh will command his angels to protect you in whatever you are doing.


## Psalms 91:12 (id: 1019091012)

12They will hold you up with their hands so that you will not hurt your foot on a big stone.


## Psalms 91:13 (id: 1019091013)

13You will be kept safe from being harmed by your enemies; it will be as though you were killing strong lions and poisonous snakes by stepping on them!


## Psalms 91:14 (id: 1019091014)

14Yahweh says, “I will rescue those who love me; I will protect them because they acknowledge that I am Yahweh.


## Psalms 91:15 (id: 1019091015)

15When they call out to me, I will answer them. I will help them when they are experiencing trouble; I will rescue them and honor them.


## Psalms 91:16 (id: 1019091016)

16I will reward them by enabling them to live a long time, and I will save them.”


## Psalms 92:1 (id: 1019092001)

1A psalm that is to be sung on Sabbath days. Yahweh, it is good for people to thank you and to sing praise to you who are greater than any other god.


## Psalms 92:2 (id: 1019092002)

2It is good to proclaim every morning that you faithfully love us and to sing songs each night that declare that you always do what you have promised to do,


## Psalms 92:3 (id: 1019092003)

3accompanied by musicians playing harps that have ten strings and by the sounds made by a lyre.


## Psalms 92:4 (id: 1019092004)

4Yahweh, you have caused me to be glad; I sing joyfully because of what you have done.


## Psalms 92:5 (id: 1019092005)

5Yahweh, the things that you do are great! But it is difficult to understand all that you think.


## Psalms 92:6 (id: 1019092006)

6There are things that you do that foolish people cannot know about, things that stupid people cannot understand.


## Psalms 92:7 (id: 1019092007)

7They do not understand that although the number of wicked people increases as blades of grass do and that those who do what is evil prosper, they will be completely destroyed.


## Psalms 92:8 (id: 1019092008)

8But Yahweh, you will be king forever.
