## Psalms 92:9 (id: 1019092009)

9Yahweh, your enemies will certainly die, and those who do wicked things will be defeated.


## Psalms 92:10 (id: 1019092010)

10But you have caused me to be as strong as a wild ox; you have caused me to be very joyful.


## Psalms 92:11 (id: 1019092011)

11I have seen you defeat my enemies, and I have heard those evil men wail while they were being slaughtered.


## Psalms 92:12 (id: 1019092012)

12But righteous people will prosper like palm trees that grow well, like the cedar trees that grow in Lebanon.


## Psalms 92:13 (id: 1019092013)

13They are like the trees that people plant at the temple of Yahweh in Jerusalem, the trees that are close to the courtyard of the temple of our God.


## Psalms 92:14 (id: 1019092014)

14Even when righteous people become old, they do many things that please God. They remain strong and full of energy like trees that remain full of sap.


## Psalms 92:15 (id: 1019092015)

15That shows that Yahweh is just; he is like a huge rock on which I am safe, and he never does anything that is wicked.


## Psalms 93:1 (id: 1019093001)

1Yahweh, you have become the King! The majesty and the power that you have are like robes that a king wears. You put the world firmly in place, and it will never be moved out of its place.


## Psalms 93:2 (id: 1019093002)

2You started to rule as king a very long time ago; you have always existed.


## Psalms 93:3 (id: 1019093003)

3Yahweh, when you created the world, you separated the water from the chaotic mass and formed oceans, and the waves of the waters of those oceans still roar,


## Psalms 93:4 (id: 1019093004)

4but you are greater than the roar of those oceans, more powerful than the ocean waves! You are Yahweh, the one who is greater than any other god!


## Psalms 93:5 (id: 1019093005)

5Yahweh, your laws never change, and your temple has always been holy. That will be true forever.


## Psalms 94:1 (id: 1019094001)

1Yahweh, you are able to get revenge on your enemies. So show them that you are going to punish them!


## Psalms 94:2 (id: 1019094002)

2You are the one who judges all people on the earth; so arise and give them what they deserve.


## Psalms 94:3 (id: 1019094003)

3Yahweh, how long will those wicked people be glad? It is not right that they continue being glad!


## Psalms 94:4 (id: 1019094004)

4They do evil things, and they boast about doing them; how long will they be allowed to continue doing that?


## Psalms 94:5 (id: 1019094005)

5Yahweh, it is as though those wicked people were crushing us, your people; they oppress the nation that you have made and that belongs to you alone.


## Psalms 94:6 (id: 1019094006)

6They murder widows and orphans and people from other countries who think it is safe to live in our land.


## Psalms 94:7 (id: 1019094007)

7Those wicked people say, “Yahweh does not see anything; the God whom those Israelites worship does not see the evil things that we do.”


## Psalms 94:8 (id: 1019094008)

8You evil people who rule Israel, you are foolish and stupid; when will you become wise?


## Psalms 94:9 (id: 1019094009)

9God made our ears; do you think that he cannot hear what you say? He created our eyes; do you think that he cannot see the evil things that you do?


## Psalms 94:10 (id: 1019094010)

10He corrects the leaders of other nations; do you think that he will not punish you? He is the one who knows everything; why do you think that he does not know what you do?


## Psalms 94:11 (id: 1019094011)

11Yahweh knows everything that people are thinking; he knows that what they think is evil and useless.


## Psalms 94:12 (id: 1019094012)

12Yahweh, how fortunate are those who allow you to discipline them, those who want you to teach them your laws.


## Psalms 94:13 (id: 1019094013)

13When those people have had troubles, you cause those troubles to cease, and someday it will be as though you will dig pits for the wicked people, and that they will fall into those pits and die.


## Psalms 94:14 (id: 1019094014)

14Yahweh will not abandon his people; he will not desert those who belong to him .


## Psalms 94:15 (id: 1019094015)

15Someday judges will decide matters fairly for people, and all honest people will be pleased about that.


## Psalms 94:16 (id: 1019094016)

16But when wicked people oppressed me, no one defended me! No one stood up to testify for me against those evil people.


## Psalms 94:17 (id: 1019094017)

17If Yahweh had not helped me at that time, I would have been executed; my life would have gone to the place where dead people say nothing.


## Psalms 94:18 (id: 1019094018)

18I said, “I am falling into disaster,” but, Yahweh, you held me up by faithfully loving me.


## Psalms 94:19 (id: 1019094019)

19Whenever I am very worried, you comfort me and cause me to be happy.


## Psalms 94:20 (id: 1019094020)

20You have nothing to do with wicked judges, those who establish laws that allow people to do what is not right.


## Psalms 94:21 (id: 1019094021)

21They plan to get rid of righteous people, and they declare that innocent people must be executed.


## Psalms 94:22 (id: 1019094022)

22But Yahweh has become like my fortress; my God is like a huge rock on which I am protected.


## Psalms 94:23 (id: 1019094023)

23He will punish those wicked leaders in return for the things that they have done; he will get rid of them because of the sins that they have committed; yes, Yahweh our God will wipe them out.


## Psalms 95:1 (id: 1019095001)

1Come, sing to Yahweh; sing joyfully to the one who protects us and saves us!


## Psalms 95:2 (id: 1019095002)

2We should thank him as we come before him and sing joyful songs as we praise him.


## Psalms 95:3 (id: 1019095003)

3Because Yahweh is a great God, he is a great king who rules over all other gods.


## Psalms 95:4 (id: 1019095004)

4He rules over the whole earth from the deepest places to the highest mountains.


## Psalms 95:5 (id: 1019095005)

5The seas are his because he made them. He is the one who made the dry land.


## Psalms 95:6 (id: 1019095006)

6We should come, worship, and bow down before him. We should kneel before Yahweh, the one who made us.


## Psalms 95:7 (id: 1019095007)

7He is our God, and we are the people whom he protects, like sheep that a shepherd takes care of. I desire that today you may hear what Yahweh is saying to you.


## Psalms 95:8 (id: 1019095008)

8He says, “Do not become stubborn as your ancestors did at Meribah, and as they did at Massah in the wilderness.


## Psalms 95:9 (id: 1019095009)

9There your ancestors wanted to see if they could do evil things without my punishing them. Even though they had seen me perform many miracles, they tested whether I would continue to be patient with them.


## Psalms 95:10 (id: 1019095010)

10For forty years I was angry with those people, and I said, ‘Those people are unreliable. They refuse to obey my commands.’


## Psalms 95:11 (id: 1019095011)

11So because I was very angry; I solemnly said about them, ‘They will never enter the land of Canaan where I would have allowed them to rest!’”


## Psalms 96:1 (id: 1019096001)

1Sing to Yahweh a new song! You people throughout the earth, sing to Yahweh!


## Psalms 96:2 (id: 1019096002)

2Sing to Yahweh and praise him! Every day proclaim to others that he has saved us.


## Psalms 96:3 (id: 1019096003)

3Tell about his glory to all people groups; tell all people groups the marvelous things that he has done.


## Psalms 96:4 (id: 1019096004)

4Yahweh is great, and he deserves to be praised very much; he should be revered more than all the gods.


## Psalms 96:5 (id: 1019096005)

5All the gods the other people groups worship are only idols, but Yahweh is truly great; he created the skies!


## Psalms 96:6 (id: 1019096006)

6God shows his splendor and majesty; they shine out from where he rules. Strength and beauty are in his holy house.


## Psalms 96:7 (id: 1019096007)

7You people in nations all over the earth, praise Yahweh! Praise Yahweh for his glorious power!


## Psalms 96:8 (id: 1019096008)

8Praise Yahweh as he deserves to be praised; bring an offering and come to his temple.


## Psalms 96:9 (id: 1019096009)

9Bow down before Yahweh because his holiness shines out from him with wonderful beauty. Everyone on earth should be very afraid in his presence, because he is good and powerful, completely different than us.


## Psalms 96:10 (id: 1019096010)

10Say to all the people groups, “Yahweh is the king! He put the world in its place, and nothing will ever be able to move it. He will judge all the people groups fairly.”


## Psalms 96:11 (id: 1019096011)

11All the beings that are in the heavens should be glad, and all the people on the earth should rejoice. The oceans and all the creatures that are in the oceans should roar to praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 96:12 (id: 1019096012)

12The fields and everything that grows in them should rejoice. When they do that, it will be as though all the trees in the forests are singing joyfully


## Psalms 96:13 (id: 1019096013)

13in front of Yahweh. That will happen when he comes to judge everyone on the earth. He will judge all the people fairly according to what he knows is true.


## Psalms 97:1 (id: 1019097001)

1Yahweh is the king! I want everyone on the earth to be glad and the people who live on the islands in the oceans to also rejoice about that!


## Psalms 97:2 (id: 1019097002)

2There are very dark clouds around him; he rules completely, justly, and fairly.


## Psalms 97:3 (id: 1019097003)

3He sends fire in front of him, and he completely burns all his enemies in that fire.


## Psalms 97:4 (id: 1019097004)

4All around the world he sends lightning to flash; people on the earth see it, and it causes them to be afraid and to tremble.


## Psalms 97:5 (id: 1019097005)

5The mountains melt like wax in front of Yahweh, in front of the one who is the Lord, who rules over all the earth.


## Psalms 97:6 (id: 1019097006)

6The angels in heaven proclaim that he acts righteously, and all the people groups see his glory.


## Psalms 97:7 (id: 1019097007)

7Everyone who worships idols should be ashamed; all those who are proud of their false gods should realize that their gods are useless. All those gods will bow down to worship Yahweh.


## Psalms 97:8 (id: 1019097008)

8The people of Jerusalem heard that God is just, and they rejoiced; people in the other cities in Judah also rejoiced because Yahweh judges and punishes wicked people.


## Psalms 97:9 (id: 1019097009)

9Yahweh is the supreme King over all the earth; he has very great power, and none of the other gods has any power.


## Psalms 97:10 (id: 1019097010)

10Yahweh loves those who hate what people do that is evil; he protects the lives of his people, and he rescues them when the wicked people try to harm them.


## Psalms 97:11 (id: 1019097011)

11He makes the righteous people truly live; he causes those who are righteous in their inner beings to rejoice.


## Psalms 97:12 (id: 1019097012)

12You righteous people, rejoice about what Yahweh has done, and thank him, our holy God!


## Psalms 98:1 (id: 1019098001)

1A psalm. Sing to Yahweh a new song because he has done wonderful things! By his power he has defeated his enemies.


## Psalms 98:2 (id: 1019098002)

2Yahweh has declared to people that he has defeated his enemies; he has revealed that he has punished his enemies, and people in all the world have seen that he has done it.


## Psalms 98:3 (id: 1019098003)

3As he promised to us Israelite people, he has faithfully loved us and been loyal to us. People who live in very remote places in all the earth have seen that our God has defeated his enemies.


## Psalms 98:4 (id: 1019098004)

4All you people everywhere should sing joyfully to Yahweh; praise him while you sing and shout joyfully!


## Psalms 98:5 (id: 1019098005)

5Praise Yahweh while you play the lyres, playing delightful music.


## Psalms 98:6 (id: 1019098006)

6Some of you should blow trumpets and other horns while others shout joyfully to Yahweh, our king.


## Psalms 98:7 (id: 1019098007)

7The oceans and all the creatures that are in the oceans should roar to praise Yahweh. Everyone on the earth should sing!


## Psalms 98:8 (id: 1019098008)

8It should seem as though the rivers were clapping their hands to praise Yahweh and that the hills were singing together joyfully in front of Yahweh


## Psalms 98:9 (id: 1019098009)

9because he will come to judge everyone on the earth! He will judge all the people groups in the world justly and fairly.


## Psalms 99:1 (id: 1019099001)

1Yahweh is the supreme king, so all the people groups should tremble in his presence! He sits on his throne in the temple above the statues of winged creatures, so the earth should quake!


## Psalms 99:2 (id: 1019099002)

2Yahweh is a mighty king in Jerusalem; he is also the supreme ruler of all the people groups.


## Psalms 99:3 (id: 1019099003)

3They should praise him because he is very great; he is holy!


## Psalms 99:4 (id: 1019099004)

4He is a mighty king who loves what is just; he has acted justly and fairly in Israel.


## Psalms 99:5 (id: 1019099005)

5Praise Yahweh, our God! Worship him in front of his footstool, the sacred chest in his temple, where he rules people. He is holy!


## Psalms 99:6 (id: 1019099006)

6Moses and Aaron were two of his priests; Samuel also was someone who prayed to him. Those three cried out to Yahweh to help them, and he answered them.


## Psalms 99:7 (id: 1019099007)

7He spoke to Moses and Aaron from the cloud that was like a huge pillar; they obeyed all the laws and commandments that he gave to them.


## Psalms 99:8 (id: 1019099008)

8Yahweh, our God, you answered your people when they cried out to you to help them; you are a God who forgave them for the sins that they had committed, even though you punished them for the things that they did that were wrong.


## Psalms 99:9 (id: 1019099009)

9Praise Yahweh, our God, and worship him at the temple on his sacred hill; it is right to do that because Yahweh, our God, is holy!


## Psalms 100:1 (id: 1019100001)

1A psalm of thanksgiving; Everyone in the world should shout joyfully to Yahweh!


## Psalms 100:2 (id: 1019100002)

2We should worship Yahweh gladly! We should come before him singing joyful songs.


## Psalms 100:3 (id: 1019100003)

3We should acknowledge that Yahweh is God; it is he who made us, and so we belong to him. We are the people that he takes care of; we are like sheep that their shepherd cares for.


## Psalms 100:4 (id: 1019100004)

4Enter the gates of his temple thanking him; enter the courtyard of the temple singing songs to praise him! Thank him and praise him


## Psalms 100:5 (id: 1019100005)

5because Yahweh always does good things for us. He faithfully loves us as he promised us, and he is faithful.


## Psalms 101:1 (id: 1019101001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, I will sing to you! I will sing about your faithful and just loyalty to us.


## Psalms 101:2 (id: 1019101002)

2I promise that while I rule people, I will behave in such a way that no one will be able to criticize me. Yahweh, when will you come to help me? I will do things that are right.


## Psalms 101:3 (id: 1019101003)

3I will not allow anyone who does what is evil to come to me. I hate the deeds of those who turn away from you; I will completely avoid those people.


## Psalms 101:4 (id: 1019101004)

4I will not be dishonest, and I will not have anything to do with evil.


## Psalms 101:5 (id: 1019101005)

5I will get rid of anyone who secretly slanders someone else, and I will not let anyone near me who is proud and arrogant.


## Psalms 101:6 (id: 1019101006)

6I will approve of people in this land who are loyal to God, and I will allow them to live with me. I will allow to serve me those who behave in such a way that no one can criticize them.


## Psalms 101:7 (id: 1019101007)

7I will not allow anyone who deceives others to work in my palace, and no one who tells lies will be allowed to continually come to work for me.


## Psalms 101:8 (id: 1019101008)

8Every day I will try to get rid of all the wicked people in this land; I will expel them from this city, which is Yahweh’s city.


## Psalms 102:1 (id: 1019102001)

1A prayer written by someone who was afflicted, when he was discouraged and pleaded for Yahweh to help. Yahweh, listen to what I am praying; hear me while I cry out to you!


## Psalms 102:2 (id: 1019102002)

2Do not turn away! Listen to me, and answer me quickly now when I am calling out to you!


## Psalms 102:3 (id: 1019102003)

3My life is ending like smoke that disappears; I have a big fever which burns my body as a fire burns.


## Psalms 102:4 (id: 1019102004)

4I feel as though I am drying up like grass that has been mown, and I do not even think about eating any food.


## Psalms 102:5 (id: 1019102005)

5I groan loudly, and my bones can be seen under my skin because I have become very thin.


## Psalms 102:6 (id: 1019102006)

6I am like a lonely and despised vulture in the desert, like an owl by itself in the abandoned ruins of a building.


## Psalms 102:7 (id: 1019102007)

7I lie awake at night; because there is no one to comfort me, I am like a lonely bird sitting on a housetop.


## Psalms 102:8 (id: 1019102008)

8All during each day my enemies insult me; those who make fun of me mention my name and say, “May you be like him” when they curse people.


## Psalms 102:9 (id: 1019102009)

9(9\-10\) Because you are very angry with me, I sit in ashes while I am suffering greatly; those ashes fall on the bread that I eat, and what I drink has my tears mixed with it. It is as though you have picked me up and thrown me away!


## Psalms 102:11 (id: 1019102011)

11My time to remain alive is short like an evening shadow that will soon be gone. I am withering as grass withers in the hot sun.


## Psalms 102:12 (id: 1019102012)

12But Yahweh, you are our king who rules forever; people who are not yet born will remember you.


## Psalms 102:13 (id: 1019102013)

13You will arise and act mercifully toward the people of Jerusalem; it is now time for you to do that; this is the time for you to be kind to them.


## Psalms 102:14 (id: 1019102014)

14Even though the city has been destroyed, we who serve you still love the stones that were formerly in the city walls; because now there is rubble everywhere, we, your people, are very sad when we see it.


## Psalms 102:15 (id: 1019102015)

15Yahweh, someday the people of other nations will have an awesome respect for you; all the kings on the earth will see that you are very glorious.


## Psalms 102:16 (id: 1019102016)

16You will rebuild Jerusalem, and you will appear there with your glory.


## Psalms 102:17 (id: 1019102017)

17You will listen to the prayers of your people who are homeless, and you will not ignore them when they plead with you to help them.


## Psalms 102:18 (id: 1019102018)

18Yahweh, I want to write these words so that people in future years will know what you have done, in order that people who are not born yet will praise you.


## Psalms 102:19 (id: 1019102019)

19They will know that you looked down from your own place in heaven and saw what was happening on the earth.


## Psalms 102:20 (id: 1019102020)

20They will know that you hear prisoners groaning and that you will set free those who have been told, “You will be executed.”


## Psalms 102:21 (id: 1019102021)

21As a result, people in Jerusalem will praise you for what you have done.


## Psalms 102:22 (id: 1019102022)

22Many people from other people groups and those who are citizens of other kingdoms will gather to worship you.


## Psalms 102:23 (id: 1019102023)

23But now you have caused me to become weak while I am still young; I think that I will not remain alive very long.


## Psalms 102:24 (id: 1019102024)

24I say to you, “My God, do not take me away from the earth now before I become old! You, on the other hand, live forever!


## Psalms 102:25 (id: 1019102025)

25You created the world long ago, and you made the heavens with your own hands.


## Psalms 102:26 (id: 1019102026)

26The earth and the heavens will disappear, but you will remain. They will wear out as clothes wear out. You will get rid of them as people get rid of old clothes, and they will no longer exist.


## Psalms 102:27 (id: 1019102027)

27But you are not like the things that you created because you are always the same; you never die.


## Psalms 102:28 (id: 1019102028)

28Someday our children will live safely in Jerusalem, and their descendants will be protected as they live in your presence.”


## Psalms 103:1 (id: 1019103001)

1A psalm written by David. I tell myself that I should praise Yahweh. I will praise him because he is holy.


## Psalms 103:2 (id: 1019103002)

2I tell myself that I should praise Yahweh and never forget all the kind things he has done for me.


## Psalms 103:3 (id: 1019103003)

3He forgives all my sins, and he heals me from all my diseases;


## Psalms 103:4 (id: 1019103004)

4he keeps me from dying, and he blesses me by faithfully loving me and acting mercifully to me as he promised to do.


## Psalms 103:5 (id: 1019103005)

5He gives me good things during my entire life. He makes me feel young and strong like eagles.


## Psalms 103:6 (id: 1019103006)

6Yahweh judges justly all those who have been treated unfairly.


## Psalms 103:7 (id: 1019103007)

7Long ago he revealed to Moses what he planned to do; he showed to the ancestors of us Israelites the mighty things that he was able to do.


## Psalms 103:8 (id: 1019103008)

8Yahweh acts mercifully and kindly; he does not quickly get angry when we sin; he is always showing us that he faithfully loves us.


## Psalms 103:9 (id: 1019103009)

9He will not keep rebuking us, and he will not remain angry forever.


## Psalms 103:10 (id: 1019103010)

10He has not punished us for our sins as we deserved.


## Psalms 103:11 (id: 1019103011)

11The skies are very high above the earth, and Yahweh’s faithful love for all those who revere him is just as great.


## Psalms 103:12 (id: 1019103012)

12He has taken away the guilt for our sins and put it as far from us as the east is from the west.


## Psalms 103:13 (id: 1019103013)

13Just as parents act mercifully toward their children, Yahweh is kind to those who revere him.


## Psalms 103:14 (id: 1019103014)

14He knows what our bodies are like; he remembers that he created us from dust and that we therefore quickly fail to do what pleases him .


## Psalms 103:15 (id: 1019103015)

15We humans do not live forever; we are like grass which withers and dies. We are like wild flowers that bloom for a short while;


## Psalms 103:16 (id: 1019103016)

16but then the hot wind blows over them, and they disappear; no one sees them again.


## Psalms 103:17 (id: 1019103017)

17But Yahweh will faithfully keep loving forever all those who revere him, as he promised. He will act fairly to our children and to their children;


## Psalms 103:18 (id: 1019103018)

18he will act that way to all those who obey the covenant he made with them to bless them if they did what he told them to do, to all those who obey what he has commanded.


## Psalms 103:19 (id: 1019103019)

19Yahweh has taken his seat in the heavens where he rules as king; from there he rules over everything.


## Psalms 103:20 (id: 1019103020)

20You angels who belong to Yahweh, praise him! You are powerful creatures who do what he tells you to do; you obey what he commands.


## Psalms 103:21 (id: 1019103021)

21Praise Yahweh, you armies of angels who serve him and do what he desires.


## Psalms 103:22 (id: 1019103022)

22All you things that Yahweh has created, praise him; praise him in every place where he rules, everywhere! I also will praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 104:1 (id: 1019104001)

1I tell myself that I should praise Yahweh. Yahweh, my God, you are very great! As a king has on his royal robes, you have honor and majesty all around you!


## Psalms 104:2 (id: 1019104002)

2You created light and you hide behind it. You spread out the whole sky as someone sets up a tent.


## Psalms 104:3 (id: 1019104003)

3You built your palace on the clouds. You made the clouds to be like chariots to carry you.


## Psalms 104:4 (id: 1019104004)

4You caused the winds to be like your messengers, and flames of fire to be like your servants.


## Psalms 104:5 (id: 1019104005)

5You placed the world firmly on its foundation so that it can never be moved.


## Psalms 104:6 (id: 1019104006)

6Later, you covered the earth with a flood, like a blanket; and the water covered the mountains.


## Psalms 104:7 (id: 1019104007)

7But when you rebuked the water, the oceans receded; your voice spoke like thunder, and then the waters rushed away.


## Psalms 104:8 (id: 1019104008)

8Mountains rose up from the water, and the valleys sank down to the levels that you had determined for them.


## Psalms 104:9 (id: 1019104009)

9Then you set a boundary for the oceans, a boundary that they cannot cross; their water will never again cover the whole earth.


## Psalms 104:10 (id: 1019104010)

10You make springs to pour water into ravines; their water flows down between the mountains.


## Psalms 104:11 (id: 1019104011)

11Those streams provide water for all the animals to drink; the wild donkeys drink the water and are no longer thirsty.


## Psalms 104:12 (id: 1019104012)

12Birds make their nests alongside the streams, and they sing among the branches of the trees.


## Psalms 104:13 (id: 1019104013)

13From the heavens you send rain down on the mountains, and you fill the earth with many good things that you create.


## Psalms 104:14 (id: 1019104014)

14You make grass to grow for the cattle to eat, and you make plants to grow for people. In that way, animals and people get their food from what grows in the soil.


## Psalms 104:15 (id: 1019104015)

15We get grapes to make wine to drink and to make us cheerful; we get olives to make our face shine, and we get grain to make bread to give us strength.


## Psalms 104:16 (id: 1019104016)

16Yahweh, you send plenty of rain to water your trees, the cedar trees that you planted in Lebanon.


## Psalms 104:17 (id: 1019104017)

17Birds make their nests in those trees, and storks make their nests in pine trees.


## Psalms 104:18 (id: 1019104018)

18High up in the mountains the wild goats live, and hyraxes live in the rocks.


## Psalms 104:19 (id: 1019104019)

19Yahweh, you made the moon to indicate the times for our festivals, and you made the sun that knows when to go down.


## Psalms 104:20 (id: 1019104020)

20You bring darkness, and it becomes night when all the animals in the forest prowl around looking for food.


## Psalms 104:21 (id: 1019104021)

21At night the young lions roar as they seek their prey, but they depend on you to give them food.


## Psalms 104:22 (id: 1019104022)

22At dawn, they go back to their dens and lie down.


## Psalms 104:23 (id: 1019104023)

23During the daytime, people go to their work; they work until it is evening.


## Psalms 104:24 (id: 1019104024)

24Yahweh, you have made so many different kinds of things! You were very wise as you made them all. The earth is full of the creatures that you made.


## Psalms 104:25 (id: 1019104025)

25We see the ocean which is very vast! It is full of many kinds of living creatures, big ones and little ones.


## Psalms 104:26 (id: 1019104026)

26We see the ships which sail along! We see the huge sea monster which you made to splash around in the sea.


## Psalms 104:27 (id: 1019104027)

27All of these creatures depend on you to give them the food that they need.


## Psalms 104:28 (id: 1019104028)

28When you give them the food that they need, they gather it. You give them what you have in your hand, and they eat it and are satisfied.


## Psalms 104:29 (id: 1019104029)

29But if you refuse to give food to them, they become terrified. When you cause them to stop breathing, they die; their bodies decay and become soil again.


## Psalms 104:30 (id: 1019104030)

30When you cause newborn creatures to begin to breathe, they start to live; You give new life to all the living creatures on the earth.


## Psalms 104:31 (id: 1019104031)

31May the glory of Yahweh last forever. May he rejoice about all the things that he has created.


## Psalms 104:32 (id: 1019104032)

32He makes the earth shake just by looking at it! By merely touching the mountains he makes them pour out fire and smoke!


## Psalms 104:33 (id: 1019104033)

33I will sing to Yahweh as long as I live. I will praise my God until the day that I die.


## Psalms 104:34 (id: 1019104034)

34May Yahweh be pleased by all these things that I have thought about him because I rejoice about knowing him.


## Psalms 104:35 (id: 1019104035)

35However, may sinners disappear from the earth; may there be no more wicked people! But as for me, I will praise Yahweh! Praise him!


## Psalms 105:1 (id: 1019105001)

1Give thanks to Yahweh; worship him and pray to him. Tell everyone in the world what he has done!


## Psalms 105:2 (id: 1019105002)

2Sing to him; praise him as you sing to him; tell others about his wonderful miracles.


## Psalms 105:3 (id: 1019105003)

3Be proud of Yahweh, who alone is God. You people who worship Yahweh, rejoice!


## Psalms 105:4 (id: 1019105004)

4Ask Yahweh to help you and give you his strength, and always seek to be with him!


## Psalms 105:5 (id: 1019105005)

5(5\-6\) You people who are descendants of God’s servant Abraham, you descendants of Jacob, the people whom God has chosen, think about all the wonderful things that he has done; he performed miracles, and he punished all our enemies.


## Psalms 105:7 (id: 1019105007)

7He is Yahweh, our God. He rules and judges people throughout the earth.


## Psalms 105:8 (id: 1019105008)

8He never forgets the covenant that he made; he made a promise that will last for a thousand generations.


## Psalms 105:9 (id: 1019105009)

9That is the covenant that he made with Abraham, and he repeated that covenant with Isaac.


## Psalms 105:10 (id: 1019105010)

10Later he confirmed it again to Jacob as a covenant for the Israelite people that would last forever.


## Psalms 105:11 (id: 1019105011)

11What he said was, “I will give you the region of Canaan; it will belong to you and your descendants forever.”


## Psalms 105:12 (id: 1019105012)

12He said that to them when there were only a few of them, a tiny group of people who were living in that land like strangers.


## Psalms 105:13 (id: 1019105013)

13They continued to wander from one place to another, from one kingdom to another.


## Psalms 105:14 (id: 1019105014)

14But he did not allow others to oppress them. He warned those kings by saying to them,


## Psalms 105:15 (id: 1019105015)

15“Do not do harm to the people whom I have chosen! Do not harm my prophets!”


## Psalms 105:16 (id: 1019105016)

16He sent a famine to Canaan, and as a result all the people had no food to eat.


## Psalms 105:17 (id: 1019105017)

17So his people went to Egypt, but first he sent someone there. He sent Joseph, who had been sold to be a slave.


## Psalms 105:18 (id: 1019105018)

18Later, while Joseph was in prison in Egypt, they put his legs in shackles that hurt his feet, and they put an iron collar around his neck.


## Psalms 105:19 (id: 1019105019)

19Joseph was in prison until the time the events he predicted came to pass. This was how Yahweh tested Joseph.


## Psalms 105:20 (id: 1019105020)

20The king of Egypt sent servants, who set him free; this ruler released Joseph from prison.


## Psalms 105:21 (id: 1019105021)

21Then he appointed him to take care of everything in the king’s household, to take care of everything that the king possessed.


## Psalms 105:22 (id: 1019105022)

22Joseph was permitted to command the king’s important servants to do anything that Joseph wanted them to do, and even to tell the king’s advisors the things that they should do for the people of Egypt.


## Psalms 105:23 (id: 1019105023)

23Later, Joseph’s father Jacob arrived in Egypt. He lived like a foreigner in the land that belonged to the descendants of Ham.


## Psalms 105:24 (id: 1019105024)

24Years later Yahweh caused the descendants of Jacob to become very numerous. As a result, their enemies, the Egyptians, considered that the Israelites were too strong.


## Psalms 105:25 (id: 1019105025)

25So Yahweh caused the rulers of Egypt to turn against the Israelite people, and they began to oppress his people.


## Psalms 105:26 (id: 1019105026)

26But then Yahweh sent his servant Moses along with Moses’ older brother Aaron, whom Yahweh had also chosen to be his servant.


## Psalms 105:27 (id: 1019105027)

27Those two performed amazing miracles among the people of Egypt in that land where the descendants of Ham lived.


## Psalms 105:28 (id: 1019105028)

28Yahweh sent darkness so that the people of Egypt could not see anything, but the rulers of Egypt refused to obey when Moses and Aaron commanded them to let the Israelite people leave Egypt.


## Psalms 105:29 (id: 1019105029)

29Yahweh caused all the water in Egypt to become blood, and his doing that caused all the fish to die.


## Psalms 105:30 (id: 1019105030)

30Then he caused the land to become full of frogs; the king and his officials even had frogs in their bedrooms.


## Psalms 105:31 (id: 1019105031)

31Then Yahweh commanded that flies come, and swarms of them descended on the people of Egypt, and gnats also swarmed across the whole country.


## Psalms 105:32 (id: 1019105032)

32Yahweh sent rain, rain that became hail that fell upon them, and he sent wild fires that burned throughout their land.


## Psalms 105:33 (id: 1019105033)

33The hail ruined their grapevines and fig trees and shattered all the other trees.


## Psalms 105:34 (id: 1019105034)

34He commanded locusts to come, and hordes of them came; so many came that they could not be counted.


## Psalms 105:35 (id: 1019105035)

35The locusts ate every green plant in the land, ruining all the crops.


## Psalms 105:36 (id: 1019105036)

36Then Yahweh killed the oldest son in every house of the people of Egypt.


## Psalms 105:37 (id: 1019105037)

37Then he brought the Israelite people out from Egypt; they were carrying heavy loads of jewelry made of silver and gold that the people of Egypt had given to them. No one was left behind because of being sick.


## Psalms 105:38 (id: 1019105038)

38The people of Egypt were glad when the Israelite people left because they had become very afraid of the Israelites.


## Psalms 105:39 (id: 1019105039)

39Then Yahweh spread a cloud to cover the Israelites; and at night it became a big fire in the sky to give them light.


## Psalms 105:40 (id: 1019105040)

40Later the Israelites asked for meat to eat, and Yahweh sent flocks of quail to them, and he gave them plenty of manna, food from the sky, each morning.


## Psalms 105:41 (id: 1019105041)

41One day he caused a rock to open up, and water poured out for them to drink; it was like a river flowing in that desert.


## Psalms 105:42 (id: 1019105042)

42He did that because he kept thinking about the sacred promise that he had given to his servant, Abraham.


## Psalms 105:43 (id: 1019105043)

43So his people were joyful as he brought them out from Egypt; these people whom he had chosen were shouting joyfully as they went.


## Psalms 105:44 (id: 1019105044)

44He gave to them the land that belonged to the people groups that lived there in Canaan, and the Israelites took all their wealth.


## Psalms 105:45 (id: 1019105045)

45Yahweh did all these things so that his people would do all the things that he had commanded them to do. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 106:1 (id: 1019106001)

1Praise Yahweh! Praise Yahweh because everything he does is good; he faithfully loves us forever as he promised us!


## Psalms 106:2 (id: 1019106002)

2Because Yahweh has done many great things, no one can tell all the great things that Yahweh has done, and no one can praise him enough.


## Psalms 106:3 (id: 1019106003)

3How fortunate are those who act fairly, those who always do what is right.


## Psalms 106:4 (id: 1019106004)

4Yahweh, be kind to me when you help your people; help me when you rescue them.


## Psalms 106:5 (id: 1019106005)

5Allow me to see your people become prosperous again and to see all the people of your nation, Israel, become happy again; allow me to be happy with them! I want to praise you along with all those others who belong to you.


## Psalms 106:6 (id: 1019106006)

6We and our ancestors have sinned; we have done what is wicked and evil.


## Psalms 106:7 (id: 1019106007)

7When our ancestors were in Egypt, they did not pay attention to the wonderful things that Yahweh did; they forgot about the many times that he showed that he faithfully loved them. Instead, when they were at the Sea of Reeds, they rebelled against God, who is greater than any other god.


## Psalms 106:8 (id: 1019106008)

8But he rescued them for the sake of his own reputation so that he could show that he is very powerful.


## Psalms 106:9 (id: 1019106009)

9He rebuked the Sea of Reeds and it became dry, and then while he led our ancestors, they walked through it as though it were as dry as a desert.


## Psalms 106:10 (id: 1019106010)

10In that way he rescued them from the power of their enemies.


## Psalms 106:11 (id: 1019106011)

11Then their enemies were drowned in the water of the Sea of Reeds; not one of them was left.


## Psalms 106:12 (id: 1019106012)

12When that happened, our ancestors believed that Yahweh had truly done for them what he had promised to do, and they sang to praise him.


## Psalms 106:13 (id: 1019106013)

13But they soon forgot what he had done for them; they did things without waiting to find out what Yahweh wanted them to do.


## Psalms 106:14 (id: 1019106014)

14They intensely wanted food like they formerly ate in Egypt. They did evil things to find out whether God would punish them or not.


## Psalms 106:15 (id: 1019106015)

15So he gave them what they requested, but he sent a horrible disease upon them.


## Psalms 106:16 (id: 1019106016)

16Later when some of the men became jealous of Moses and his older brother Aaron, who was dedicated to serve Yahweh by being a priest,


## Psalms 106:17 (id: 1019106017)

17the ground opened up and swallowed Dathan and also buried Abiram and his family.


## Psalms 106:18 (id: 1019106018)

18God sent down from heaven a fire which burned up all the wicked people who supported them.


## Psalms 106:19 (id: 1019106019)

19Then the Israelite leaders made a gold statue of a calf at Mount Sinai and worshiped it.


## Psalms 106:20 (id: 1019106020)

20Instead of worshiping our glorious God, they started to worship a statue of an ox that eats grass!


## Psalms 106:21 (id: 1019106021)

21They forgot about God, who had rescued them by the great miracles that he performed in Egypt.


## Psalms 106:22 (id: 1019106022)

22They forgot about the wonderful things that he did for them in Egypt and the amazing things that he did for them at the Sea of Reeds.


## Psalms 106:23 (id: 1019106023)

23Because of that, God said that he would get rid of the Israelites; but Moses, whom God had chosen to serve him, stood up to persuade God not to do that. As a result, God did not destroy them.


## Psalms 106:24 (id: 1019106024)

24Later, our ancestors refused to enter the beautiful land of Canaan because they did not believe that God would do as he promised and would enable them to take the land from the people who were living there.


## Psalms 106:25 (id: 1019106025)

25They stayed in their tents and grumbled and would not pay attention to what Yahweh said that they should do.


## Psalms 106:26 (id: 1019106026)

26So he solemnly told them that he would cause them to die there in the wilderness,


## Psalms 106:27 (id: 1019106027)

27that he would scatter their descendants among the people of other nations and groups who did not believe in him, and that he would allow them to die in those lands.


## Psalms 106:28 (id: 1019106028)

28Later the Israelite people started to worship the idol of Baal at Mount Peor, and they ate meat that had been sacrificed to Baal and those other lifeless gods.


## Psalms 106:29 (id: 1019106029)

29Yahweh became very angry because of what they had done, so again he sent a terrible disease to attack them.


## Psalms 106:30 (id: 1019106030)

30But Phinehas stood up and punished the ones who had sinned greatly, and as a result the plague ended.


## Psalms 106:31 (id: 1019106031)

31People have remembered that righteous deed that Phinehas did, and in future years people will remember it.


## Psalms 106:32 (id: 1019106032)

32Then at the springs of Meribah our ancestors caused Yahweh to become angry again, and as a result Moses had trouble.


## Psalms 106:33 (id: 1019106033)

33They caused Moses to become very angry, and he said things that were foolish.


## Psalms 106:34 (id: 1019106034)

34Our ancestors did not destroy the other people groups as he told them to do.


## Psalms 106:35 (id: 1019106035)

35Instead, the men took women from those people groups, and they started to do the evil things that those people did.


## Psalms 106:36 (id: 1019106036)

36Our ancestors worshiped the idols of those people, which resulted in their being destroyed.


## Psalms 106:37 (id: 1019106037)

37Some of the Israelites sacrificed their sons and daughters to the demons that those idols represented.


## Psalms 106:38 (id: 1019106038)

38They killed children who had done nothing wrong, and offered them as sacrifices to the idols in Canaan. As a result, the land of Canaan was polluted by those murders.


## Psalms 106:39 (id: 1019106039)

39So by their deeds they made it impossible for God to accept them; because they did not faithfully worship only God, they became like women who sleep with other men instead of sleeping only with their husbands.


## Psalms 106:40 (id: 1019106040)

40So Yahweh became very angry with his people; he was completely disgusted with them.


## Psalms 106:41 (id: 1019106041)

41As a result, he allowed people groups who did not believe in him to conquer them, so those who hated our ancestors started to rule over them.


## Psalms 106:42 (id: 1019106042)

42Their enemies oppressed them and completely controlled them.


## Psalms 106:43 (id: 1019106043)

43Many times Yahweh rescued his people, but they continued to rebel against him, and they were finally destroyed because of the sins that they committed.


## Psalms 106:44 (id: 1019106044)

44However, Yahweh always heard them when they cried out to him, and he listened to them when they were distressed.


## Psalms 106:45 (id: 1019106045)

45For their sake, he thought about the covenant that he had made to bless them; because he never stopped loving them very much, he changed his mind about punishing them more.


## Psalms 106:46 (id: 1019106046)

46He caused all those who had taken the Israelites to Babylonia to feel sorry for them.


## Psalms 106:47 (id: 1019106047)

47Yahweh our God, rescue us and bring us back to Israel from among those people groups so that we may thank you and joyfully praise you.


## Psalms 106:48 (id: 1019106048)

48Praise Yahweh, the God whom we Israelites worship, praise him now and forever! All the people should agree! Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 107:1 (id: 1019107001)

1Give thanks to Yahweh because he always does good things for us! His faithful love for us lasts forever, as he has promised us!


## Psalms 107:2 (id: 1019107002)

2Those whom Yahweh has saved should tell others that he has rescued them from their enemies.


## Psalms 107:3 (id: 1019107003)

3He has gathered those of you who were exiled to many lands; he has gathered you together from the east and the west, from the north and from the south.


## Psalms 107:4 (id: 1019107004)

4Some of those who returned from those countries wandered in the desert; they were lost and had no homes to live in.


## Psalms 107:5 (id: 1019107005)

5They were hungry and thirsty, and they even collapsed in exhaustion.


## Psalms 107:6 (id: 1019107006)

6When they were in trouble, they called out to Yahweh, and he rescued them from being distressed.


## Psalms 107:7 (id: 1019107007)

7He led them along a straight road where they walked safely to cities in Canaan where they could live.


## Psalms 107:8 (id: 1019107008)

8They should praise Yahweh for loving them faithfully and for the wonderful things that he does for people.


## Psalms 107:9 (id: 1019107009)

9He gives thirsty people plenty of water to drink, and he gives hungry people plenty of good things to eat.


## Psalms 107:10 (id: 1019107010)

10Some of them were in very dark prisons; they were prisoners, suffering because of chains fastened to their hands and feet.


## Psalms 107:11 (id: 1019107011)

11They were in prison because they had rebelled against the message of God; they were there because they had despised the advice given by God, who is greater than all other gods.


## Psalms 107:12 (id: 1019107012)

12That is why God made them suffer hardships so that they would no longer be proud; when they got into trouble, there was no one who would help them.


## Psalms 107:13 (id: 1019107013)

13When they were in trouble, they called out to Yahweh, and he rescued them from being distressed.


## Psalms 107:14 (id: 1019107014)

14He broke the chains that were on their hands and feet and brought them out of those very dark prisons.


## Psalms 107:15 (id: 1019107015)

15(15\-16\) He broke down the prison gates that were made of bronze; he cut through the prison bars that were made of iron. They should praise Yahweh for loving them faithfully and for the wonderful things that he does for people.


## Psalms 107:17 (id: 1019107017)

17Some of them foolishly rebelled against God, so they suffered for their sins.


## Psalms 107:18 (id: 1019107018)

18They did not want to eat any food, and they almost died.


## Psalms 107:19 (id: 1019107019)

19When they were in trouble, they called out to Yahweh, and he rescued them from being distressed.


## Psalms 107:20 (id: 1019107020)

20When he commanded that they be healed, they were healed; he saved them from dying.


## Psalms 107:21 (id: 1019107021)

21They should praise Yahweh for loving them faithfully and for the wonderful things that he does for people.


## Psalms 107:22 (id: 1019107022)

22They should give offerings to him to show that they are thankful, and they should sing joyfully about the miracles that he has performed.


## Psalms 107:23 (id: 1019107023)

23Some of them sailed in ships; they were selling things in cities far away.


## Psalms 107:24 (id: 1019107024)

24As they were sailing, they also saw the miracles that Yahweh performed, the wonderful things that he did when they were on very deep seas.


## Psalms 107:25 (id: 1019107025)

25He gave orders to the winds, and they became strong and stirred up high waves.


## Psalms 107:26 (id: 1019107026)

26The ships in which they were sailing were tossed high in the air, and then they sank into the troughs between the high waves; then the sailors were terrified at the danger.


## Psalms 107:27 (id: 1019107027)

27They stumbled about and staggered like drunken men, and they did not know what to do.


## Psalms 107:28 (id: 1019107028)

28When they were in trouble, they called out to Yahweh, and he rescued them from being distressed.


## Psalms 107:29 (id: 1019107029)

29He calmed the storm and he stilled the waves.


## Psalms 107:30 (id: 1019107030)

30They were very glad when it became calm; and Yahweh brought them safely into a harbor as they wished.


## Psalms 107:31 (id: 1019107031)

31They should praise Yahweh for loving them faithfully and for the wonderful things that he does for people.


## Psalms 107:32 (id: 1019107032)

32They should praise him among the Israelite people when they have gathered together, and they should praise him in front of the leaders of the country.


## Psalms 107:33 (id: 1019107033)

33Sometimes Yahweh causes rivers to become dry, with the result that the land becomes a wilderness, and springs of water become dry land.


## Psalms 107:34 (id: 1019107034)

34Sometimes he causes land that has produced lots of crops to become salty wastelands, with the result that they do not produce crops. He does that because the people who live there are very wicked.


## Psalms 107:35 (id: 1019107035)

35But sometimes he causes pools of water to appear in deserts, and he causes springs to flow in very dry ground.


## Psalms 107:36 (id: 1019107036)

36He brings hungry people into that land, to live there and to build cities there.


## Psalms 107:37 (id: 1019107037)

37They plant seeds in their fields, and they plant grapevines that produce large crops of grapes.


## Psalms 107:38 (id: 1019107038)

38He blesses the people, and the women give birth to many children, and they have large herds of cattle.


## Psalms 107:39 (id: 1019107039)

39When the number of people became smaller and they were humiliated by their enemies by being oppressed and caused to suffer,


## Psalms 107:40 (id: 1019107040)

40Yahweh shows contempt for the leaders who oppress them, and makes them to wander in a wilderness where there are no roads.


## Psalms 107:41 (id: 1019107041)

41But he rescues poor people from being in misery and causes their families to increase in number like flocks of sheep.


## Psalms 107:42 (id: 1019107042)

42People who live rightly see God do these things, and they rejoice; wicked people hear about these things, too, but they have nothing to say against Yahweh in reply.


## Psalms 107:43 (id: 1019107043)

43Those who are wise should think carefully about these things; they should consider all the things that Yahweh has done to show that he faithfully loves them.


## Psalms 108:1 (id: 1019108001)

1A psalm written by David; God, I am very confident in you. I will sing to praise you. It is an honor to wake up and praise you.


## Psalms 108:2 (id: 1019108002)

2I will arise before the sun rises, and I will praise you while I play my harp and my lyre.


## Psalms 108:3 (id: 1019108003)

3I prayed, “Yahweh, I will thank you among all the people groups; I will sing to praise you among the nations


## Psalms 108:4 (id: 1019108004)

4because your faithful love for us reaches up to the heavens, and you are as faithful in keeping your promises as the clouds are high above the earth.


## Psalms 108:5 (id: 1019108005)

5Yahweh, show in the heavens that you are very great! Show your glory to people all over the earth!


## Psalms 108:6 (id: 1019108006)

6Answer our prayers and, by your power help us to defeat our enemies so that we, the people whom you love, may be saved.”


## Psalms 108:7 (id: 1019108007)

7Yahweh answered our prayers and spoke from his temple, saying, “Because I have conquered your enemies, I will joyfully divide the city of Shechem, and I will distribute among my people the land in the Valley of Succoth.


## Psalms 108:8 (id: 1019108008)

8The region of Gilead is mine; the people of the tribe of Manasseh are mine; and the tribe of Judah is like my scepter.


## Psalms 108:9 (id: 1019108009)

9The region of Moab is like my washbasin; I throw my sandal over the region of Edom to show that it belongs to me; I shout triumphantly because I have defeated the people of the region of Philistia.”


## Psalms 108:10 (id: 1019108010)

10Because we want to attack the people of Edom, who will lead my army to their capital city that has strong walls around it?


## Psalms 108:11 (id: 1019108011)

11God, we do not want you to abandon us; we want you to go with us when our army marches out to fight our enemies.


## Psalms 108:12 (id: 1019108012)

12We need you to help us when we fight against our enemies because the help that humans can give us is worthless.


## Psalms 108:13 (id: 1019108013)

13But with you helping us, we shall win; you will enable us to defeat our enemies.


## Psalms 109:1 (id: 1019109001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director. God, you are the one whom I praise, so please answer my prayer


## Psalms 109:2 (id: 1019109002)

2because wicked people slander me and tell lies about me.


## Psalms 109:3 (id: 1019109003)

3They are constantly saying that they hate me, and they harm me for no reason.


## Psalms 109:4 (id: 1019109004)

4I show them that I love them and that I pray for them, but instead of being kind to me, they say that I have done evil things.


## Psalms 109:5 (id: 1019109005)

5In return for my doing good things for them and loving them, they do evil things to me and hate me.


## Psalms 109:6 (id: 1019109006)

6So appoint a wicked judge who will judge my enemy, and bring in one of his enemies who will stand up and accuse him.


## Psalms 109:7 (id: 1019109007)

7When the trial ends, cause the judge to declare that he is guilty and cause even his plea for mercy to be considered a sin.


## Psalms 109:8 (id: 1019109008)

8Then cause him to die soon; bring someone else to take over his work.


## Psalms 109:9 (id: 1019109009)

9Cause his children not to have a father anymore, and cause his wife to become a widow.


## Psalms 109:10 (id: 1019109010)

10Cause his children to leave the ruined homes that they have been living in and to wander around begging for food.


## Psalms 109:11 (id: 1019109011)

11Cause all the people to whom he owed money to seize his property; cause strangers to take away everything that he worked to acquire.


## Psalms 109:12 (id: 1019109012)

12Make sure that no one acts with any loyalty toward his memory for the sake of your covenant; make sure that no one pities his children.


## Psalms 109:13 (id: 1019109013)

13Cause all his children to die, so that no one will live to carry on his name.


## Psalms 109:14 (id: 1019109014)

14Yahweh, remember and do not forgive his ancestors for the evil things that they did, and do not even forgive the sins that his mother committed.


## Psalms 109:15 (id: 1019109015)

15Think about his sins continually, but cause everyone living to completely forget who he was.


## Psalms 109:16 (id: 1019109016)

16I pray these things because that man, my enemy, never acted toward anyone as your covenant says we must; he persecuted poor and needy people and even killed helpless people.


## Psalms 109:17 (id: 1019109017)

17He liked to curse people. So those terrible things that he requested to happen to others—cause them to happen to him! He did not want to bless others, so make sure that no one blesses him!


## Psalms 109:18 (id: 1019109018)

18He often cursed other people, also; cause the terrible things that he wanted to happen to others to happen to him and enter his body as water does, as olive oil soaks into a person’s bones when it is rubbed on his skin.


## Psalms 109:19 (id: 1019109019)

19Cause those terrible things to cling to him like his clothes and be around him like the belt that he wears every day.


## Psalms 109:20 (id: 1019109020)

20Yahweh, I wish that you will punish all my enemies that way, those who say evil things about me.


## Psalms 109:21 (id: 1019109021)

21But Yahweh, my God, do good things for me in order that I may honor you; rescue me from my enemies because you faithfully love me as you promised.


## Psalms 109:22 (id: 1019109022)

22I request you to do this because I am poor and needy and my inner being is full of pain.


## Psalms 109:23 (id: 1019109023)

23I think that my time to remain alive is as short as an evening shadow that will soon disappear. I will be blown away as a locust is blown by the wind.


## Psalms 109:24 (id: 1019109024)

24My knees are weak because I have fasted very often, and my body has become very thin.


## Psalms 109:25 (id: 1019109025)

25The people who accuse me make fun of me; when they see me, they insult me by shaking their heads at me.


## Psalms 109:26 (id: 1019109026)

26Yahweh, my God, help me! Because you faithfully love me, rescue me!


## Psalms 109:27 (id: 1019109027)

27When you save me, cause my enemies to know that you are the one who has done it!


## Psalms 109:28 (id: 1019109028)

28They may curse me, but I ask that you bless me. Cause those who persecute me to be defeated and disgraced, but cause me to be glad!


## Psalms 109:29 (id: 1019109029)

29Cause those who accuse me to be completely disgraced; cause other people to see that they are disgraced as easily as they see the clothes that they wear!


## Psalms 109:30 (id: 1019109030)

30But I will thank Yahweh very much; I will praise him when I am among the crowd of people who are worshiping him.


## Psalms 109:31 (id: 1019109031)

31I will do that because he defends poor people like me and because he saves us from those who have said that we must die.


## Psalms 110:1 (id: 1019110001)

1A psalm written by David. Yahweh said to my lord the king, “Sit here, close to me, in the place of highest honor until I completely defeat your enemies and make them like a stool for your feet!”


## Psalms 110:2 (id: 1019110002)

2Yahweh will extend your power as king from Jerusalem to other lands; you will rule over all your enemies.


## Psalms 110:3 (id: 1019110003)

3On the day that you lead your armies into battle, many of your people will volunteer to join your army. Your youthful strength will act for you like the dew that waters the earth early in the morning.”


## Psalms 110:4 (id: 1019110004)

4Yahweh has made a solemn promise and he will never change his mind; he has said to the king, “You will be a priest forever like Melchizedek.”


## Psalms 110:5 (id: 1019110005)

5The Lord stands at your right side; when he becomes angry, he will defeat many kings.


## Psalms 110:6 (id: 1019110006)

6He will judge and punish the people of many nations; many bodies of the killed enemy soldiers will lie on the ground. He will crush kings all over the earth.


## Psalms 110:7 (id: 1019110007)

7But the king will drink from the stream alongside the road; he will be refreshed after defeating his enemies.


## Psalms 111:1 (id: 1019111001)

1Praise Yahweh! I will thank Yahweh with my entire inner being every time that those who do what is right come together.


## Psalms 111:2 (id: 1019111002)

2The things that Yahweh has done are wonderful! All those who are delighted with those things desire to study them.


## Psalms 111:3 (id: 1019111003)

3Because he is a great king and does wonderful things, people greatly honor him and respect him; the righteous things that he does will endure forever.


## Psalms 111:4 (id: 1019111004)

4He has done wonderful things that people will always remember; Yahweh always acts kindly and mercifully.


## Psalms 111:5 (id: 1019111005)

5He provides food for those who have an awesome respect for him; he never forgets the covenant that he made with our ancestors.


## Psalms 111:6 (id: 1019111006)

6By enabling his people to capture the lands that belonged to other people groups, he has shown to us, his people, that he is very powerful.


## Psalms 111:7 (id: 1019111007)

7He does everything fairly, as he has promised us, and we can depend on him to help us when he commands us to do things.


## Psalms 111:8 (id: 1019111008)

8What he commands must be obeyed forever; and he acted in a true and righteous manner when he gave us those commands.


## Psalms 111:9 (id: 1019111009)

9He rescued us, his people, from being slaves in Egypt, and he made a covenant with us that will last forever. He is holy and awesome!


## Psalms 111:10 (id: 1019111010)

10Having an awesome respect for Yahweh is the way to become wise. All those who obey his commands will know what is good for them to decide to do. We should praise him forever!


## Psalms 112:1 (id: 1019112001)

1Praise Yahweh! How fortunate are those who have an awesome respect for him, those who happily obey his commands.


## Psalms 112:2 (id: 1019112002)

2Their children will prosper in their land; God will bless their descedants.


## Psalms 112:3 (id: 1019112003)

3Their families will be wealthy, and their righteous deeds will endure forever.


## Psalms 112:4 (id: 1019112004)

4For those who honor God, it is as if a light were shining on them in the darkness, on those who are kind, merciful and righteous.


## Psalms 112:5 (id: 1019112005)

5Things will go well for those who generously lend money to others and who conduct their businesses honestly.


## Psalms 112:6 (id: 1019112006)

6Righteous people will not be overwhelmed because of their troubles; other people will always treasure their memories of them.


## Psalms 112:7 (id: 1019112007)

7They are not afraid when they receive bad news; they confidently trust in Yahweh.


## Psalms 112:8 (id: 1019112008)

8They are confident and not afraid because they know that they will see God defeat their enemies.


## Psalms 112:9 (id: 1019112009)

9They give things generously to poor people; their kind deeds will endure forever, and they will be exalted and honored.


## Psalms 112:10 (id: 1019112010)

10Wicked people see those things and are angry; they gnash their teeth angrily, but they will disappear and die. The wicked things that they want to do will never happen.


## Psalms 113:1 (id: 1019113001)

1Praise Yahweh! You people who serve Yahweh, praise him! Praise him!


## Psalms 113:2 (id: 1019113002)

2Everyone should praise Yahweh now and forever!


## Psalms 113:3 (id: 1019113003)

3People who live in the east and people who live in the west, everyone, should praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 113:4 (id: 1019113004)

4Yahweh rules over all the nations, and high in the heavens he shows that his glory is very great.


## Psalms 113:5 (id: 1019113005)

5There is no one who is like Yahweh, our God, who lives in the highest heaven


## Psalms 113:6 (id: 1019113006)

6and looks far down through the heavens and sees the people on the earth.


## Psalms 113:7 (id: 1019113007)

7He lifts poor people up so that they no longer sit in the dirt; he lifts needy people up so that they no longer sit on heaps of ashes


## Psalms 113:8 (id: 1019113008)

8and causes them to be honored by sitting next to leaders, leaders who rule his own people.


## Psalms 113:9 (id: 1019113009)

9He also enables women who have no children to live in their houses as happy as mothers with children. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 114:1 (id: 1019114001)

1When the Israelite people left Egypt, when the descendants of Jacob left people who spoke a foreign language,


## Psalms 114:2 (id: 1019114002)

2the land of Judah became the place where people worshiped God; and Israel became the land that he ruled over.


## Psalms 114:3 (id: 1019114003)

3When they came to the Sea of Reeds, it was as though the water saw them and ran away! When they came to the Jordan River, the water in the river stopped flowing so that the Israelites could cross it.


## Psalms 114:4 (id: 1019114004)

4When they came to Mount Sinai and there was a big earthquake, it was as though the mountains skipped like goats and the hills jumped around like lambs.


## Psalms 114:5 (id: 1019114005)

5If someone asks, “What happened at the Sea of Reeds that caused the water to run away? What happened that caused the water in the Jordan River to stop flowing?


## Psalms 114:6 (id: 1019114006)

6What happened that caused the mountains to skip like goats and caused the hills to jump around like lambs?”


## Psalms 114:7 (id: 1019114007)

7Indeed, all the earth will tremble before the Lord! Everyone will tremble in the presence of the God whom Jacob worshiped!


## Psalms 114:8 (id: 1019114008)

8He is the one who caused pools of water to flow from a rock for the Israelite people to drink, and he is the one who caused a spring to flow from a solid rock cliff!


## Psalms 115:1 (id: 1019115001)

1A psalm written by David; Yahweh, people should praise you alone; they must praise you, not us, because you faithfully love us and always do what you have promised to do.


## Psalms 115:2 (id: 1019115002)

2It is not right that other people groups should say about us, “They claim that their God is very powerful, but if that is true, why does he not help them?”


## Psalms 115:3 (id: 1019115003)

3Our God is in heaven, and he does whatever he wants!


## Psalms 115:4 (id: 1019115004)

4But their idols are only statues made of silver and gold, things that humans have made.


## Psalms 115:5 (id: 1019115005)

5Their idols have mouths, but they cannot say anything; they have eyes, but they cannot see anything.


## Psalms 115:6 (id: 1019115006)

6They have ears, but they cannot hear anything; they have noses, but they cannot smell anything.


## Psalms 115:7 (id: 1019115007)

7They have hands, but they cannot feel anything; they have feet, but they cannot walk, and they cannot even make any sounds in their throats!


## Psalms 115:8 (id: 1019115008)

8The people who make those idols are as powerless as those idols, and those who trust in those idols can accomplish nothing, just like their idols!


## Psalms 115:9 (id: 1019115009)

9You, my fellow Israelite people, trust in Yahweh! He is the one who helps you and protects you like a shield.


## Psalms 115:10 (id: 1019115010)

10You priests, descendants of Aaron, trust in Yahweh! He is the one who helps you and protects you like a shield.


## Psalms 115:11 (id: 1019115011)

11All you who have a reverential respect for Yahweh, trust in him! He is the one who helps you and protects you like a shield.


## Psalms 115:12 (id: 1019115012)

12Yahweh has not forgotten us; he will bless us Israelite people! He will bless the priests,


## Psalms 115:13 (id: 1019115013)

13and he will bless all those who have a reverential respect for him; he will bless important people and people who are considered to be unimportant, everyone!


## Psalms 115:14 (id: 1019115014)

14I wish that Yahweh may give many children to you, my fellow Israelite people, and to your descendants.


## Psalms 115:15 (id: 1019115015)

15I wish that Yahweh, the one who made heaven and the earth, may bless all of you!


## Psalms 115:16 (id: 1019115016)

16The highest heavens belong to Yahweh, but he gave everything that is on the earth to us people.


## Psalms 115:17 (id: 1019115017)

17Dead people are not able to praise Yahweh; when they descend into the place where dead people are, they are unable to speak and cannot praise him.


## Psalms 115:18 (id: 1019115018)

18But we who are alive will thank him, now and forever. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 116:1 (id: 1019116001)

1I love Yahweh because he hears me when I cry to him for help.


## Psalms 116:2 (id: 1019116002)

2He listens to me, so I will call out to him all during my life.


## Psalms 116:3 (id: 1019116003)

3Everything around me caused me to think that I would die; I was very afraid that I would die and go to the place where dead people are. I was very distressed and afraid.


## Psalms 116:4 (id: 1019116004)

4But then I called out to Yahweh, saying, “Yahweh, I plead with you to save me!”


## Psalms 116:5 (id: 1019116005)

5Yahweh is kind and does what is right; he is our God, and he acts mercifully to us.


## Psalms 116:6 (id: 1019116006)

6He protects those who are helpless; when I thought that I would die, he saved me.


## Psalms 116:7 (id: 1019116007)

7I must encourage myself because Yahweh has done very good things for me.


## Psalms 116:8 (id: 1019116008)

8Yahweh has saved me from dying and has kept me from troubles that would cause me to cry. He has kept me from disaster.


## Psalms 116:9 (id: 1019116009)

9So here on the earth where people are still alive, I live, knowing that Yahweh is directing me.


## Psalms 116:10 (id: 1019116010)

10I continued to believe in Yahweh, even when I said, “I am greatly afflicted.”


## Psalms 116:11 (id: 1019116011)

11Even when I was distressed and said, “I cannot trust anyone,” I continued to trust in Yahweh.


## Psalms 116:12 (id: 1019116012)

12So now I will tell you what I will offer to Yahweh because of all the good things that he has done for me.


## Psalms 116:13 (id: 1019116013)

13I will offer to him a cup of wine to thank him for saving me.


## Psalms 116:14 (id: 1019116014)

14When I am together with many people who belong to Yahweh, I will give to him the offerings that I solemnly promised to give to him.


## Psalms 116:15 (id: 1019116015)

15Yahweh is very grieved when one of his people dies.


## Psalms 116:16 (id: 1019116016)

16I am one of those who serves Yahweh; I serve him like my mother did. He has ended my troubles.


## Psalms 116:17 (id: 1019116017)

17So I will offer to him a sacrifice to thank him, and I will pray to him.


## Psalms 116:18 (id: 1019116018)

18(18\-19\) When I am together with many of the people who belong to Yahweh in the courtyard outside his temple in Jerusalem, I will give to him the offerings that I solemnly promised to give to him. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 117:1 (id: 1019117001)

1You people of all nations, praise Yahweh! All you people groups, praise him


## Psalms 117:2 (id: 1019117002)

2because he faithfully loves us as he promised to do, and he will forever do for us what he promised that he would do. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 118:1 (id: 1019118001)

1Tell Yahweh that you thank him very much for the good things that he has done for you! He faithfully loves us, his people, forever.


## Psalms 118:2 (id: 1019118002)

2You Israelite people should repeatedly shout, “He faithfully loves us, his people, forever!”


## Psalms 118:3 (id: 1019118003)

3You priests who are descendants of Aaron should repeatedly shout, “He faithfully loves us, his people, forever!”


## Psalms 118:4 (id: 1019118004)

4All you who revere him should repeatedly shout, “He faithfully loves us, his people, forever!”


## Psalms 118:5 (id: 1019118005)

5When I was distressed, I called out to Yahweh, and he answered me and set me free from my worries.


## Psalms 118:6 (id: 1019118006)

6Yahweh is on my side, so I will not be afraid of anything. No one can do anything that will prevent God from blessing me forever.


## Psalms 118:7 (id: 1019118007)

7Yes, Yahweh is on my side, so I will look triumphantly at my enemies while he defeats them.


## Psalms 118:8 (id: 1019118008)

8It is better to trust in Yahweh than to depend on people.


## Psalms 118:9 (id: 1019118009)

9It is better to trust Yahweh to protect us than to trust that influential people will protect us.


## Psalms 118:10 (id: 1019118010)

10Armies of many nations surrounded us, but Yahweh enabled us to defeat them by his power.


## Psalms 118:11 (id: 1019118011)

11They completely surrounded us, but we defeated them all by Yahweh’s power.


## Psalms 118:12 (id: 1019118012)

12They swarmed around me like angry bees; they were like a fire that flares up in a thornbush, but we defeated them by Yahweh’s power.


## Psalms 118:13 (id: 1019118013)

13Our enemies attacked us fiercely and almost defeated us, but Yahweh helped us.


## Psalms 118:14 (id: 1019118014)

14Yahweh is the one who makes me strong, and he is the one about whom I always sing; he has saved us from my enemies.


## Psalms 118:15 (id: 1019118015)

15Listen to the joyful songs of victory being sung in the tents of the people who honor God! They sing, “Yahweh has defeated our enemies by his mighty power;


## Psalms 118:16 (id: 1019118016)

16he has raised his strong right arm to show he is happy over defeating his enemies. Yahweh has completely defeated them!”


## Psalms 118:17 (id: 1019118017)

17I will not be killed in battle; I will live to proclaim the great things that Yahweh has done.


## Psalms 118:18 (id: 1019118018)

18Yahweh has punished me severely, but he has not allowed me to die.


## Psalms 118:19 (id: 1019118019)

19You gatekeepers, open for me the gates of the temple so that I may enter and thank Yahweh.


## Psalms 118:20 (id: 1019118020)

20Those are the gates through which we enter the temple to worship Yahweh; those who honor God enter through those gates.


## Psalms 118:21 (id: 1019118021)

21Yahweh, I thank you that you answered my prayer and that you saved me from my enemies.


## Psalms 118:22 (id: 1019118022)

22Yahweh’s chosen king is like a stone that the builders rejected when they were building a house, but that stone became the cornerstone.


## Psalms 118:23 (id: 1019118023)

23This was done by Yahweh, and it is a wonderful thing for us to see.


## Psalms 118:24 (id: 1019118024)

24This is the day on which we remember that Yahweh acted powerfully to defeat our enemies; we will rejoice and be glad today.


## Psalms 118:25 (id: 1019118025)

25Yahweh, we plead with you to keep rescuing us from our enemies. Yahweh, please help us accomplish what we want to do.


## Psalms 118:26 (id: 1019118026)

26Yahweh, bless the one who will come with your power. From the temple we bless all of you.


## Psalms 118:27 (id: 1019118027)

27Yahweh is God, and he has caused his light to come to us. Come, bring animal sacrifice and tie it to the horns of the altar.


## Psalms 118:28 (id: 1019118028)

28Yahweh, you are the God whom I worship, and I will praise you! You are my God, and I will tell everyone that you are great!


## Psalms 118:29 (id: 1019118029)

29Thank Yahweh because he does good things for us! He will faithfully love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 119:1 (id: 1019119001)

1How fortunate are those about whom no one can say truthfully that they have done things that are wrong, those who always obey the laws of Yahweh.


## Psalms 119:2 (id: 1019119002)

2How fortunate are those who obey his weighty commands, those who request him with their entire inner beings to help them to do that.


## Psalms 119:3 (id: 1019119003)

3They do not do things that are wrong; they behave as Yahweh wants them to.


## Psalms 119:4 (id: 1019119004)

4Yahweh, you have given us your principles of behavior, and you told us to obey them faithfully.


## Psalms 119:5 (id: 1019119005)

5I want so much to faithfully keep everything that you command.


## Psalms 119:6 (id: 1019119006)

6If I did that, I would not be ashamed when I thought about your commands.


## Psalms 119:7 (id: 1019119007)

7When I learn all of your just regulations, I will praise you with a pure inner being.


## Psalms 119:8 (id: 1019119008)

8I will obey all your statutes; do not desert me!


## Psalms 119:9 (id: 1019119009)

9I know how a young person can live in a pure way; it is by obeying your commands.


## Psalms 119:10 (id: 1019119010)

10I try to serve you with my entire inner being; do not allow me to wander away from what you have commanded.


## Psalms 119:11 (id: 1019119011)

11I have memorized your commands so that I will not sin against you.


## Psalms 119:12 (id: 1019119012)

12Yahweh, I praise you; teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:13 (id: 1019119013)

13I have announced to the people all the things that you have commanded us to do.


## Psalms 119:14 (id: 1019119014)

14I delight in obeying your requirements; I enjoy that more than being very rich.


## Psalms 119:15 (id: 1019119015)

15I will study everything you have commanded, and I will pay attention to how you have shown me to live.


## Psalms 119:16 (id: 1019119016)

16I will be happy to obey your statutes, and I will not forget your words.


## Psalms 119:17 (id: 1019119017)

17Do good things for me, the one who serves you, so that I may continue to live and obey your words during all my life.


## Psalms 119:18 (id: 1019119018)

18Help me to understand with my mind, to know the wonderful things that are written in your laws.


## Psalms 119:19 (id: 1019119019)

19I am living here on the earth for only a short time; do not keep me from understanding.


## Psalms 119:20 (id: 1019119020)

20In my inner being I strongly desire to know your decrees all the time.


## Psalms 119:21 (id: 1019119021)

21You rebuke those who are proud; you curse those who disobey your commands.


## Psalms 119:22 (id: 1019119022)

22Do not allow them to continue to insult and scorn me; I request this because I have obeyed your requirements.


## Psalms 119:23 (id: 1019119023)

23Rulers gather together and plan ways to harm me, but I will meditate on what you have commanded.


## Psalms 119:24 (id: 1019119024)

24I am delighted with your requirements; it is as though they were my advisors.


## Psalms 119:25 (id: 1019119025)

25I think that I will soon die; save my life as you have promised me that you would.


## Psalms 119:26 (id: 1019119026)

26When I told you about all the things I did, you answered me; teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:27 (id: 1019119027)

27Help me to understand how you want me to behave, and then I will meditate on your amazing instructions.


## Psalms 119:28 (id: 1019119028)

28I am very sad, with the result that I have no strength; enable me to be strong again as you promised me that you would do.


## Psalms 119:29 (id: 1019119029)

29Prevent me from telling lies, and be kind to me by teaching me your laws.


## Psalms 119:30 (id: 1019119030)

30I have decided that I will faithfully obey you; I am determined to follow your commands.


## Psalms 119:31 (id: 1019119031)

31Yahweh, I try to carefully cling to your requirements; do not abandon me or let me be disgraced.


## Psalms 119:32 (id: 1019119032)

32I will eagerly obey your commands because you have helped me understand better and better what you want me to do.


## Psalms 119:33 (id: 1019119033)

33Yahweh, teach me the meaning of your statutes, and then I will completely obey them.


## Psalms 119:34 (id: 1019119034)

34Help me to understand your laws so that I may obey them with all my inner being.


## Psalms 119:35 (id: 1019119035)

35I am happy with your commands, so lead me along the paths that you have chosen for me.


## Psalms 119:36 (id: 1019119036)

36Cause me to want to do what you command and not to want to become rich.


## Psalms 119:37 (id: 1019119037)

37Do not allow me to look at things that are worthless; make me able to live as you want me to live.


## Psalms 119:38 (id: 1019119038)

38Because I am one who serves you, do what you promised to do for me, which is what you also promise to do for all those who honor you.


## Psalms 119:39 (id: 1019119039)

39I become afraid when my enemies insult me; stop them! But you are right when you punish my enemies.


## Psalms 119:40 (id: 1019119040)

40I very much desire to obey your principles of behavior; because you are righteous, allow me to continue to live.


## Psalms 119:41 (id: 1019119041)

41Yahweh, show me that you faithfully love me, and rescue me as you promised you would.


## Psalms 119:42 (id: 1019119042)

42After you do that, I will be able to reply to those who insult me because I trust in your word.


## Psalms 119:43 (id: 1019119043)

43Never prevent me from speaking your truth because I have confidence in your regulations.


## Psalms 119:44 (id: 1019119044)

44I will always obey your laws forever and ever.


## Psalms 119:45 (id: 1019119045)

45I will always be safe because I have tried to obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:46 (id: 1019119046)

46I will tell to kings what you require, and because they are unable to prove me wrong, they will not cause me to be ashamed.


## Psalms 119:47 (id: 1019119047)

47I am delighted to obey your commands, and I love them.


## Psalms 119:48 (id: 1019119048)

48I respect your commandments, and I love them; I will meditate on everything you require us to do.


## Psalms 119:49 (id: 1019119049)

49Do not forget what you said you would do for me, the one who serves you, because what you have said has caused me to confidently expect good things from you.


## Psalms 119:50 (id: 1019119050)
