50When I have been suffering, you comforted me; you did what you promised me, and that kept me alive.


## Psalms 119:51 (id: 1019119051)

51Proud people are always making fun of me, but I do not turn away from obeying your laws.


## Psalms 119:52 (id: 1019119052)

52Yahweh, when I think about your regulations that you gave to us long ago, I am comforted.


## Psalms 119:53 (id: 1019119053)

53When I see wicked people disregard your laws, I become very angry.


## Psalms 119:54 (id: 1019119054)

54While I have been living here on the earth for a short time, I have written songs about your statutes.


## Psalms 119:55 (id: 1019119055)

55Yahweh, during the night I think about you, and so I obey your laws.


## Psalms 119:56 (id: 1019119056)

56What I have always done is to obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:57 (id: 1019119057)

57Yahweh, you are the one whom I have chosen, and I promise to obey your words.


## Psalms 119:58 (id: 1019119058)

58With all my inner being I plead with you to be good to me; act kindly to me as you promised that you would do.


## Psalms 119:59 (id: 1019119059)

59I have thought about my behavior, and I have decided to return to obeying your requirements.


## Psalms 119:60 (id: 1019119060)

60I hurry to obey your commands; I do not delay at all.


## Psalms 119:61 (id: 1019119061)

61Wicked people have tried to seize me as a hunter tries to catch an animal with a net, but I do not forget your laws.


## Psalms 119:62 (id: 1019119062)

62In the middle of the night I awake, and I praise you for your commands because they are fair.


## Psalms 119:63 (id: 1019119063)

63I am a friend of all those who have an awesome respect for you, those who obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:64 (id: 1019119064)

64Yahweh, you faithfully love people all over the earth; teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:65 (id: 1019119065)

65Yahweh, you have done good things for me as you promised that you would do.


## Psalms 119:66 (id: 1019119066)

66Teach me to think carefully before I decide what to do, and teach me other things that I need to know because I believe that it is right for us to obey your commands.


## Psalms 119:67 (id: 1019119067)

67Before you afflicted me, I did things that were wrong, but now I obey your words.


## Psalms 119:68 (id: 1019119068)

68You are very good, and what you do is good; teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:69 (id: 1019119069)

69Proud people have told many lies about me, but as for me, I obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:70 (id: 1019119070)

70Those people are stubborn, but as for me, I am delighted with your laws.


## Psalms 119:71 (id: 1019119071)

71It was good for me that you afflicted me because the result was that I learned your statutes.


## Psalms 119:72 (id: 1019119072)

72The laws that you give to us are worth more to me than gold, more than thousands of pieces of gold and silver.


## Psalms 119:73 (id: 1019119073)

73You created me and formed my body; help me to be wise so that I may learn your commands.


## Psalms 119:74 (id: 1019119074)

74Those who have an awesome respect for you will see what you have done for me, because they have confidence in the promises of your word.


## Psalms 119:75 (id: 1019119075)

75Yahweh, I know that your regulations are right and that you have made me suffer because you love me without end.


## Psalms 119:76 (id: 1019119076)

76Comfort me by showing that you faithfully love me as you said to me that you would do.


## Psalms 119:77 (id: 1019119077)

77Act mercifully to me so that I may continue to live because I am delighted with your laws.


## Psalms 119:78 (id: 1019119078)

78Cause the proud people who falsely accuse me to be shamed; but as for me, I will continue meditating on what you have commanded I should do.


## Psalms 119:79 (id: 1019119079)

79Cause those who have an awesome respect for you to come back to me so that they may learn what you command.


## Psalms 119:80 (id: 1019119080)

80Enable me to perfectly obey your statutes so that I may not be ashamed because of not doing that.


## Psalms 119:81 (id: 1019119081)

81I am waiting for you to save me from my enemies; I confidently expect that you will tell me what you will do.


## Psalms 119:82 (id: 1019119082)

82My eyes are tired from waiting a long time for you to do what you promised that you would do, and I ask, “When will you help me?”


## Psalms 119:83 (id: 1019119083)

83I have become as useless as a wineskin that is shriveled from hanging a long time in the smoke inside a house, but I have not forgotten your statutes.


## Psalms 119:84 (id: 1019119084)

84How long must I wait? When will you punish those who persecute me?


## Psalms 119:85 (id: 1019119085)

85It is as though proud people, those who do not obey your laws, have dug deep pits for me to fall into.


## Psalms 119:86 (id: 1019119086)

86All your commands are trustworthy; but people are persecuting me by telling lies about me, so please help me.


## Psalms 119:87 (id: 1019119087)

87Those people almost killed me, but I have not stopped obeying your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:88 (id: 1019119088)

88Because you faithfully love me, allow me to continue to live so that I may continue to obey your requirements that you have spoken.


## Psalms 119:89 (id: 1019119089)

89Yahweh, your word will last forever; it is firmly fixed in heaven.


## Psalms 119:90 (id: 1019119090)

90You will faithfully continue to act for people who are not yet born; you have put the earth in its place, and it remains firmly there.


## Psalms 119:91 (id: 1019119091)

91To this day, all things on the earth remain because you decided that they should remain; everything on the earth serves you.


## Psalms 119:92 (id: 1019119092)

92If I had not been delighted in obeying your laws, I would have died because of what I was suffering.


## Psalms 119:93 (id: 1019119093)

93I will never forget your principles of behavior because as a result of my obeying them, you have enabled me to continue to live.


## Psalms 119:94 (id: 1019119094)

94I belong to you; save me from my enemies because I have tried to obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:95 (id: 1019119095)

95Wicked men are waiting to kill me, but I will think about your requirements.


## Psalms 119:96 (id: 1019119096)

96I have learned that there is a limit for everything, but your commands have no limit.


## Psalms 119:97 (id: 1019119097)

97I love your laws very much. I meditate on them all during the day.


## Psalms 119:98 (id: 1019119098)

98Because I know your commands and because I think about them all the time, I have become wiser than my enemies.


## Psalms 119:99 (id: 1019119099)

99I understand more than my teachers do because I meditate on what you command.


## Psalms 119:100 (id: 1019119100)

100I understand more than many old people do because I obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:101 (id: 1019119101)

101I have avoided all evil behavior so that I may obey your words.


## Psalms 119:102 (id: 1019119102)

102I have not refused to obey them because you have taught me while I have studied them.


## Psalms 119:103 (id: 1019119103)

103When I read your words, they are like honey that I eat; yes, they are even sweeter than honey.


## Psalms 119:104 (id: 1019119104)

104Because I have learned your principles of behavior, I am able to understand many things; therefore I hate all evil things that some people do.


## Psalms 119:105 (id: 1019119105)

105Your word is a lamp to guide me; it is like a light that shows me where to walk.


## Psalms 119:106 (id: 1019119106)

106I have solemnly promised, and I am solemnly promising it again, that I will always obey your regulations; they are all fair.


## Psalms 119:107 (id: 1019119107)

107Yahweh, I am suffering very much; cause me to be strong again as you have promised to do.


## Psalms 119:108 (id: 1019119108)

108Yahweh, when I thank you while I pray, it is like a sacrifice to you; please accept it, and teach me your regulations.


## Psalms 119:109 (id: 1019119109)

109My enemies are often trying to kill me, but I do not forget your laws.


## Psalms 119:110 (id: 1019119110)

110Wicked people have tried to seize me as a hunter tries to catch little animals with a trap, but I have not disobeyed your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:111 (id: 1019119111)

111I have your requirements forever; because of them, I am joyful in my inner being.


## Psalms 119:112 (id: 1019119112)

112I have decided to always obey your commands, every one of them.


## Psalms 119:113 (id: 1019119113)

113I hate people who only say they love you, but I love your laws.


## Psalms 119:114 (id: 1019119114)

114You are like a place where I can hide from my enemies, and you are like a shield behind which I am protected from them; I trust in your promises.


## Psalms 119:115 (id: 1019119115)

115You evil people, go away from me so than I may obey my God’s commands!


## Psalms 119:116 (id: 1019119116)

116Enable me to be strong as you promised that you would do, so that I may continue to live. I am confidently expecting that you will restore me; do not disappoint me.


## Psalms 119:117 (id: 1019119117)

117Hold me up so that I may be safe and always pay attention to your commands.


## Psalms 119:118 (id: 1019119118)

118You reject all those who disobey your statutes; because they make deceitful plans and they do not keep their word.


## Psalms 119:119 (id: 1019119119)

119You get rid of all the wicked people on the earth as people get rid of trash; therefore I love your requirements.


## Psalms 119:120 (id: 1019119120)

120I tremble because I am afraid of you; I am afraid because you punish those who do not obey your regulations.


## Psalms 119:121 (id: 1019119121)

121But I have done what is right and fair; so do not allow people to oppress me.


## Psalms 119:122 (id: 1019119122)

122Be responsible for doing good things for me, and do not allow proud people to oppress me.


## Psalms 119:123 (id: 1019119123)

123My eyes are tired from waiting a long time for you to rescue me, for you to save me as you promised that you would.


## Psalms 119:124 (id: 1019119124)

124Do something for me to show that you faithfully love me, and teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:125 (id: 1019119125)

125I am one who serves you; enable me to understand what you want me to know so that I may learn your requirements.


## Psalms 119:126 (id: 1019119126)

126Yahweh, now is the time for you to punish people because they have disobeyed your laws.


## Psalms 119:127 (id: 1019119127)

127Truly, I love your commands more than I love gold; I love them more than I love very pure gold.


## Psalms 119:128 (id: 1019119128)

128So I conduct my life by your principles of behavior, and I hate all the evil things that some people do.


## Psalms 119:129 (id: 1019119129)

129Your requirements are wonderful, so I obey them with all my inner being.


## Psalms 119:130 (id: 1019119130)

130When someone explains your words, it is as though they are lighting a light; what they say causes even people who have not learned your laws to be wise.


## Psalms 119:131 (id: 1019119131)

131I eagerly desire to know your commands as a dog pants with its mouth open, wanting to be fed.


## Psalms 119:132 (id: 1019119132)

132Listen to me and act kindly to me as you do to all those who love you.


## Psalms 119:133 (id: 1019119133)

133Guide me as you promised; do not allow evil people to control what I do.


## Psalms 119:134 (id: 1019119134)

134Rescue me from those who oppress me so that I may obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:135 (id: 1019119135)

135Act kindly toward me and teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:136 (id: 1019119136)

136I cry very much because many people do not obey your laws.


## Psalms 119:137 (id: 1019119137)

137Yahweh, you are righteous and your regulations are just.


## Psalms 119:138 (id: 1019119138)

138You did what was right when you gave us the laws of your covenant promise, and you can be trusted when you made those promises to us.


## Psalms 119:139 (id: 1019119139)

139I am furious because my enemies disregard your words.


## Psalms 119:140 (id: 1019119140)

140I have found that your promises are dependable, and I love them.


## Psalms 119:141 (id: 1019119141)

141I am not important, and people despise me, but I do not forget your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:142 (id: 1019119142)

142You are righteous and you will be righteous forever, and your laws will never be changed.


## Psalms 119:143 (id: 1019119143)

143I constantly have troubles and I am worried, but your commands cause me to be happy.


## Psalms 119:144 (id: 1019119144)

144Your requirements are always fair; help me to understand them so that I may continue to live.


## Psalms 119:145 (id: 1019119145)

145Yahweh, with all my inner being I call out to you; answer me and I will obey your statutes.


## Psalms 119:146 (id: 1019119146)

146I call out to you, “Save me, and I will keep your commandments.”


## Psalms 119:147 (id: 1019119147)

147Each morning I arise before dawn and call to you to help me; I confidently expect you to do what you have promised.


## Psalms 119:148 (id: 1019119148)

148All during the night I am awake, and I meditate on your commands and your promises.


## Psalms 119:149 (id: 1019119149)

149Yahweh, because you faithfully love me, listen to me while I pray; keep me safe because I keep your regulations.


## Psalms 119:150 (id: 1019119150)

150Those evil people who oppress me are coming closer to me; they do not pay any attention to your laws.


## Psalms 119:151 (id: 1019119151)

151But Yahweh, you are near to me, and I know that your commands will never be changed.


## Psalms 119:152 (id: 1019119152)

152Long ago I found out about your requirements, and I know that you intended them to last forever.


## Psalms 119:153 (id: 1019119153)

153Look at me, see that I am suffering very much, and heal me because I do not forget your laws.


## Psalms 119:154 (id: 1019119154)

154Defend me when others accuse me and rescue me from them; allow me to continue to live as you promised that you would.


## Psalms 119:155 (id: 1019119155)

155Wicked people do not obey your statutes, so you will certainly not save them.


## Psalms 119:156 (id: 1019119156)

156Yahweh, you have been merciful by helping me in many ways; allow me to continue to live as you have done until now.


## Psalms 119:157 (id: 1019119157)

157Many people are my enemies; many people cause me to suffer, but I do not neglect your commands.


## Psalms 119:158 (id: 1019119158)

158When I look at those who are not faithful to you, I am disgusted because they do not obey your requirements.


## Psalms 119:159 (id: 1019119159)

159Yahweh, notice that I love your principles of behavior; because you faithfully love me, allow me to continue to live.


## Psalms 119:160 (id: 1019119160)

160I can rely on everything that you have said; all your regulations will endure forever.


## Psalms 119:161 (id: 1019119161)

161Rulers persecute me for no reason, but in my inner being I have a very awesome respect for your words.


## Psalms 119:162 (id: 1019119162)

162I am happy about your words, as happy as someone who has found a great treasure.


## Psalms 119:163 (id: 1019119163)

163I thoroughly hate all lies but I love your laws.


## Psalms 119:164 (id: 1019119164)

164I praise you seven times a day for your commandments because they are all just.


## Psalms 119:165 (id: 1019119165)

165Things go well for those who love your laws; nothing will make them abandon your laws.


## Psalms 119:166 (id: 1019119166)

166Yahweh, I confidently expect that you will rescue me from my troubles, and I obey your commands.


## Psalms 119:167 (id: 1019119167)

167I obey what you require us to do; I love it all very much.


## Psalms 119:168 (id: 1019119168)

168I obey your principles of behavior, and you see everything that I do.


## Psalms 119:169 (id: 1019119169)

169Yahweh, listen while I pray for you to help me; help me to understand your words.


## Psalms 119:170 (id: 1019119170)

170Hear me while I pray, and rescue me as you said you would.


## Psalms 119:171 (id: 1019119171)

171I will always praise you because you teach me your rules.


## Psalms 119:172 (id: 1019119172)

172I will sing about your words because all your commands are just.


## Psalms 119:173 (id: 1019119173)

173I request you to always be ready to help me because I have chosen to obey your principles of behavior.


## Psalms 119:174 (id: 1019119174)

174Yahweh, I eagerly desire for you to rescue me from my enemies; I am delighted with your laws.


## Psalms 119:175 (id: 1019119175)

175Allow me to continue to live in order that I can continue to praise you so that your regulations will continue to help me.


## Psalms 119:176 (id: 1019119176)

176I have sinned and turned away from you like a sheep that has left its flock; search for me because I have not forgotten your commands.


## Psalms 120:1 (id: 1019120001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship; I cried out to Yahweh when I was distressed and he responded to me.


## Psalms 120:2 (id: 1019120002)

2{I prayed,} “Yahweh, save me from those who lie to me and try to deceive me!”


## Psalms 120:3 (id: 1019120003)

3You who deceive other people, Yahweh will certainly punish you!


## Psalms 120:4 (id: 1019120004)

4When Yahweh punishes you, it will be as if soldiers were shooting sharp arrows at you as well as throwing hot coals from the wood of a broom tree.


## Psalms 120:5 (id: 1019120005)

5It is terrible for me because {it has been like I have lived far from Israel}. For it was as though I was sojourning in the region of Meshech or living among those who live in the tents of the region of Kedar.


## Psalms 120:6 (id: 1019120006)

6I lived for a long time among people who hate to live with others peacefully.


## Psalms 120:7 (id: 1019120007)

7I want to live with others peacefully. But every time I talk about living together peacefully, they talk about wanting to start a war.


## Psalms 121:1 (id: 1019121001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship; I look up toward the tops of the hills and I think, “Who will help me?”


## Psalms 121:2 (id: 1019121002)

2{Then I remember,} “Yahweh is the one who will help me. He is the one who made the whole world.”


## Psalms 121:3 (id: 1019121003)

3{Then someone said to me,} “God will keep your from being harmed, he will always be ready to protect you.


## Psalms 121:4 (id: 1019121004)

4Surely Yahweh, who protects the Israelites, is always ready to protect you.


## Psalms 121:5 (id: 1019121005)

5Yahweh guards you. He is like the shade of a tree that protects you,


## Psalms 121:6 (id: 1019121006)

6so that the sun will not harm you during the day, and the moon will not harm you during the night.


## Psalms 121:7 (id: 1019121007)

7Yahweh will guard you from all kinds of harm. He will keep you safe.


## Psalms 121:8 (id: 1019121008)

8Yahweh will protect you from the time that you leave your house in the morning until you return to your house in the evening. He will protect you now and he will protect you forever.”


## Psalms 122:1 (id: 1019122001)

1A psalm written by David for people going up to the temple to worship. I was glad when people said to me, “We should go to the temple of Yahweh in Jerusalem!”


## Psalms 122:2 (id: 1019122002)

2O Jerusalem, we are standing inside your gates.


## Psalms 122:3 (id: 1019122003)

3Jerusalem was built to be a city that protects its inhabitants.


## Psalms 122:4 (id: 1019122004)

4It is a city that people who belong to Yahweh can go up to. He has commanded them to do this, so that they can praise him.


## Psalms 122:5 (id: 1019122005)

5In that city are the thrones, from where the kings judged the people, from where the descendants of King David ruled.


## Psalms 122:6 (id: 1019122006)

6Pray that the people of Jerusalem might live peacefully! May the people who love you live prosperously!


## Psalms 122:7 (id: 1019122007)

7May those who live inside of the walls of the city live peacefully. May those who live in the fortresses live securely.


## Psalms 122:8 (id: 1019122008)

8For the sake of my relatives and friends, I will pray that those who live in the city might live peacefully.


## Psalms 122:9 (id: 1019122009)

9And because I love the temple of Yahweh our God, I desire that Yahweh will do good things for the people who live in Jerusalem.


## Psalms 123:1 (id: 1019123001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship; Yahweh, I look up toward you, up to heaven, from where you rule.


## Psalms 123:2 (id: 1019123002)

2As servants ask their masters for what they need and as maids ask their mistresses for what they need, we ask you, Yahweh our God, for what we need, until you act mercifully toward us.


## Psalms 123:3 (id: 1019123003)

3Yahweh, act very mercifully toward us because our enemies have acted very contemptuously toward us.


## Psalms 123:4 (id: 1019123004)

4Arrogant people have made fun of us for a long time, and proud people have oppressed us and have acted as though we were worthless.


## Psalms 124:1 (id: 1019124001)

1A psalm written by David for people going up to the temple to worship. You Israelite people, answer this question: What would have happened to us if Yahweh had not been helping us?


## Psalms 124:2 (id: 1019124002)

2When our enemies attacked us, if Yahweh had not been fighting for us,


## Psalms 124:3 (id: 1019124003)

3we would have all been killed because they were very angry with us!


## Psalms 124:4 (id: 1019124004)

4They would have been like a flood of water sweeping us away; it would have been as though the water had covered us,


## Psalms 124:5 (id: 1019124005)

5and we would all have drowned in the flood.


## Psalms 124:6 (id: 1019124006)

6But we praise Yahweh because he has not allowed our enemies to destroy us.


## Psalms 124:7 (id: 1019124007)

7We have escaped from our enemies as a bird escapes from the trap that hunters have set; it is as though the trap that our enemies set for us was broken and we have escaped from it!


## Psalms 124:8 (id: 1019124008)

8Yahweh is the one who helps us; he is the one who made heaven and the earth.


## Psalms 125:1 (id: 1019125001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship. Those who trust in Yahweh are like Mount Zion, which cannot be shaken or moved out of its place.


## Psalms 125:2 (id: 1019125002)

2As the hills that surround Jerusalem protect it, so Yahweh protects us, his people, and he will protect us forever.


## Psalms 125:3 (id: 1019125003)

3Wicked people should not be allowed to rule over the land where righteous people live. If they did that, those righteous people would think of doing wrong themselves.


## Psalms 125:4 (id: 1019125004)

4Yahweh, do good things to those who do good things to others and to those who sincerely obey your commands.


## Psalms 125:5 (id: 1019125005)

5But when you punish the Israelites who no longer obey you, you will punish them the same as you punish all the other evildoers. I wish that things may go well for people in Israel!


## Psalms 126:1 (id: 1019126001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship. When Yahweh made Jerusalem prosperous again, it was wonderful; it seemed as though we were dreaming.


## Psalms 126:2 (id: 1019126002)

2We were extremely happy, and we continued shouting joyfully. Then the other people groups said about us, “Yahweh has done great things for them!”


## Psalms 126:3 (id: 1019126003)

3We said, “Yes, Yahweh truly has done great things for us, and we are very happy.”


## Psalms 126:4 (id: 1019126004)

4Restore us, O Yahweh, like the rains that fill the streams in the southern Judean wilderness. Enable our nation to become great again like it was before.


## Psalms 126:5 (id: 1019126005)

5We cried when we planted seeds because it was hard work preparing the soil that had not been plowed for many years; now we want to shout joyfully because we are gathering a big harvest.


## Psalms 126:6 (id: 1019126006)

6Those who cried as they carried the bags of seeds to the fields will shout joyfully when they bring the crops to their houses at harvest time.


## Psalms 127:1 (id: 1019127001)

1A psalm written by Solomon for people going up to the temple to worship. If people are building a house without Yahweh helping them, they are building it in vain. Similarly, if Yahweh does not protect a city, it is useless for guards to stay awake at night.


## Psalms 127:2 (id: 1019127002)

2It is also useless to arise very early and go to sleep late at night so that you can work hard all day to earn money to buy food because Yahweh gives food to those whom he loves even while they sleep.


## Psalms 127:3 (id: 1019127003)

3Children are a gift that comes to parents from Yahweh; they are a reward from him.


## Psalms 127:4 (id: 1019127004)

4If a man has sons while he is still young, when they grow up, they will be able to help him defend his family as a soldier can defend himself if he has a bow and arrows in his hand.


## Psalms 127:5 (id: 1019127005)

5How fortunate is a man who has many sons; he is like a soldier who has many arrows in his quiver. If a man with his many grown sons is taken by his enemies to the place where they decide matters, his enemies will never be able to defeat that man because his sons will help to defend him.


## Psalms 128:1 (id: 1019128001)

1A psalm written for those going up to the temple to worship. How fortunate are you who have an awesome respect for him and do what he wants you to do.


## Psalms 128:2 (id: 1019128002)

2You will be able to enjoy the food you provide yourself with; you will be fortunate and prosperous.


## Psalms 128:3 (id: 1019128003)

3Your wife will be like a grapevine that bears many grapes; she will give birth to many children. Your children who sit around your table; you will be like a strong olive tree that has many shoots growing up around it.


## Psalms 128:4 (id: 1019128004)

4Like that, Yahweh will bless every man who has an awesome respect for him.


## Psalms 128:5 (id: 1019128005)

5I wish that God in his temple on Mount Zion may help you greatly, and that you will see the people of Jerusalem prospering every day that you live!


## Psalms 128:6 (id: 1019128006)

6I wish that you may live many years and that you may have grandchildren and be able to see them. I wish that things may go well for people in Israel!


## Psalms 129:1 (id: 1019129001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship. I say that my enemies have afflicted me ever since I was young. Now I ask you, my fellow Israelites, to repeat those same words:


## Psalms 129:2 (id: 1019129002)

2“Our enemies have afflicted us since our nation began, but they have not defeated us!


## Psalms 129:3 (id: 1019129003)

3Our enemies struck us with whips that cut into our backs as a farmer uses a plow to cuts deep furrows into the ground.”


## Psalms 129:4 (id: 1019129004)

4But Yahweh is righteous, and he has freed us from being slaves to wicked people.


## Psalms 129:5 (id: 1019129005)

5I wish that they may all be shamed because we will defeat them—all of Jerusalem’s enemies.


## Psalms 129:6 (id: 1019129006)

6I hope that they may be of no value, like grass that grows on the roofs of houses, that dries up and does not grow tall;


## Psalms 129:7 (id: 1019129007)

7no one wants to cut it and tie it up as bundles and carry it away.


## Psalms 129:8 (id: 1019129008)

8People who pass by and see men harvesting grain usually greet them by saying to them, “We wish that Yahweh may bless you!” But this will not happen to the enemies of Israel. We, acting as Yahweh’s representatives, bless you, our fellow Israelites!


## Psalms 130:1 (id: 1019130001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship. Yahweh, I have great troubles, so I call out to you.


## Psalms 130:2 (id: 1019130002)

2Yahweh, hear me while I call out to you to have mercy on me!


## Psalms 130:3 (id: 1019130003)

3Yahweh, if you kept a record of the sins that we have committed, not one of us would escape from being condemned and punished!


## Psalms 130:4 (id: 1019130004)

4But you forgive us, with the result that we have an awesome respect for you.


## Psalms 130:5 (id: 1019130005)

5Yahweh has said that he would help me; I trust what he said, and I wait eagerly for him to do that.


## Psalms 130:6 (id: 1019130006)

6I wait for Yahweh to help me more than watchmen wait for the morning to come; yes, I wait more eagerly than they do!


## Psalms 130:7 (id: 1019130007)

7You, my fellow Israelites, confidently expect that Yahweh will bless us. He will bless us because he has mercy on us, and he is very willing to save us.


## Psalms 130:8 (id: 1019130008)

8It is he who will save us Israelite people from being punished for all the sins that we have committed.


## Psalms 131:1 (id: 1019131001)

1A psalm written by David for people going up to the temple to worship. Yahweh, I am not proud; I do not deserve to achieve impressive things in life. I do not worry about problems that are too difficult for me to solve.


## Psalms 131:2 (id: 1019131002)

2Instead, I am calm and peaceful in my inner being like a small child who no longer nurses but is happy to be with its mother. In the same way, I am peaceful within my inner being.


## Psalms 131:3 (id: 1019131003)

3You, my fellow Israelites, confidently expect that Yahweh will do good things for you now and forever!


## Psalms 132:1 (id: 1019132001)

1A song to sing along the road up to Jerusalem. Yahweh, do not forget King David and all the hardships he endured!


## Psalms 132:2 (id: 1019132002)

2He made a solemn promise to you, the mighty God whom our ancestor Jacob worshiped.


## Psalms 132:3 (id: 1019132003)

3He said, “I will not go home, I will not rest on my bed,


## Psalms 132:4 (id: 1019132004)

4and I will not sleep at all


## Psalms 132:5 (id: 1019132005)

5until I build a place for Yahweh, a home for the mighty God whom Jacob worshiped.”


## Psalms 132:6 (id: 1019132006)

6In Ephrathah we heard where the sacred chest was. So we went and found it near the city of Kiriath Jearim, and we took it to Jerusalem.


## Psalms 132:7 (id: 1019132007)

7Later we said, “Let us go to the sacred tent of Yahweh in Jerusalem; let us worship there in front of the throne where he is sitting.”


## Psalms 132:8 (id: 1019132008)

8Yahweh, come to the place where you live eternally, to the place where your sacred chest is, to the place that shows that you are very powerful.


## Psalms 132:9 (id: 1019132009)

9I want that the righteous behavior of your priests will always be evident, and that your people will always shout joyfully.


## Psalms 132:10 (id: 1019132010)

10You chose David to serve you as king of Israel; do not reject him!


## Psalms 132:11 (id: 1019132011)

11Yahweh, you made a solemn promise to David, a promise that you will not break. You said, “I will cause your descendants to rule as kings like you.


## Psalms 132:12 (id: 1019132012)

12If they obey my covenant with them and obey all the commands that I will give them, the line of kings descended from you will never end.”


## Psalms 132:13 (id: 1019132013)

13Yahweh has chosen Jerusalem; that is where he wants to rule from.


## Psalms 132:14 (id: 1019132014)

14He said, “This is the city where I will live forever; this is the place where I want to stay.


## Psalms 132:15 (id: 1019132015)

15I will give to the people of Jerusalem all that they need; I will give enough food to satisfy even the poor people there.


## Psalms 132:16 (id: 1019132016)

16I will cause the priests to behave in a manner worthy of ones whom I have saved; and all my people who live there will shout joyfully.


## Psalms 132:17 (id: 1019132017)

17There in Jerusalem I will cause one of David’s descendants to become a great king; he also will be my chosen king, It is there that I will make David’s line of descendants continue.


## Psalms 132:18 (id: 1019132018)

18I will defeat his enemies and cause them to be very ashamed; but the crown that my king wears will always shine.”


## Psalms 133:1 (id: 1019133001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship. It is very good and very pleasant for God’s people to gather together in peace.


## Psalms 133:2 (id: 1019133002)

2It is as delightful as the precious oil that ran down from the high priest Aaron’s head onto his beard when Moses anointed him, that ran down onto the collar of his robes.


## Psalms 133:3 (id: 1019133003)

3Gathering together in peace is as delightful as the dew that falls on Mount Hermon and the dew that falls on Mount Zion. Yahweh has promised to bless his people there in Jerusalem by making their nation last forever.


## Psalms 134:1 (id: 1019134001)

1A psalm written for people going up to the temple to worship. All you people who serve Yahweh, who stand up and serve him at night in his temple, come and praise him!


## Psalms 134:2 (id: 1019134002)

2Lift up your hands to pray to him in the temple and praise him!


## Psalms 134:3 (id: 1019134003)

3I hope that Yahweh, who created heaven and the earth, may bless you from where he lives in the temple on Mount Zion!


## Psalms 135:1 (id: 1019135001)

1Praise Yahweh! You who worship Yahweh, praise him!


## Psalms 135:2 (id: 1019135002)

2You who stand at the temple of Yahweh our God in its courtyards, ready to serve him, praise him !


## Psalms 135:3 (id: 1019135003)

3Praise Yahweh because he does good things for us; sing to him because it is a joyful thing to do so.


## Psalms 135:4 (id: 1019135004)

4He has chosen us, the descendants of Jacob; he has chosen us Israelites to belong to him.


## Psalms 135:5 (id: 1019135005)

5I say these things because I know that Yahweh is great; he is greater than all the gods.


## Psalms 135:6 (id: 1019135006)

6Yahweh does whatever he desires to do in heaven, on the earth, and in the seas, down to the bottom of the seas.


## Psalms 135:7 (id: 1019135007)

7He is the one who causes clouds to appear from very distant places on the earth; he makes lightning bolts to flash with the rain, and he brings the winds from the places where he stores them.


## Psalms 135:8 (id: 1019135008)

8He is the one who killed all the firstborn males in Egypt, the firstborn of people and of animals.


## Psalms 135:9 (id: 1019135009)

9There he performed many kinds of miracles to punish the king and all his officials.


## Psalms 135:10 (id: 1019135010)

10He attacked many nations and killed the powerful kings who ruled them:


## Psalms 135:11 (id: 1019135011)

11Sihon, the king of the Amor people group, Og, the king of Bashan, and all the other kings in the land of Canaan.


## Psalms 135:12 (id: 1019135012)

12Yahweh gave us their land, so that it would belong to us, his people Israel, forever.


## Psalms 135:13 (id: 1019135013)

13Yahweh, your name will endure forever, and people who are not yet born will remember the great things that you have done.


## Psalms 135:14 (id: 1019135014)

14Yahweh declares that we, his people, are innocent, and he acts mercifully toward us.


## Psalms 135:15 (id: 1019135015)

15But the idols that the other people groups worship are only statues made of silver and gold, things that humans have made.


## Psalms 135:16 (id: 1019135016)

16Their idols have mouths, but they cannot say anything; they have eyes, but they cannot see anything.


## Psalms 135:17 (id: 1019135017)

17They have ears, but they cannot hear anything, and they are not even able to breathe.


## Psalms 135:18 (id: 1019135018)

18The people who make those idols are as powerless as those idols, and those who trust in those idols can accomplish no more than their idols can!


## Psalms 135:19 (id: 1019135019)

19My fellow Israelites, praise Yahweh! You priests who are descended from Aaron, praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 135:20 (id: 1019135020)

20You men who are descended from Levi, you who assist the priests, praise Yahweh! All you who have a reverential respect for Yahweh, praise him!


## Psalms 135:21 (id: 1019135021)

21Praise Yahweh in the temple on Mount Zion in Jerusalem where he lives! Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 136:1 (id: 1019136001)

1Thank Yahweh because he does good things for us; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:2 (id: 1019136002)

2Thank God, the one who is greater than all other gods; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:3 (id: 1019136003)

3Thank the Lord who is greater than all other lords; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:4 (id: 1019136004)

4He is the only one who performs great miracles; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:5 (id: 1019136005)

5He is the one who, by being very wise, created the heavens; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:6 (id: 1019136006)

6He is the one who caused the ground to rise up above the deep waters; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:7 (id: 1019136007)

7He is the one who created great lights in the sky; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:8 (id: 1019136008)

8He created the sun to shine in the daytime; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:9 (id: 1019136009)

9He created the moon and stars to shine during the nighttime; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:10 (id: 1019136010)

10He is the one who killed the firstborn males in Egypt; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:11 (id: 1019136011)

11He led the Israelite people out of Egypt; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:12 (id: 1019136012)

12With his strong hand he led them out; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:13 (id: 1019136013)

13He is the one who caused the Sea of Reeds to divide; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:14 (id: 1019136014)

14He enabled the Israelite people to walk through it on dry land; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:15 (id: 1019136015)

15But he caused the king of Egypt and his army to drown in it; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:16 (id: 1019136016)

16He is the one who led his people safely through the wilderness; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:17 (id: 1019136017)

17He killed powerful kings; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:18 (id: 1019136018)

18He killed kings who were famous; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:19 (id: 1019136019)

19He killed Sihon, the king of the Amor people group; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:20 (id: 1019136020)

20He killed Og, the king of the region of Bashan; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:21 (id: 1019136021)

21He gave their lands to us, his people; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:22 (id: 1019136022)

22He gave those lands to us people of Israel, who serve him; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:23 (id: 1019136023)

23He is the one who did not forget about us when our enemies had defeated us; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:24 (id: 1019136024)

24He rescued us from our enemies; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:25 (id: 1019136025)

25He is the one who gives food to all living creatures; he will love us forever as he has promised.


## Psalms 136:26 (id: 1019136026)

26So thank God, who lives in heaven because he will love us forever as he has promised.!


## Psalms 137:1 (id: 1019137001)

1When we had been taken to Babylonia far from Jerusalem, we sat down by the rivers there, and we cried when we thought about the temple on Mount Zion in Jerusalem.


## Psalms 137:2 (id: 1019137002)

2On the willow trees alongside the rivers we hung our harps because we did not want to play them anymore and because we were very sad.


## Psalms 137:3 (id: 1019137003)

3The soldiers who had captured us and taken us to Babylonia forced us to sing for them; they told us to entertain them; they said, “Sing for us one of the songs that you previously sang in Jerusalem!”


## Psalms 137:4 (id: 1019137004)

4But we thought to ourselves, “We are sad because we have been punished by Yahweh and brought to this foreign land; we cannot sing songs about Yahweh while we are here!”


## Psalms 137:5 (id: 1019137005)

5If I forget about Jerusalem, I hope that my right hand will wither so that I will be unable to play my harp!


## Psalms 137:6 (id: 1019137006)

6I hope that I will not be able to sing again if I forget about Jerusalem, if I do not consider that Jerusalem causes me to be more joyful than anything else does.


## Psalms 137:7 (id: 1019137007)

7Yahweh, punish the people of the Edom people group for what they did on the day that the army of Babylon captured Jerusalem. Do not forget that they said, “Tear down all the buildings! Destroy them completely! Leave only the foundations!”


## Psalms 137:8 (id: 1019137008)

8You people of Babylon, you will certainly be destroyed! How fortunate are those who punish you for what you did to us;


## Psalms 137:9 (id: 1019137009)

9How fortunate are those who take your babies and smash them to pieces on the rocks.


## Psalms 138:1 (id: 1019138001)

1A psalm written by David. Yahweh, I thank you with all my inner being. I sing to praise you, even though many people worship idols.


## Psalms 138:2 (id: 1019138002)

2When I look toward your sacred temple, I bow down and thank you because you faithfully love us and do all that you have promised. You have given cause for people everywhere to honor you and what you have said more than anything else.


## Psalms 138:3 (id: 1019138003)

3When I called out to you, you answered me; you enabled me to be strong and brave.


## Psalms 138:4 (id: 1019138004)

4Yahweh, someday all the kings of this earth will praise you because they will have heard what you have said.


## Psalms 138:5 (id: 1019138005)

5They will sing about what you have done; they will sing and say that you are very great.


## Psalms 138:6 (id: 1019138006)

6Yahweh, you are supreme, but you take care of people who are considered to be unimportant. However, you do not show yourself to proud people as faithful.


## Psalms 138:7 (id: 1019138007)

7When I am in the middle of many troubles, you save me. With your hand you rescue me from my enemies who are angry at me.


## Psalms 138:8 (id: 1019138008)

8Yahweh, you will do for me everything that you promised; you faithfully love us forever. Finish what you started to do for us, your Israelite people!


## Psalms 139:1 (id: 1019139001)

1A psalm written by David for the choir director. Yahweh, you have examined what is in my inner being, and you know everything about me.


## Psalms 139:2 (id: 1019139002)

2You know when I sit down and when I stand up. Even though you are far away from me, you know what I am thinking.


## Psalms 139:3 (id: 1019139003)

3From the time that I rise in the morning until I lie down to sleep at night, you know everything that I do.


## Psalms 139:4 (id: 1019139004)

4Yahweh, even before I say anything, you know everything that I am going to say!


## Psalms 139:5 (id: 1019139005)

5You protect me on all sides; you put your hand on me to protect me with your power.


## Psalms 139:6 (id: 1019139006)

6I am not able to understand that you know everything about me. That is too hard for me to really understand.


## Psalms 139:7 (id: 1019139007)

7Where could I go to escape from your Spirit? Where could I go to get away from you?


## Psalms 139:8 (id: 1019139008)

8If I go up to heaven, you will be there. If I lie down in the place where the dead people are, you will be there.


## Psalms 139:9 (id: 1019139009)

9If the sun could carry me across the sky, if I flew west and made a place to live on an island in the ocean,


## Psalms 139:10 (id: 1019139010)

10you would be there also to lead me by your hand, and you would help me.


## Psalms 139:11 (id: 1019139011)

11I could wish for the darkness to hide me, or I could wish for the light around me to become darkness.


## Psalms 139:12 (id: 1019139012)

12But even if that happened, you would still see me. For you the night is as bright as the daytime, because daylight and darkness are no different to you.


## Psalms 139:13 (id: 1019139013)

13You created all the parts of my body; you put the parts of my body together when I was still in my mother’s womb.


## Psalms 139:14 (id: 1019139014)

14I praise you because you made my body very awesomely and wonderfully. Everything that you do is amazing! I certainly know that very well.


## Psalms 139:15 (id: 1019139015)

15When my body was being formed, while it was being put together where no one else could see it, you saw it!


## Psalms 139:16 (id: 1019139016)

16You saw me before I was born. You wrote in your book the number of days that you had decided that I would live. You did that before any of those days had even started!


## Psalms 139:17 (id: 1019139017)

17God, what you think about me is very valuable. There are a huge amount of things that you think about.


## Psalms 139:18 (id: 1019139018)

18If I could count them, I would see that they are more than the grains of sand at the seashore. When I awake, I am still with you.


## Psalms 139:19 (id: 1019139019)

19God, I wish that you would kill the wicked people! I wish that violent men would all leave me.


## Psalms 139:20 (id: 1019139020)

20They say wicked things about you; they slander your name.


## Psalms 139:21 (id: 1019139021)

21Yahweh, I certainly hate those who hate you! I despise those who rebel against you.


## Psalms 139:22 (id: 1019139022)

22I hate them completely, and I consider that they are my enemies.


## Psalms 139:23 (id: 1019139023)

23God, search my inner being; find out what I am thinking!


## Psalms 139:24 (id: 1019139024)

24Find out whether there is anything evil in my inner being, and lead me along the road that leads to my being with you forever.


## Psalms 140:1 (id: 1019140001)

1A psalm written by David. Yahweh, rescue me from being attacked by evil men; even more, keep me safe from being attacked by violent people.


## Psalms 140:2 (id: 1019140002)

2They are always planning to do evil things, and they are always encouraging people to start quarrels.


## Psalms 140:3 (id: 1019140003)

3By what they say, they injure people as poisonous snakes do.


## Psalms 140:4 (id: 1019140004)

4Yahweh, protect me from the power of wicked people. Keep me safe from violent men who plan to ruin me.


## Psalms 140:5 (id: 1019140005)

5It is as though proud people have set a trap for me; it is as though they have spread their nets to catch me; it is as though they have put these things along the road to catch me.


## Psalms 140:6 (id: 1019140006)

6I say to you, “Yahweh, you are my God. Listen to me while I cry out to you to help me.”


## Psalms 140:7 (id: 1019140007)

7Yahweh, my Lord, you are the one who strongly defends me; you have protected me during battles as though you had put a helmet on my head.


## Psalms 140:8 (id: 1019140008)

8Yahweh, do not give to wicked people the things that they desire, and do not allow them to do the evil things that they plan to do.


## Psalms 140:9 (id: 1019140009)

9Do not allow my enemies to become proud; cause the evil things that they say they will do to me to happen to them instead.


## Psalms 140:10 (id: 1019140010)

10Cause burning coals to fall on their heads! Cause them to be thrown into deep pits from which they cannot climb out!


## Psalms 140:11 (id: 1019140011)

11Do not allow those who slander others to succeed; cause evil things to happen to violent men and destroy them!


## Psalms 140:12 (id: 1019140012)

12Yahweh, I know that you will defend those who are oppressed, and that you will do what is just.


## Psalms 140:13 (id: 1019140013)

13Righteous people will surely thank you, and they will live in your presence.


## Psalms 141:1 (id: 1019141001)

1A psalm written by David. Yahweh, I call out to you; please help me quickly! Listen to me when I am calling to you.


## Psalms 141:2 (id: 1019141002)

2Accept my prayer as though it were incense being burned as an offering to you. Accept me while I lift up my hands to pray to you, just as you accept sacrifices that are offered to you in the evening.


## Psalms 141:3 (id: 1019141003)

3Yahweh, do not allow me to say things that are wrong; guard what I say as a sentry guards a door.


## Psalms 141:4 (id: 1019141004)

4Prevent me from wanting to do anything that is wrong and from joining with wicked men when they want to do evil deeds. Do not even allow me to share in eating delightful food with them!


## Psalms 141:5 (id: 1019141005)

5It is all right if righteous people strike me or rebuke me because they are trying to act kindly toward me to teach me to do what is right; if they do that, it will be as if someone honored me by anointing my head with olive oil; but I am always praying that you will punish the wicked because of the wicked deeds that they do.


## Psalms 141:6 (id: 1019141006)

6When their rulers are thrown down from the top of rocky cliffs, they will know that what I am saying here is good.


## Psalms 141:7 (id: 1019141007)

7They will know one day that their bodies will lie scattered on the ground in the place of the dead, just as one scatters clods of earth when he plows a field.


## Psalms 141:8 (id: 1019141008)

8But Yahweh God, I continue to request that you help me. I ask you to protect me; do not allow me to die now!


## Psalms 141:9 (id: 1019141009)

9It is as though people have set traps for me; protect me from falling into those traps. It is as though they have spread nets to catch me; keep me from being caught in those nets.


## Psalms 141:10 (id: 1019141010)

10I wish that wicked people may fall into the traps they have set to catch me while I escape from them.


## Psalms 142:1 (id: 1019142001)

1A psalm that David prayed when he was hiding in a cave. Yahweh, I cry out to you; I plead for you to help me.


## Psalms 142:2 (id: 1019142002)

2I am bringing to you all my problems; I am telling you all my troubles.


## Psalms 142:3 (id: 1019142003)

3When I am very discouraged, you know what I should do. Wherever I walk, it is as though my enemies have hidden traps for me to fall into.


## Psalms 142:4 (id: 1019142004)

4I look around, but there is no one who sees me, no one who will protect me, and no one who cares about what happens to me.


## Psalms 142:5 (id: 1019142005)

5So Yahweh, I cry out to you to help me; you are the one who protects me; you are all that I need while I am alive.


## Psalms 142:6 (id: 1019142006)

6Listen to me while I cry out to you for help because I am very distressed. Rescue me because those who make me suffer are very strong; I cannot escape from them.


## Psalms 142:7 (id: 1019142007)

7Free me from my troubles so that I may thank you. If you do that, when I am with others who live rightly, I will praise you for having been very good to me.


## Psalms 143:1 (id: 1019143001)

1A psalm written by David. Yahweh, hear me while I pray to you! Because you are righteous and because you faithfully do what you have promised, listen to what I am pleading for you to do for me.


## Psalms 143:2 (id: 1019143002)

2I am one who worships you; do not judge me because you do not consider anyone to be completely innocent.


## Psalms 143:3 (id: 1019143003)

3My enemies have pursued me; they have completely defeated me. It is as though they have put me in a dark prison where I have nothing good to hope for.


## Psalms 143:4 (id: 1019143004)

4So I am very discouraged in my inner being; I am very dismayed.


## Psalms 143:5 (id: 1019143005)

5I remember what has happened previously; I meditate on all the things that you have done; I consider all the great deeds that you have performed.


## Psalms 143:6 (id: 1019143006)

6I lift up my hands to you while I pray; I want very much to be with you as much as I would thirst for water in a vast wilderness.


## Psalms 143:7 (id: 1019143007)

7Yahweh, I am very discouraged, so please answer me right now! Do not keep away from me because if you do that, I will soon be among those who descend to where the dead people are.


## Psalms 143:8 (id: 1019143008)

8Every morning cause me to remember that you faithfully love me because I trust in you. I pray to you; show me the things that I should do.


## Psalms 143:9 (id: 1019143009)

9Yahweh, I have gone to you for you to protect me, so rescue me from my enemies.


## Psalms 143:10 (id: 1019143010)

10You are my God; teach me to do what you want me to do. I want your good Spirit to show me the right things to do.


## Psalms 143:11 (id: 1019143011)

11Yahweh, restore me when I am close to dying as you promised to do because you are righteous!


## Psalms 143:12 (id: 1019143012)

12I am one who serves you; so because you faithfully love me as you promised to do, kill my enemies and get rid of all those who oppress me.


## Psalms 144:1 (id: 1019144001)

1Written by David; I praise Yahweh, who is like a huge rock on which I am safe! He trains my hands so that I can use them to fight battles; he trains my fingers so that I can shoot arrows in a war.


## Psalms 144:2 (id: 1019144002)

2He is the one who protects me as he promised; he is like a fortress in which I am safe, he protects me as shields protect soldiers, and he gives me refuge. He defeats other nations and then puts them under my power.


## Psalms 144:3 (id: 1019144003)

3Yahweh, we people are so insignificant! Why do you notice us? It is amazing to me that you pay attention to humans.


## Psalms 144:4 (id: 1019144004)

4The time that we live is as short as a puff of wind; our time to live disappears as a shadow does.


## Psalms 144:5 (id: 1019144005)

5Yahweh, tear open the sky and come down! Touch the mountains so that smoke may pour out from them!


## Psalms 144:6 (id: 1019144006)

6Cause lightning to flash with the result that your enemies will run away! Shoot your arrows at them and cause them to run away in panic.


## Psalms 144:7 (id: 1019144007)

7It is as though my enemies are like a flood around me; reach your hand down from heaven and rescue me from them. They are men from foreign countries


## Psalms 144:8 (id: 1019144008)

8who always tell lies. Even when they swear to tell the truth, they tell lies.


## Psalms 144:9 (id: 1019144009)

9God, I will sing a new song to you, and I will play my ten\-stringed harp while I sing to you.


## Psalms 144:10 (id: 1019144010)

10You enable kings to defeat their enemies; you rescue those who serve you as I did.


## Psalms 144:11 (id: 1019144011)

11So I ask you to save me from being killed by the swords that those evil people carry. Rescue me from the power of those men from foreign countries who always tell lies. Even when they swear to tell the truth, they tell lies.


## Psalms 144:12 (id: 1019144012)

12I wish that our sons may all grow to full adulthood; I wish that our daughters may grow up to be as straight and tall as the pillars that stand in the corners of palaces.


## Psalms 144:13 (id: 1019144013)

13I wish that our barns may be full of many different crops. I wish that the sheep in our fields may give birth to tens of thousands of baby lambs.


## Psalms 144:14 (id: 1019144014)

14I wish that our cattle may give birth to many calves without having any miscarriages or deaths when they are born. I wish that there may not be any time when the people in our streets cry out in distress because foreign armies are invading.


## Psalms 144:15 (id: 1019144015)

15If good things like that happen to a nation, the people will be very fortunate. How fortunate are those who worship Yahweh as God!


## Psalms 145:1 (id: 1019145001)

1A psalm written by David to praise God. My God and King, I will proclaim that you are very great; I will praise you now and forever.


## Psalms 145:2 (id: 1019145002)

2Every day I will praise you; Yes, I will praise you forever.


## Psalms 145:3 (id: 1019145003)

3Yahweh, you are great, and you ought to be praised very much; we cannot fully realize how great you are.


## Psalms 145:4 (id: 1019145004)

4Parents will tell their children the things that you have done; they will tell their children about your mighty deeds.


## Psalms 145:5 (id: 1019145005)

5I will think about how you are very glorious and majestic, and I will meditate on all your wonderful deeds.


## Psalms 145:6 (id: 1019145006)

6People will speak about your powerful and awesome deeds, and I will proclaim that you are very great.


## Psalms 145:7 (id: 1019145007)

7People will remember and proclaim that you are very good to us, and they will sing joyfully that you always act justly.


## Psalms 145:8 (id: 1019145008)

8Yahweh, you act kindly and mercifully toward us; you do not quickly become angry; you faithfully love us very much as you have promised to do.


## Psalms 145:9 (id: 1019145009)

9Yahweh, you are good to everyone, and you act mercifully to everything that you have made.


## Psalms 145:10 (id: 1019145010)

10Yahweh, all the creatures that you made will thank you, and all your people will praise you.


## Psalms 145:11 (id: 1019145011)

11They will tell others that you rule very gloriously as our king and that you are very powerful.


## Psalms 145:12 (id: 1019145012)

12They will do that so that everyone will know about your powerful deeds and that you rule over us gloriously.


## Psalms 145:13 (id: 1019145013)

13You will never stop being king; you will rule throughout all generations.


## Psalms 145:14 (id: 1019145014)

14Yahweh, you help all those who are discouraged, and you lift up all those who have lost hope.


## Psalms 145:15 (id: 1019145015)

15All of the creatures that you made expect that you will provide food for them, and you give them food when they need it.


## Psalms 145:16 (id: 1019145016)

16You give food to all living creatures generously, and you cause them to be satisfied.


## Psalms 145:17 (id: 1019145017)

17Everything that Yahweh does, he does justly; all that he does, he does mercifully.


## Psalms 145:18 (id: 1019145018)

18Yahweh comes near to all those who call out to him, to those who call to him sincerely.


## Psalms 145:19 (id: 1019145019)

19To all those who have an awesome respect for him he gives what they need. He hears them when they cry out to him and saves them.


## Psalms 145:20 (id: 1019145020)

20Yahweh protects all those who love him, but he will get rid of all the wicked people.


## Psalms 145:21 (id: 1019145021)

21I will always praise Yahweh; I wish that all people everywhere may praise him forever, for he does everything perfectly.


## Psalms 146:1 (id: 1019146001)

1Praise Yahweh. With my whole inner being I will praise Yahweh.


## Psalms 146:2 (id: 1019146002)

2I will praise Yahweh as long as I am alive; I will sing to praise my God all the rest of my life.


## Psalms 146:3 (id: 1019146003)

3You people, do not trust in your leaders; do not trust humans because they cannot save.


## Psalms 146:4 (id: 1019146004)

4When they die, their corpses decay and become soil again. After they die, they can no longer do the things that they planned to do.


## Psalms 146:5 (id: 1019146005)

5But how fortunate are those whom God helps, the God whom Jacob worshiped. These are the people who confidently expect Yahweh, their God, to help them.


## Psalms 146:6 (id: 1019146006)

6He is the one who created the heavens and the earth, the oceans and all the creatures that are in them. He always does what he has promised to do.


## Psalms 146:7 (id: 1019146007)

7He decides matters fairly for those who are treated unfairly, and he provides food for those who are hungry. He frees those who are in prison.


## Psalms 146:8 (id: 1019146008)

8Yahweh enables those who are blind to see again. He lifts up those who have fallen down. He loves the righteous people.


## Psalms 146:9 (id: 1019146009)

9Yahweh takes care of those from other countries who live in our land, and he helps widows and orphans. But he stops wicked people from what they are doing.


## Psalms 146:10 (id: 1019146010)

10Yahweh will continue to be our king forever; you people of Israel, your God will rule forever! Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 147:1 (id: 1019147001)

1Praise Yahweh! It is good to sing praises to our God. It is a delightful thing to do and the right thing to do.


## Psalms 147:2 (id: 1019147002)

2Jerusalem was destroyed, but Yahweh is enabling us to build Jerusalem again. He is bringing back the people who were taken to other lands.


## Psalms 147:3 (id: 1019147003)

3He enables those who were very discouraged to be encouraged again; it is as though they have wounds and he bandages them.


## Psalms 147:4 (id: 1019147004)

4He has determined how many stars there will be and gives names to all of them.


## Psalms 147:5 (id: 1019147005)

5Yahweh is great and very powerful, and no one can measure how much he understands.


## Psalms 147:6 (id: 1019147006)

6Yahweh lifts up those who have been oppressed, and he throws the wicked down to the ground.


## Psalms 147:7 (id: 1019147007)

7Thank Yahweh while you are singing to him to praise him; on the harps, play music to our God.


## Psalms 147:8 (id: 1019147008)

8He covers the sky with clouds, and then he sends rain to the earth and causes grass to grow on the hills.


## Psalms 147:9 (id: 1019147009)

9He gives to animals the food that they need; he gives food to young crows when they cry out because they are hungry.


## Psalms 147:10 (id: 1019147010)

10He is not impressed with strong horses or with men who can run fast.


## Psalms 147:11 (id: 1019147011)

11Instead, what pleases him are those who have an awesome respect for him, those who confidently expect him to continue to love them as he promised to do.


## Psalms 147:12 (id: 1019147012)

12You people of Jerusalem, praise Yahweh! Praise your God!


## Psalms 147:13 (id: 1019147013)

13He guards your city by keeping its gates strong. He blesses the people who live there.


## Psalms 147:14 (id: 1019147014)

14He causes your people to become wealthy. He gives you plenty of very good wheat to eat.


## Psalms 147:15 (id: 1019147015)

15He commands things to happen throughout the earth; his words quickly reach the place to which he sends them.


## Psalms 147:16 (id: 1019147016)

16He sends snow to cover the ground like a white wool blanket, and he scatters frost on the ground as wind scatters ashes.


## Psalms 147:17 (id: 1019147017)

17He sends hail down like pebbles; when that happens, it is very difficult to endure because the air becomes very cold.


## Psalms 147:18 (id: 1019147018)

18But he commands the wind to blow, and it blows. Then the hail melts and the water flows into the streams.


## Psalms 147:19 (id: 1019147019)

19He sends his message to the descendants of Jacob; he tells to his Israelite people the things that he has decreed and what he has decided.


## Psalms 147:20 (id: 1019147020)

20He has not done that for any other nation; the other nations do not know his laws. Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 148:1 (id: 1019148001)

1Praise Yahweh! Praise him, you angels who are in the heavens; praise him, you angels up in the sky!


## Psalms 148:2 (id: 1019148002)

2All you angels who belong to him, praise him! All you who are in the armies of Yahweh, praise him!


## Psalms 148:3 (id: 1019148003)

3Sun and moon, you also must praise him! You shining stars, you praise him!


## Psalms 148:4 (id: 1019148004)

4You highest heavens, praise him! You waters that are high above the sky, praise him!


## Psalms 148:5 (id: 1019148005)

5I want all of these to praise Yahweh because by commanding that they exist, he created them.


## Psalms 148:6 (id: 1019148006)

6He set them in place; he commanded that they should be there forever. They cannot disobey that command!


## Psalms 148:7 (id: 1019148007)

7Everything on the earth, praise Yahweh! You huge creatures and everything else that is deep in the ocean,


## Psalms 148:8 (id: 1019148008)

8fire and hail, snow and frost, and strong winds that obey what he commands, I tell all of you to praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 148:9 (id: 1019148009)

9Hills and mountains, fruit trees and cedar trees,


## Psalms 148:10 (id: 1019148010)

10all the wild animals and all tame animals, reptiles and other things that creep on the ground, and all the birds, I tell all of you to praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 148:11 (id: 1019148011)

11You kings on this earth and all the people that you rule, you princes and all other rulers,


## Psalms 148:12 (id: 1019148012)

12you young men and young women, you old people and children, everyone, praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 148:13 (id: 1019148013)

13I want them all to praise Yahweh because he is greater than anyone else. His power controls everything on the earth and in the heavens.


## Psalms 148:14 (id: 1019148014)

14He caused us, his people, to be strong so that we Israelite people who are very precious to him should praise him, So praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 149:1 (id: 1019149001)

1Praise Yahweh! Sing a new song to Yahweh; praise him whenever his faithful people gather together!


## Psalms 149:2 (id: 1019149002)

2You Israelite people, be glad because of what God, who created you, has done for you! You people of Jerusalem, rejoice because of what God, your king, has done for you!


## Psalms 149:3 (id: 1019149003)

3Praise Yahweh by dancing, by beating tambourines, and by playing harps to praise him!


## Psalms 149:4 (id: 1019149004)

4Yahweh is pleased with his people; he honors humble people by helping them to defeat their enemies.


## Psalms 149:5 (id: 1019149005)

5Because they have won battles, God’s people should rejoice and sing joyfully all during the night!


## Psalms 149:6 (id: 1019149006)

6They should shout loudly to praise God; but they should also hold sharp swords in their hands,


## Psalms 149:7 (id: 1019149007)

7ready to use them to defeat the soldiers of nations that do not worship God and to punish the people of those nations.


## Psalms 149:8 (id: 1019149008)

8They will fasten their kings and other leaders with iron chains.


## Psalms 149:9 (id: 1019149009)

9They will judge and punish the people of those nations as God wrote should be done. Everyone else will honor God’s faithful people for doing that! Praise Yahweh!


## Psalms 150:1 (id: 1019150001)

1Praise Yahweh! Praise God in his temple! Praise him who is in his fortress in heaven!


## Psalms 150:2 (id: 1019150002)

2Praise him for the mighty deeds that he has performed; praise him because he is very great!


## Psalms 150:3 (id: 1019150003)

3Praise him by blowing trumpets loudly; praise him by playing harps and small stringed instruments!


## Psalms 150:4 (id: 1019150004)

4Praise him by beating drums and by dancing. Praise him by playing stringed instruments and by playing flutes!


## Psalms 150:5 (id: 1019150005)

5Praise him by clashing cymbals; praise him by clashing very loud cymbals!


## Psalms 150:6 (id: 1019150006)

6I want all living creatures to praise Yahweh! Praise Yahweh!
